NA_0.0–0.1^1	aviyuta sāmānya viśeṣa deśinam vardhamānam ānamya nyāya avatāra vivṛtiḥ smṛti bīja vivṛddhaye kriyate asya ca idam ādi vākyam pramāṇa vyutpādana artham idam ārabhyate pramāṇa ityādi anena ca tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa saṃbandha vikala tayā dhvaneḥ bahis artham prati prāmāṇya ayogāt abhidheya ādi sūcana dvara utpanna artha saṃśaya mukhena śrotāraḥ śravaṇam prati protsāhyante iti dharma uttaraḥ manyate tat ayuktam yadi hi śabdasya artha prakāśanam prati sāmarthyam na samasti tat katham asau abhidheya ādi sūcane api paṭiṣṭhaḥ syāt na ca tasya aprāmāṇyaḥ etad śravaṇāt artha saṃśayam kurvanti prekṣāvantaḥ tadvat tā hāneḥ mithyājñānāt api pravṛtti avirāma prasaṅgāt ca arcaṭaḥ tu āha na śrāvaka utsāhakam etat prāmāṇya abhāvāt teṣām ca apramāṇāt apravṛtteḥ anyathā prekṣāvat ta akṣateḥ kim tarhi prakaraṇa artha kathana avasara upasthita para upanyasta hetu asiddha tā udbhāvanā artham 
NA_0.1^2	 tathā hi sambhavati evaṃvādī na ārabdhavyam idam abhidheya ādi śūnya tvāt kāka danta parīkṣā ādi vat iti tat anena asya tadvat tā prakāśakena vacasā tad hetūnām asiddha tā udbhāvyate iti tat ayuktataram yatas yadi idam apramāṇam iti na abhidheya ādīni sākṣāt lakṣayat pravartayati tatas para upanyasta hetu asiddha tām kathayati iti yukti riktam paśyāmaḥ apramāṇasya akiñcitkara tvāt anyathā pramāṇa vicāraṇam ānarthakyam aśnuvīta tasmāt idam pramāṇa bhūtam sat abhidheya ādīni pratipādayat prekṣāvataḥ pravartayati iti prakaraṇa ādau upanyastam 
NA_0.2^1	 sambandha śūnya tvāt asya katham arthe pramāṇa tā iti ced pratyakṣe api katham tarhi sā iti vācyam grāhya grāhaka bhāva sambandha balāt iti ced atra api vācya vācaka bhāvāt iti brūmaḥ saḥ eva katham iti ced adhyakṣe api vedya vedaka bhāvaḥ katham iti vācyam tad utpatti tad ākāra tābhyām iti ced kā iyam tat utpattiḥ nāma tat janyatā iti ced pratikṣaṇa bhaṅgura tve sāiva durupapāda iti ācakṣmahe tathā hi kṣaṇa naśvaraḥ arthaḥ su akṣaṇe pūrvam paścāt vā kāryam kuryāt iti trayī gatiḥ 
NA_0.2^2	 tatra na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ kakṣīkaraṇīyaḥ sama kāla bhāvini vyāpāra abhāvāt itarathāi kakṣaṇa vartinām samasta artha kṣaṇānām itaretaram kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prasajyeta tathā ca tad prayuktaḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ ca iti asamañjasam āpanīpadyeta atha su akṣaṇāt pūrvam acāru etat api svayam asataḥ bhaviṣyat śaṅkha cakravarti ādeḥ iva pūrva kāla vartini kārye vyāpāra abhāvāt atha su akṣaṇāt ūrdhvam kāryam vidhattaḥ iti manyethāḥ etat api asādhīyaḥ vinaṣṭasya kārya karaṇa akṣama tvāt anyathā mṛtasya śikhinaḥ kekāyitam syāt tat ākāra tā api kim artha ākāra saṅkrāntyā atha tad sadṛśatayā utpatteḥ jñānasya iti 
NA_0.2^3	 yadi ādyaḥ kalpaḥ tat ayuktam jñāne sva ākāra arpaṇāt arthasya nirākāra tā anuṣaṅgāt sva deha pṛthutara artha adarśana prasaṅgāt śiraḥ sphoṭana plāvana ādi anartha prasakteḥ ca uta dvitīyaḥ tathā sati sādṛśya vaśāt artha vyavasthā iti āyātam na ca sādṛśyam bhavatām darśane tāttvikam asti vivikta kṣaṇa kṣayi paramāṇu lakṣaṇa sva lakṣaṇānām pāramārthika tva abhyupagamāt anādi kāla ālīna vāsanā prabodha sampādita sattāka nirvikalpaka vi vikta darśana uttara kāla bhāvi vikalpa vyavasthāpita sādṛśya vaśāt artha grahaṇa niyame sati eka nīla sva lakṣaṇe kṣaṇe sakala kāla kalāpa vyāpi kāka kuvalaya ādi gata nīla tāyāḥ vyavasthitiḥ aviśeṣeṇa anuṣajeta tathā ca pratiniyataḥ grāhya grāhaka bhāvaḥ na ghaṭām aṭāṭyeta 
NA_0.2^4	 aṅgulī agra nirdiśyamāna puras varti nīla sva lakṣaṇa darśana bala āyāta tvāt nailya vikalpasya tat eva adhyavasyati na bhūtam bhāvi kāka kuvalayādi gatam vā iti ced tarhi vikalpaḥ sva lakṣaṇa niṣṭhaḥ prāptaḥ niyata deśa daśā avacchinna artha kriyā samartha artha grahaṇāt tathā hi tad adhyavasāyaḥ kim tad vikalpanam uta tad grahaṇam na tāvat tad vikalpanam vikalpānām bhavat abhiprāyeṇa sva lakṣaṇa antar praveśa abhāvāt tat uktam tena anya apoha viṣayāḥ proktāḥ sāmānya gocarāḥ śabdāḥ ca buddhayaḥ ca aiva vastuni eṣām asambhavāt iti 
NA_0.3^1	 atha brūyāt yadi api vikalpāḥ sāmānyam gocarayanti tattvataḥ tathā api pratyakṣa vikalpayoḥ yaugapadyena pravṛtteḥ vimūḍhaḥ pratipattā vikalpasya sva lakṣaṇa niṣṭhatām vyavasyati tathā ca uktam manasoḥ yugapad vṛtteḥ sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ vimūḍhaḥ laghu vṛtteḥ vā tayoḥ aikyam vyavasyati tat kim idam śapathaiḥ pratyeyam yat uta mohāt vikalpena sva lakṣaṇam adhyavasyati na punar viśada nirbhāsena sākṣātkaroti evam ca adhyakṣam api sakala artha vyaktīḥ gocarayati vikalpa mohāt tu sannihita viṣayam lakṣyate iti paraḥ anuṣañjayan durnivāraḥ syāt uta tad grahaṇam adhyavasāyaḥ tadā sva lakṣaṇa niṣṭhatā vikalpasya sva vācā bhavadbhiḥ pratipannā syāt 
NA_0.3^2	 evam ca vikalpa yugalake api artha kriyā samartha artha paryavasita sattāka tā vikalpasya āḍhaukate yadā ca vikalpaḥ sva lakṣaṇa saudha madhyam adhyāste iti abhidadhyāḥ tathā sati dhvaneḥ api tad antar praveśaḥ durnivāraḥ syāt tad sahacara tvāt yat āha bhavat ācāryaḥ saḥ eva śabdānām viṣayaḥ yaḥ vikalpānām iti na ca vikalpam vyatiricya sādṛśya vyavasthāpakam anyat asti pratyakṣasya sakala jagat vilakṣaṇa sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa pravaṇa tvāt tat yadi tad sadṛśa tayā utpattiḥ tad ākāra tā tadā pratipādita nyāyāt vikalpasya sannihita artha gocara torarīkartavyā tathā ca dhvaniḥ api tad viṣayaḥ sidhyati iti siddham naḥ samīhitam anyathā tad ākāra tā na samasti gati antara abhāvāt tat na tat utpatti tat ākārate grāhya grāhaka bhāva hetū saṃstaḥ 
NA_0.4^1	 saṃstām vā tathā api vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ bhavān kim ete grahaṇa kāraṇam pārthakyena uta sāmastyena tat yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ kapā lakṣaṇaḥ ghaṭa antyakṣaṇasya grāhakaḥ prāpnoti tad janya tvāt jala candraḥ vā nabhaḥ candrasya grāhakaḥ syāt tad ākāra tvāt atha dvitīyaḥ tathā sati ghaṭottarakṣaṇaḥ pūrvakṣaṇasya grāhakaḥ prasajati tad utpatteḥ tad ākāra tvāt ca jaḍa tvāt arthasya na grāhaka tvam api tu jñānasya tad utpatti tad ākāra tayoḥ satyoḥ iti ced idam idānīm viditam asmābhiḥ etat api samāna artha grāhi prācīna saṃveda nakṣaṇa lakṣaṇa manaskāra utpādya jñāne grāhaka lakṣaṇam vyabhicarati utpādaka prākta na kṣaṇa varti manaskāra āgrāhaka tvāt tad adhyavasāya sāhityena tad utpatti tad ākāra tayoḥ grahaṇa kāraṇa tvam sampūrṇam manaskāre tat na asti iti ced kim idam bhinna gocareṇa saha sāhityam 
NA_0.4^2	 tathā hi adhyavasāyaḥ vāsanā prabodha vaśāt utpannaḥ sāmānyam anartha rūpam vikalpayati pratyakṣam bahis arthāt labdha ātma lābham tat ākāram tam eva sākṣātkaroti iti bhavatām darśanam tat na vikalpa sāhityam pratyakṣasya kañcana viśeṣam puṣṇāti tat idam grāhya grāhaka bhāva kāraṇam pratyakṣe api yat bhavadbhiḥ abhyadhāyi tat yathā yathā vicāryate tathā tathā viśīryate iti anapekṣaṇīyam tat yathā kathañcid pratyakṣasya pratipādita grāhya grāhaka bhāva lakṣaṇa vaikalye api grāhaka tvam arthasya grāhya tvam tathā dṛṣṭa tvāt anyathā nikhila vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt bhavadbhiḥ api pratyapādi tathā śabdasya vācaka tvam arthasya vācya tvam pratipadyadhvam yūyam atra api dṛṣṭa hāneḥ vyavahāra ucchedasya samāna tvāt 
NA_0.4^3	 atha ittham ācakṣīthāḥ yathā nadyāḥ tīre guḍa śakaṭam paryastam dhāvata dhāva ta ḍimbhakāḥ ityādi vipra tāraka puruṣa vacana śravaṇāt pravartamānāḥ vipralambha bhājaḥ jāyante atas sakala vacaneṣu anāśvāsaḥ iti evam tarhi cikicikāyamāna maru marīcikā cakra cumbi yat jala ullekhi viśada darśanam udaya padavīm samāsādayati tat alīkam avalokitam iti sakala adhyakṣeṣu anāśvāsaḥ iti abhidadhmahe pāścātya viparīta artha upasthāpaka pramāṇa bādhita tvāt maru marīcikāsu jala jñānam apramāṇam na śeṣa satya stambha ādi jñānāni bādhā rahita tvāt iti ced tarhi dhvanau api ayam nyāyaḥ kim kākaiḥ bhakṣitaḥ na hi vayam sarva śabdānām prāmāṇyam pratipadyemahi kim tarhi su niścita āpta praṇetṛkāṇām eva tat na prāmāṇyam prati pratyakṣa śabdayoḥ viśeṣam upalabhāmahe 
NA_0.4^4	 eṣa tu viśeṣaḥ syāt pratyakṣam cakṣuḥ ādi sāmagrīvi śeṣa janya tvāt sannihita niyata artha grāhi spaṣṭa pratibhāsam śābdam tu tathāvidha kāraṇa vikala tvāt niyata aniyata artha grāhī aspaṣṭa pratibhāsam na ca āiṣa viśeṣaḥ prāmāṇya kṣati kārī itaratha anumānasya api aprāmāṇyam āsajyeta tasya api aviśadāniyata artha grāhi tvāt paramārthataḥ tu tri kāla vyāpinaḥ sarva artha grahaṇa svabhāva tve api āvaraṇa tiraskṛtasya jīva dravyasya cakṣuḥ ādi sāma grīsa apekṣa āvaraṇa kṣaya upaśama vaśāt sannihita spaṣṭa artha grahaṇa pariṇāmaḥ pratyakṣam iti ucyate śabda sāpekṣa kṣaya upaśamāt niyata aniyatā viśada artha grahaṇa pariṇāmaḥ tu śābdam iti tat na tat utpatti tat ākārate pratyakṣe śābde anyasmin vā jñāne vāstavyau staḥ tasmāt pāramārthika abhidheya prayojana sambandha pratipādakam etat ādi vākyam iti sthitam 
NA_0.5^1	 tatra abhidheyam vācyam tat ca iha pramāṇam tasya aiva prakaraṇena pratipādya tvāt tat pramāṇa iti avayavena lakṣayati prayojanam dvedhā śrotuḥ kartuḥ ca punar api dvividham anantaram vyavahitam ca tatra śrotuḥ anantara prayojanam pramāṇa viṣayā vyutpattiḥ kartuḥ vyutpadyamānasya prājña tvāt śiṣyasya vyutpādanam tatra ātma prayojanam darśayan āhārabhyate iti asya mayā iti pada savyapekṣa tvāt śiṣya prayojanam tu vyutpaditi anena upasarga dhātu samudāyena aiva tad antara gatam lapsyate iti abhiprāyavān kartā ātma vyāpāram ṇijantena nirdiśati pramāṇa vyutpādana artham iti 
NA_0.5^2	 vyavahita prayojanam dvedhā vyāvahārikam pāramārthikam ca vyāvahārikam heya upādeya upekṣaṇīyeṣu artheṣu hāna upādāna upekṣā lakṣaṇam pāramārthikam abhyudaya niḥśreyasa avāptiḥ iti etat tu sākṣāt anuktam api anantara prayojana phala tvāt tad vacanena aiva ākṣiptam avagantavyam sambandhaḥ tu upāya upeya lakṣaṇaḥ tatra upeyam prakaraṇa artha parijñānam prakaraṇam upāyaḥ tatas tad abhilaṣa tā prakaraṇam idam ārambhaṇīyam iti anuktaḥ api vacanena sambandhaḥ arthāt gamyate iti tātparya arthaḥ 
NA_0.6^1	 adhunā akṣara arthaḥ vivriyate tatra yadi api pramāṇa śabdasya sarva kārakaiḥ bhāvena ca vyutpatteḥ sukara tvāt kṛtyalyuṭaḥ bahulam anyatra api iti vacanāt yathākramam amī kartṛ artha ādi kāraka bhāva vyutpattyā pramāṇa śabda vācyāḥ tat yathā ātma artha jñāna artha kriyā kāraṇa kalāpa kṣaya upaśama kriyā rūpāḥ tathā api iha jñānam eva adhikriyate tasya aiva parīkṣā kṣama tvāt itareṣām parīkṣāyāḥ tad puraḥsara tvāt vaiyarthāt ca tathā hi na arthaḥ tāvat ātmanaḥ parīkṣayā tasya bhrānta abhra anta jñāneṣu samāna tvāt na api arthasya tasya upeya tvāt upāya bhūta jñāna parīkṣaṇena aiva gata tvāt na artha kriyāyāḥ tad avagatau parīkṣā vaiyarthyāt na api kāraṇa kalāpasya jñāna utpatteḥ prāk svarūpa anavagateḥ paścāt tad svarūpa nirṇayāt eva tad sādguṇya vaiguṇya avagateḥ nairarthakyāt na api kṣaya upaśamasya tasya jñāna utpāda unnīya māna rūpa tvāt 
NA_0.6^2	 na api pramiti mātrasya tasya pramāṇa sādhya tayā tad cāru tā dvāreṇa aiva samīcī natā siddheḥ iti tat ayam abhiprāyaḥ yadi api ananta dharma adhyāsite vastuni sarve eva śabda arthāḥ nirupacaritāḥ ghaṭante tathā api yena artham paricchidya artha kriyā samartha artha prārthanayā pravartante pramātāraḥ tat eva iha jñānam ātmanā saha dharmi rūpa tayā tādātmye api dharma rūpa tayā vyatiriktam pramīyate anena iti pramāṇam iti ucyate tasya vyutpādanam para parikalpita lakṣaṇa ādi vyudāsena sva abhipreta lakṣaṇa ādi svarūpa prakāśanam tad artham artha śabdaḥ prayojana paryāyaḥ idam iti artha rūpa tayā sva cetasi vivartamānam prakaraṇa śarīram parāmṛśati dvividham hi prakaraṇa śarīram śabdaḥ arthaḥ ca iti bahis śabda rūpa tayā prakāśayiṣyamāṇa tve api antar tattva artha ākāreṇa pratyakṣa tvāt ārabhyate iti pada vākya śloka ādi racanayā prakriyate iti yāvat 
NA_0.7	 iha ca lakṣaṇa saṃkhyā gocara phaleṣu pramāṇam prati vipratipadyante pare tathā hi lakṣaṇe tāvat pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam iti saugatāḥ anadhigata artha adhigantṛ pramāṇam iti mīmāṃsakāḥ artha upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam iti naiyāyika ādayaḥ tathā saṃkhyāyām pratyakṣa anumāne dve eva pramāṇe iti saugatāḥ pratyakṣa anumāna śabda upamāna artha apatti abhāvāḥ pramāṇāni iti mīmāṃsakāḥ pratyakṣa anumāna śabda upamānāni pramāṇāni iti naiyāyikāḥ pratyakṣa anumāna śabdāni pramāṇāni iti vaiśeṣikāḥ etāni eva sāṃkhyāḥ pratyakṣam eva aikam pramāṇam iti cārvākāḥ tathā gocare paraspara vinirluṭhi ta kṣaṇa kṣayi parama anulakṣaṇāni sva lakṣaṇāni pramāṇa gocaraḥ tāttvikaḥ iti bauddhāḥ sāmānya viśeṣa ātmakam vastu iti mīmāṃsakāḥ paraspara vibhaktau sāmānya viśeṣau iti naiyāyika vaiśeṣikāḥ traiguṇya rūpam sāmānyam iti sāṃkhyāḥ bhūta caṭuṣṭayam pramāṇa bhūmi iti cārvākāḥ tathā phale api vipratipadyante artha adhigatiḥ pramāṇa phalam iti saugatāḥ pūrvam pūrvam pramāṇam uttaram uttaram tu phalam iti mīmāṃsaka ādayaḥ 
NA_1.0–1.1^1	 tatra tāvat lakṣaṇa saṃkhyā vipratipattī nirācikīrṣuḥ āha pramāṇam sva para ābhāsi jñānam bādha vivarjitam pratyakṣam ca parokṣam ca dvidhā meya viniścayāt tatra api pūrva ardhena lakṣaṇa vipratipattim uttara ardhena tu saṃkhyā vipratipattim nirācaṣṭe lakṣaṇam ca para rūpebhyaḥ vyāvartana kṣamaḥ asādhāraṇa dharmaḥ lakṣyate paricchidyate vijātīyebhyaḥ vyāvṛttam lakṣyam yena tat lakṣaṇam iti ucyate tat ca iha dvaye pratyāyyāḥ sva darśana anurakta antaḥkaraṇāḥ tīrtha antarīyāḥ vipratipannāḥ tathā mugdha buddhayaḥ laukikāḥ avyutpannāḥ ca iti 
NA_1.0–1.1^2	 tatas ca yat ādau vipratipannān prati lakṣaṇam tadā aivam lakṣya lakṣaṇa bhāvaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yat idam bhavatām asmākam ca pramāṇam iti prasiddham tat sva para ābhāsi jñānam bādha vivarjitam mantavyam prasiddham pramāṇam anūdya aprasiddham sva para ābha asi tva ādi vidhīyate yadā tu avyutpannam atīn prati idam lakṣaṇam tadā pratiprāṇi sva para prakāśinaḥ jñānasya bādha rahitasya kasyacid siddha tvāt anyathā pratiniyata vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt evam te bodhyante yat adaḥ bhavatām kvacid niyata artha grāhi sva para prakāśakam bādha rahitam jñānam prasiddham tat pramāṇam iti budhyantām atra api siddhasya anuvādaḥ asiddhasya vidhānam yojyam 
NA_1.2	 adhunā akṣara arthaḥ tatra pramāṇam iti pūrvavat sve ātmā svarūpam paraḥ arthaḥ tau ābhāsayitum prakāśayitum śīlam yasya tat tathā jñāyate nirṇīyate tattvam yena tat jñānam bādhyate anena iti bādhaḥ viparīta artha upasthāpaka pramāṇa pravṛttiḥ iti yāvat tena viśeṣeṇa varjitam rahitam yat jñānam tat pramāṇam iti saṇṭaṅkaḥ 
NA_1.3^1	 iha ca vyavacchedya apekṣayā lakṣaṇe viśeṣaṇa pravṛtteḥ sva parābhāsi iti anena ye svābhāsi eva jñānam manyante jñāna vādinaḥ bauddha viśeṣāḥ ye ca para ābhāsi eva mīmāṃsaka naiyāyika ādayaḥ te nirastāḥ te hi bahis artha abhāvāt jñānam sva aṃśa paryavasita sattākam iti ācakṣīran tat ayuktam jñeya artha abhāve jñāna abhāva prasaṅgāt atha artha abhāve api svapna daśāyām vana deva kula ādi nānā pratibhāsam jñānam avalokitam iti tathābhūtam sakalam brūṣe tat na tasya api jāgrat avasthā bhāvi sadbhūta artha darśana sampādita ātma saṃskāra middha ādi kāraṇa kalāpa sannidhāna prabodha savyapekṣa tvāt itaratha atyantān anubhūta bhūta pañcaka atirikta ṣaṣṭha bhūta pratibhāsaḥ syāt 
NA_1.3^2	 kim ca katham ekam jñānam sita pīta ādi aneka ākāra vivartam iti praṣṭavyaḥ bhavān anādya vidyau= āsanāt iti ced atra api vikalpa yugalam amalam avatarati tatas jñānāt sā vāsanā vyabhaitsīt vā na vā vyatyaraikṣīt ced evam sati tad grāhaka pramāṇam abhidhānīyam jñāna vyatiriktāyāḥ saṃvedana abhāvāt tad saṃvedane ca arthasya api vyatiriktasya saṃvedanam iti sa duṣpratiṣedhaḥ syāt vedya vedaka ākāra kaluṣitāt jñānāt eva vyatiriktā tad kāraṇa bhūtāḥ jñāna rūpāiva sā anumīyate iti ced na tayā saha sambandha grahaṇa abhāvāt dṛṣṭa hānyadṛṣṭa parikalpanā prasaṅgāt ca 
NA_1.3^3	 kim ca yathā vyatirikta vāsanā vaśāt ekam api jñānam nānā ākāram tathā jaḍam api tad vaśāt eva bodha rūpam prakāśate iti viparīta āpatteḥ arthaḥ eva siddhim āskandet na jñānam atha avyatiriktā hanta jñānam eva tat na vāsanā tad avyatirikta tvāt tad svarūpavat iti āstām tāvat para ābhāsi api sva prakāśa abhāvāt abhidadhīran tat api asambaddham sva prakāśa abhāve para prakāśa ayogāt na hi pradīpaḥ sva rūpam anuddyotayan ghaṭa ādi uddyotane vyāpriyate svayam ca apratītam api yadi artham grāhayati jñānam devadattasya utpannam yajñadattam grāhayet viśeṣa abhāvāt 
NA_1.3^4	 anyat ca para prakāśana mātre dūra āsanna ādi bhedaḥ prathamānānām arthānām kim apekṣaḥ cakāsti śarīra apekṣaḥ iti ced na tasya api prakāśyatā viśeṣāt tasmāt antar mukha ākārasya bahis artha grahaṇe sati ayam ghaṭām āṭīkate na anyathā atha arthāpatti ādinā pramāṇa antareṇa tat antar niviṣṭam gṛhyate tatas tad apekṣayā yokṣyate dūra āsanna ādi bhedaḥ iti ced na tatra api vikalpa yugalaka anativṛtteḥ tathā hi tat pramāṇa antaram sva prakāśam anya prakāśam vā sva prakāśam ced prathamasya kim kṣūṇam ! anya prakāśam ced tatra api iyam eva vārtā iti anavasthā tasmāt sva rūpam avabhāsayat eva jñānam artha grahaṇāya vyāpriyate iti sthitam 
NA_1.4	 jñānam iti anena tu yat naiyāyika ādibhiḥ paryakalpi sannikarṣaḥ pramāṇam iti tasya prāmāṇyam nirasyati yatas snāna pāna avagāhana ādi artha kriyā nirvartana kṣamam artham niścitya avyavadhānena pravartante pramātāraḥ tat eva jñānam pramāṇam na sannikarṣaḥ jaḍa tayā asti avyavahita nirṇaya abhāvāt iti ākūtam artha upalabdhi hetu tvāt tasya prāmāṇyam iti ced viśīrṇa idānīm pramāṇeyattā deha ādeḥ api tad kāraṇa tayā prāmāṇya āpatteḥ iti āstām tāvat 
NA_1.5	 bādha vivarjitam iti amunā tu yat timira ādi tiraskṛta nayana dīdhiti prasara ādīnām nabhastala avalambi niśīthinī nātha dvaya ādi pratibhāsam yat ca kutarka bhrānta cetasām nija nija darśana ākarṇana prabhavam kṣaṇa kṣayi sāmānya viśeṣāi kānta īśvara ādi kṛta bhuvana pratibhāsam jñānam tad pratyanīka artha pratyāyaka pramāṇa antara upanipāta plāvita tvāt pratikṣipati viśeṣa artha viśabda upādānāt tu yaḥ khalu bahula kāmalā avalepa lupta locana balānām dhavale jalaje pītimānam ādadhānaḥ bodhaḥ samullasati sa yadi api sakala kālam tad doṣa avyuparame pramātuḥ nija darśanena na bādhyate tathā api tad jalaja dhavalatā grāhinā jana antara darśanena bādhita tvāt na pramāṇam iti uktam bhavati 
NA_1.6^1	 samasta lakṣaṇena tu yat pare pratyapīpadan anadhigata artha adhigantṛ pramāṇam avisaṃvādakam pramāṇam artha upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam ityādi tat nirāsthat tathā hi anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tvam kim abhidhīyate jñāna antareṇa anadhigatam artham yat adhigacchati tat pramāṇam iti ced tarhi tat jñāna antaram parakīyam svakīyam vā tat yadi parakīyam tat ayuktam sarvajña jñānasya sakala artha gocara tayā sarva prākṛta loka jñānānām adhigata artha adhigantṛ tvena aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tad artha grāhi jana antara darśana sambhavāt ca atha svakīyam tatra api saḥ adhigamyaḥ arthaḥ kim dravyam uta paryāyaḥ yat vā dravya viśiṣṭaḥ paryāyaḥ paryāya viśiṣṭam vā dravyam iti tathā kim sāmānyam uta viśeṣa āhosvit sāmānya viśiṣṭaḥ viśeṣaḥ viśeṣa viśiṣṭam vā sāmānyam iti aṣṭau pakṣāḥ tatra yadi ādyam urarī kuruṣe tat ayuktam dravyasya nitya tvāika tvābhyām anadhigata aṃśa abhāvāt 
NA_1.6^2	 atha dvitīyam tat api acāru paryāyasya prācīna saṃvedana udaya samaya dhvastasya saṃvedana antara prabhava kālam yāvat pratīkṣaṇā sambhavena viśeṣaṇa ānarthakyāt uta tṛtīyam tat api asādhīyaḥ vikalpa dvaya anatikramāt sa hi dravya viśiṣṭaḥ paryāyaḥ sama kāla bhāvinā jñānena anadhigataḥ adhigamyate yat vā kāla antara bhāvinā iti na tāvat sama kāla bhāvinā tad sambhava abhāvena viśeṣaṇa vaiphalyāt na hi sambhavaḥ asti ekasya pramātuḥ eka kālam dravya kroḍī kṛtāika paryāya viṣaya saṃvedana dvaya vṛtteḥ tathā anubhava abhavāt parasparam adhigata artha adhigantṛ tvena aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt ca na api kāla antara bhāvinā gṛhyamāṇa paryāyasya kāla antarānāskandanāt pūrva uttara kṣaṇa truṭita vartamāna kṣaṇa mātra sambaddha tvāt tasya etena paryāya viśiṣṭa dravya pakṣaḥ api prativyūḍhaḥ samāna yogakṣema tvāt atha sāmānyam tat api asambaddham tad ekatayā prathama jñānena sākalya grahaṇāt uttareṣām sāmānya jñānānām adhigata artha gocara tayā prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt atha viśeṣaḥ sa nityaḥ anityaḥ vā iti vaktavyam 
NA_1.6^3	 nityaḥ ced evam sati ādya saṃvedanena aiva tasya sāmastya grahaṇāt uttareṣām tad viṣayāṇām adhigata gocara tvena aprāmāṇya prasaktiḥ anityaḥ ced paryāya dūṣaṇena pratikṣiptiḥ atha sāmānya viśiṣṭaḥ viśeṣaḥ kā asya viśiṣṭa tā kim tādātmyam uta tad sannidhi mātram tādātmyam ced prathama jñānena sāmānya vat tasya api grahaḥāt anyathā tādātmya kṣateḥ tad viṣayāni ajñānānām aprāmāṇyam prasajyeta tat sānnidhya pakṣe tu dvayoḥ api parasparam viśakalita rūpa tvāt pakṣa dvaya uditam dūṣaṇam paścāt lagnam dhāvati viśeṣa viśiṣṭa sāmānya pakṣe punar etat eva viparītam yojyam tat na anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tvam jñānasya kathañcid vicāra bhāra gauravam sahate iti alakṣaṇam iti sthitam avisaṃvādaka tvam adhunā vicāryate tat kim pradarśita artha prāpti āhosvit prāpti yogya artha upadarśaka tvena uta avicalita artha viṣaya tvena bhavān jñānasya prāmāṇyam kathayati 
NA_1.6^4	 yadi prathamaḥ kalpaḥ tat ayuktam jala budbuda ādi mumūrṣu padārtha utpādita saṃvedanasya apramāṇa tā utpatteḥ prāpti kāle tasya dhvasta tvāt atha dvitīyaḥ tat api acāru prāpti ayogya deśa sthita graha nakṣatra ādi gocara jñānasya aprāmāṇya prasakteḥ anucita deśa avasthānena aiva prāpti anarha tvāt teṣām atha tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tatra api avicalita viṣaya tām katham avaiṣi jñāna antareṇa tad viṣaya nirākaraṇa abhāvāt iti ced etat eva asmābhiḥ uditam kim bhavataḥ paruṣam ābhāti na hi sva para prakāśi jñānam bādhā rahitam vimucya anyasya viṣaya anirākaraṇam jñāna antareṇa prekṣāmahe tat tat eva nyāyāt pramāṇam bhavadbhiḥ abhyupagatam iti artha upalabdhi hetuḥ pramāṇam iti etat api na parīkṣām kṣamate śarīra ādeḥ api tad kāraṇa tayā prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt avyavahitam artha upalambha kāraṇam pramāṇam na deha ādikam iti ced evam tarhi jñānam eva sva parāvirbhāvakam nirbādhakam ca pramāṇam na sannikarṣa ādi tad sadbhāve api artha pariccheda abhāvāt tasmāt etat eva cāru pramāṇa lakṣaṇam iti 
NA_1.7	 adhunā tad saṃkhyām āha pratyakṣam ca ityādi tatra siddhānta prasiddha pāramārthika pratyakṣa apekṣayā akṣa śabdaḥ jīva paryāya tayā prasiddhaḥ iha tu vyāvahārika pratyakṣa prastāvāt akṣa dhvaniḥ indriya vacanaḥ gṛhyate tatas ca akṣam pratigatam pratyakṣam yat indriyam āśritya ujjihīte artha sākṣāt kāri jñānam tat pratyakṣam iti arthaḥ etat ca pratyakṣa śabda vyutpatti nimittam na tu pravṛtti nimittam sa hi evam vyutpāditaḥ sākṣāt grāhya grāhakam jñāna viśeṣam lakṣayati tatra aiva rūḍha tvāt yathā gamana kriyāyām vyutpāditaḥ api go śabdaḥ kakudādi mantam piṇḍa viśeṣam gacchantam agacchantam vā gocarayati tatra aiva tasya prasiddha tvāt na gamana kriyā yuktam api puruṣa ādikam viparyayāt iti tatas ca sarva jñānānām yat svarūpa saṃvedanam tat api pratyakṣam iti uktam bhavati tatra api svarūpasya grāhyasya sākṣātkaraṇa sadbhāvāt iti akṣebhyaḥ paratas vartate iti parokṣam akṣa vyāpāra nirapekṣam manaḥ vyāpāreṇa asākṣāt artha paricchedakam yat jñānam tat parokṣam iti bhāvaḥ 
NA_1.8	 caśabdau pratyakṣa parokṣayoḥ tulya kakṣatām lakṣayataḥ tena yat pare prāhuḥ pratyakṣam sakala pramāṇa jyeṣṭham ityādi tat apāstam bhavati dvayoḥ api prāmāṇyam prati aviśeṣāt viśada aviśada pratibhāsa viśeṣasya sataḥ api jyeṣṭha tām prati anaṅga tvāt pratyakṣasya puraḥsara tvāt parokṣasya kaniṣṭhata iti ced na ayam ekāntaḥ sarvatra anyathā anupapanna tā avadhārita ucchvāsa niḥśvāsa ādi jīva liṅga sadbhāva asadbhāvābhyām jīva sākṣātkāri pratyakṣa kṣūṇe api jīvan mṛta pratīti darśanāt anyathā loka vyavahāra abhāva prasaṅgāt kvacid pratyakṣa parigṛhīta sambandha balāt parokṣam pravartate iti pratyakṣasya jyeṣṭha tva kalpane paśya mṛgaḥ dhāvati ityādi śabda balāt kṛkāṭikā moṭana dvāreṇa mṛga viṣayam tathā smaraṇāt saṅketa grahaṇāt vā apūrvā pūrva artha darśana kutūhala ādinā vana deva kula ādi gocaram parokṣa pūrvam pratyakṣam dṛṣṭam iti parokṣasya jyeṣṭhatāsajyeta 
NA_1.9–1.10^1	 dvidhā iti sarvam vākyam sa avadhāraṇam pravartate iti nyāyāt anyathā niyata artha apradarśaka tvena tad uccāraṇa vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt viparīta ākāra nirākaraṇa cāturya ayogena nirākāṅkṣa pravṛtti asiddheḥ dvidhā aiva iti avadhāraṇena para parikalpita viparīta saṃkhyā antaram tiraskurute tasya yukti bādhita tvāt tathā hi pratyakṣam eva aikam pramāṇam iti asat parokṣa abhāve tasya aiva prāmāṇya ayogāt sa hi kāścid pratyakṣa vyaktīḥ artha kriyā samartha artha prāpaka tvena avyabhicāriṇīḥ upalabhya anyāḥ tad viparīta tayā vyabhicāriṇīḥ ca tatas kāla antare punar api tādṛśa itarāṇām pratyakṣa vyaktīnām pramāṇa tā itarate samācakṣīta na ca pūrva apara parāmarśa śūnyam puras varti artha grahaṇa paryavasita sattākam pratyakṣam pūrva apara kāla bhāvinīnām pratyakṣa vyaktīnām sādṛśyam prāmāṇya nibandhanam upalakṣayitum kṣamate 
NA_1.10^2	 na ca ayam sva pratīti gocarāṇām api pratyakṣa vyaktīnām prāmāṇyam param pratipādayitum īśaḥ tasmāt avaśyantayā yathā dṛṣṭa pratyakṣa vyakti sādharmyat vāreṇa adhunātana pratyakṣa vyaktīnām prāmāṇya pratyāyakam para paripādakam ca parokṣa antargatam anumāna rūpam pramāṇa antaram urarīkartavyam para avabodha artham ca pratyakṣam eva aikam pramāṇam na anyat asti iti ullapan unmatta tām ātmanaḥ lakṣayati pratyakṣeṇa para cetaḥ vṛtti sākṣāt karaṇa abhāvāt vyāpāra vyāhāra ceṣṭā viśeṣa darśanāt bodha viśeṣa avagatau parokṣasya prāmāṇyam balāt āpatati iti nyāyāt 
NA_1.10^3	 svarga adṛṣṭa devatā ādi pratiṣedham na pratyakṣeṇa kartum arhati tasya sannihita mātra viṣaya tvāt na ca ayam tad pratiṣedhena khara kharaka cārvāka tām āpnoti pramāṇa antaram ca tad pratiṣedha artham na icchati iti viṣamam etat katham kuryāt iti sa vismayam naḥ cetaḥ kim ca pratyakṣam api katham pramāṇa tām svīkaroti iti vaktavyam gṛhyamāṇa padārtha anvaya vyatireka anukaraṇāt 
NA_1.10^4	 tathā hi tat samagra sāmagrīka padārtha balena unmajjati tata bhāve visphārita īkṣaṇa yugalasya api pramātuḥ na udīyate iti yadi brūṣe parokṣe api tarhi samānam eva āitat tat api bahis artha sāmarthyāt eva ullasati tad sambaddha liṅga śabda dvāreṇa tasya utpatteḥ anyathā parokṣa ābhāsa tā prasaṅgāt tasya ca alīka tve pāramārthika parokṣa prāmāṇī akṣateḥ ayogāt anyathā pratyakṣam api gagana tala avalambi śaśa dhara yugala avalokana caturam alīkam avalokitam iti sakala viśada darśanāni satyatā abhimatāni api alīka tām aśnu vīran tat na pramāṇa bhūtam parokṣam kadācana gṛhyamāṇa padārtha sattām vihāya utpattum utsahate iti pratyakṣa vat pramāṇa koṭim ārohati balāt iti sthitam 
NA_1.11	 tathā yat api paraiḥ ukta dvaya atiriktam pramāṇa saṃkhyā antaram pratyajñāyi tatra api yat paryālocyamānam upamāna artha āpatti vat pramāṇa tām ātmasāt karoti tat anayoḥ eva pratyakṣa parokṣayoḥ antar bhāvanīyam yat punar vicāryamāṇam mīmāṃsaka parikalpita abhāva vat prāmāṇyam eva na askandati na tena bahis bhūtena antarbhūtena vā kiñcid naḥ prayojanam avastu tvāt iti apakarṇanīyam 
NA_1.12	 atha katham upamānasya prāmāṇyam iti brūṣe tat ucyate prathamam hi viśada darśana adhigata gopiṇḍa viśeṣasya yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti vākya ākarṇanāhita ātma saṃskārasya puṃsaḥ aṭavyām paryaṭataḥ gavaya piṇḍa viśeṣa viṣaya vivikta darśana puraḥsaram yat pūrva apara goga vaya piṇḍa gocara darśana vyāpāra sampādita janmakam ayam tena sadṛśaḥ anayoḥ vā sādṛśyam iti sādṛśya viśiṣṭam piṇḍam piṇḍa viśiṣṭam sādṛśyam vā gocarayat saṃvedanam udīyate tat upamānam iti yathā āhuḥ tad vādinaḥ tasmāt yat dṛśyate tat syāt sādṛśyena viśeṣitam prameyam upamānasya sādṛśyam vā tad anvitam iti 
NA_1.13^1	 tatas ca pūrva apara darśanayoḥ puras varti goga vaya piṇḍa grahaṇa paryavasita sattāka tvāt pūrva apara parāmarśa śūnya tvāt viśada nirbhāsitayā śabda ullekha rahita tvāt tad adhikam avyabhicaritam vyavahāra kāri sādṛśyam avasyat upamānam sva para prakāśi tayā nirbādhaka tvāt ca pramāṇam pūrva apara piṇḍa atiriktam aparam sādṛśyam na upalabhyate iti ced kaḥ ayam upalambhaḥ yena na upalabhyate sādṛśyam yadi pratyakṣam tat yadi pratyakṣe sādṛśyam upamāna gocara tvāt na pratibhāti kaḥ asya aparādhaḥ na hi jñāna antare tad gocaraḥ na pratibhāti iti nirgocaram tat iti vaktum śakyam itaratha upamāne api pratyakṣa nirgrāhyā vyaktiḥ na bhāti iti nirgocaram adhyakṣam anuṣajyeta tat yathā sva viṣaye adhyakṣam pramāṇam tathā upamānam api na hi dvayoḥ prathamānayoḥ ekam prati viśeṣa abhāve pakṣapātaḥ kartum yuktaḥ 
NA_1.13^2	 etena pratyabhijñā jñāna smṛti ūha ādīnām avisaṃvādakānām parokṣa viśeṣāṇām prāmāṇyam vyākhyātam avagantavyam samāna nyāya anupāti tvāt tathā hi prathamam artha darśanam ātmani saṃskāram ādhatte tādṛśa darśanāt asau saṃskāraḥ prabudhyate prabuddhaḥ pūrva artha viṣayam saḥ eva ayam tad jātīyaḥ vā iti ullekhena pratyabhijñā jñānam utthāpayati tasya ūrdhva tiraścīna bheda sāmānya dvaya avasthāpaka tvāt asañjāta pūrva artha gocara darśanasya tad udaya abhāvāt tathā saḥ eva saṃskāraḥ tādṛśa artha darśanena ābhoga ādinā vā prabuddhaḥ anubhūta viṣaya asampramoṣa lakṣaṇam smaraṇam upajanayati adṛṣṭa arthasya puṃsaḥ smaraṇa anupapatteḥ iti ūhaḥ api pratyakṣa anumāna asaṃvedya sādhya arthāni atha anupapanna tva lakṣaṇa liṅga sambandha grahaṇa pravaṇaḥ pramāṇa antaram iti kathayiṣyate 
NA_1.14^1	 arthāpattiḥ tu pratyakṣa ādi gocarīkṛta sphoṭa ādi padārthāni atha anupapattyā dahana śakti ādikam pāvaka ādeḥ artha antaram pūrva darśana gocarāt samadhikam avyabhicaritam parikalpayanti iti pramāṇa tām svīkaroti eva tad lakṣaṇa yogāt evam anyat api pratyakṣa gocara ādhikya sampādakam nirākāṅkṣa tayā vyavahāra kāri yat yat saṃvedanam tat tat pramāṇam iti samarthanīyam sva para prakāśi nirbādha tvāt pūrva apara sopāna paddhati darśana uttara kāla bhāvi tat saṃkhyā saṃvedana vat sarveṣām ca āiteṣām parokṣe antarbhāvaḥ anyathā anupapanna artha antara darśana dvāreṇa prastuta artha saṃvedana catura tvāt iti kiñcid viśeṣāt tu pramāṇa antara parikalpane pramāṇeyattā viśīryet a ānantyaprāpteḥ āvaraṇa kṣaya upaśama vicitra tayā jñāna pravṛtteḥ vicitra tvāt iti 
NA_1.14^2	 nanu ca aivam sati yat parokṣasya dvaividhyam vakṣyamāṇam anumāna śābda bhedena tat api katham upapatsyate tatra api hi āpta praṇīta vacana prabhava jñānasya arthānyatha anupapanna tvena anumāna antarbhāvaḥ na durupapādaḥ tatas ca anumānam eva aikam avaśiṣyate tat eva parokṣa śabdena yadi ucyate yuktam āste viduṣām abhidhānam prati anādarāt satyam etat evam tu manyate yadi api kayācid prakriyayā anumāne śābdam antar bhāvayitum śakyam tathā api tat prati vipratipadyante pare atas tasya āhatya prāmāṇyam samarthanīyam na ca apṛthak bhūtasya tat viviktam vaktum śakyam iti atas pārthakyena upanyāsaḥ anena ca aitat upalakṣayati anyeṣām api parokṣa viśeṣāṇām anumāna antarbhāva sambhave api yam yam prati pareṣām vipratipattiḥ tam tam parokṣāt niṣkṛṣya vivikta yukti upanyāsena tasya tasya prāmāṇyam āvedanīyam tathā ca śāstra antare yat ūhā ādīnām lakṣaṇam akārī ācāryaiḥ tat yuktam eva iti uktam bhavati 
NA_1.15	 katham tarhi mīmāṃsaka parikalpitaḥ abhāvaḥ na pramāṇam nirgocara tvāt iti brūmaḥ tathā hi pratyakṣam eva anvaya vyatireka dvārena bhū talam eva idam ghaṭa ādiḥ na asti iti vastu pariccheda prāvīṇyam ābibhrāṇam tad adhika grāhya artha abhāvāt pramāṇa antaram parikalpyamānam nirasyati iti kim naḥ cintayā tasya sat asat rūpa vastu grāhiṇaḥ pratiprāṇi prasiddha tvāt atha kadācid abhidadhyāt adhyakṣam bhāva aṃśam eva akalaya ti indriya dvāreṇa utpatteḥ tasya ca bhāva aṃśaḥ eva vyāpārān na astita ajñānam tu vastu grahaṇa uttara kālam pratiyogi smaraṇa sadbhāve mānasam akṣa vyāpāra nirapekṣam unmajjati tat uktam na tāvat indriyeṇa āiṣā na asti iti utpādyate matiḥ bhāva aṃśena aiva saṃyogaḥ yogya tvāt indriyasya hi gṛḥītvā avastu sadbhāvam smṛtvā ca pratiyoginam mānasam na astita ajñānam jāyate akṣa an apekṣayā 
NA_1.16	 atra ucyate bhāva aṃśāt abhāva aṃśaḥ tarhi abhinnaḥ bhinnaḥ vā abhinnaḥ ced katham agrahaṇam bhāva aṃśāt avyatirikta tvāt eva tad svarūpa vat bhinnaḥ ced ghaṭa ādi abhāva vinirluṭhitam bhū talam ādya darśanena gṛhyate iti ghaṭa ādayaḥ gṛhyante iti prāptam tad abhāva agrahaṇasya tad bhāva grahaṇana āntarīyaka tvāt tathā ca abhāvaḥ api paścāt pravartamānaḥ tān utsārayitum apaṭiṣṭhaḥ syāt anyathā pratyakṣam asaṅkīrṇasya saṅkīrṇa tā grahaṇāt bhrāntam āpanīpadyeta kim ca pramāṇa abhāvāt artha abhāvaḥ abhāva pramāṇena sādhyate iti bhavataḥ abhiprāyaḥ pramāṇa pañcakam yatra vastu rūpe na jāyate vastu sattā avabodha artham tatra abhāva pramāṇa tā 
NA_1.17	 iti vacanāt tat ayuktam yatas pramāṇa abhāvaḥ katham grāhyaḥ tad grāhaka pramāṇa antara abhāvāt iti ced tasya api abhāva grahaṇe tad grāhaka pramāṇa antara abhāvaḥ grāhyaḥ iti anavasthā atha artha abhāvāt pramāṇasya pramāṇa abhāvāt ca arthasya abhāvaḥ pratipadyeta iti manyethāḥ tat etat itaretara āśrayam durghaṭam āpadyeta na yāvat artha abhāvaḥ agṛhītaḥ tāvat pramāṇa abhāvaḥ sidhyati artha abhāvaḥ ca pramāṇa abhāvāt setsyati iti āvartanāt atha indriya vat svayam avijñātaḥ api pramāṇa abhāvaḥ artha abhāvam jñāpayiṣyati iti abhidadhīthāḥ tat ayuktam tasya tucchatayā sakala śakti viraha lakṣaṇa tvāt indriyasya tu tad viparyasta tayā jñāna utpādana dakṣa tvāt tasmāt pratyakṣam evam bhū tala ādi pratiniyata vastu grāhitām bibharti yadi tad viparīta ghaṭa ādi pratiyogi vastu antara vaiviktyam tasya akalayati na anyathā vijātīya vyavaccheda abhāve tasya aiva pratiniyata tva asiddheḥ sakala saṅkīrṇa tayā grahaṇa prasaṅgāt atas adhika grāhya abhāvāt nirviṣaya tayā abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam yat paraiḥ paryakalpi tat apramāṇam iti sthitam 
NA_1.18^1	 dvidhā iti asmin sati api pratyakṣam ca parokṣam ca iti niyata dvaividhya pradarśanena saugata parikalpitam pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti dvaividhyam apakṣipati tad ākūtena tasya ayogāt pratyakṣa atiriktam hi tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa sambandha upalakṣita kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi rūpa liṅga traya sampādita janmakam anumānam eva pramāṇam na śābda ūha ādikam sambandha vikala tvāt iti tadā ākūtam ayuktam ca aitat pratyakṣa anumāna atirikta pramāṇa antara abhāva grahaṇa upāya abhāvāt na tāvat pratyakṣāt pramāṇa antara abhāva avagatiḥ tasya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvena abhāva grāhita avirodhāt na api svabhāva kārya anumānābhyām tayoḥ vastu sādhaka tvāt na api anupalabdheḥ tasyāḥ api atyanta abhāva sādhana virodhāt 
NA_1.18^2	 sā hi caturvidhā varṇyate mūla bheda apekṣayā tat yathā viruddha upalabdhiḥ viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ ca iti na tāvat viruddha upalabdheḥ pramāṇa antarasya atyanta abhāvaḥ dṛśya ātmanaḥ viruddhasya vidhānena itara abhāva sādhanāt sannihita deśaḥ eva pratiyogi abhāva siddheḥ etena viruddha kārya upalabdhiḥ api vyākhyātāḥ tasyāḥ api pratiṣedhya virodhi sannidhāpana dvāreṇa abhāva sādhaka tvāt kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api tad deśa āśaṅkita kāryasya aiva abhāvam sādhayati na sarvatra svayam asiddha tvāt svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ api eka jñāna saṃsargi padārtha upalambha rūpā tad deśaḥ eva pratidvandvi abhāvam gamayati atas pramāṇa antarasya api kvacid niṣedhaḥ syāt na sarvatra tat na pramāṇa antara bādhakam samasti 
NA_1.19^1	 pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ ca prāmāṇyam kutas iti cintyam na tāvat pratyakṣāt tasya nirvikalpaka tayā sataḥ api asat kalpa tvāt tad pṛṣṭha bhāvī vikalpaḥ tu na sva lakṣaṇa ambhodhi madhyam avagāhate tat katham tatra apraviṣṭaḥ tad svarūpam niścinuyāt apramāṇa bhūtāt ca tasmāt prāmāṇya nirṇayaḥ iti nibiḍa jaḍima āviṣkaraṇam bhavatām anumānāt prāmāṇya nirṇayaḥ iti ced na tasya api sva lakṣaṇāt bahis plavanāt aprāmāṇya vyavacchedaḥ tena sādhyate iti ced na vyavacchedasya vyavacchinna avyatirekāt itaratha andhakāra nartana kalpam anumānam āsajyeta nirviṣaya tvāt kim ca tad prāmāṇya nirṇāyakam anumānam pramāṇam apramāṇam vā na tāvat apramāṇam tatas prāmāṇya asiddheḥ na api pramāṇam tad prāmāṇya sādhaka abhāvāt na hi pratyakṣāt tad siddhiḥ vikalpa śūnyatayā kiñcitkara tvāt iti uktam anumānāt tu tad sādhane vikalpa yugalam tad avastham eva avatiṣṭheta tad prāmāṇya sādhane api anumāna kalpanā iti anavasthā 
NA_1.19^2	 kim ca gṛhīta sambandhasya anumānam pravarteta sambandhaḥ tri kāla gocaraḥ grāhyaḥ na ca pratyakṣam tam lakṣayitum kṣamate pūrva aparakṣaṇa truṭita rūpa vārtamāni kakṣaṇa grahaṇa paryavasita sattāka tvāt tad uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ vikalpasya api vyāvahārika abhiprāyeṇa tad niṣṭhata abhyupagamāt anumānāt grahīṣyati iti ced nanu tat api sambandha pūrvakam pravarteta tad grahaṇe api iyam vārtā iti anavasthā tasmāt anumānam abhilaṣatā gati antara abhāvāt tad sambandha grahaṇa pravaṇaḥ tri kāla gocaraḥ avyabhicārī vitarkaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā ca prastuta tad dvaividhyasya vighaṭita tvāt anyat api yat evaṃvidham avisaṃvādi jñānam tat pramāṇam astu iti alam śuṣka abhimānena iti yadi punar sādhya arthāni atha anupapanna hetu sampāditam anumānam iṣyeta tadā pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti api dvaividhyam ghaṭām aṭet eva pratyakṣa vyatirikta jñānasya sāmastyena anumāne antarbhāva sambhavāt anyathā anupapanna artha antaram antareṇa parokṣa artha viṣaya pratīteḥ abhāvāt iti 
NA_1.20^1	 sāmpratam anyathā sūtra avayavena aiva prakṛta niyama kāraṇam āha meya viniścayāt iti dvidhā eva iti ca kāka akṣi golaka nyāyena atra api sambandhanīyam tatas ca ayam arthaḥ dvābhyām eva prakārābhyām meyasya grāhya arthasya viniścayāt svarūpa nirṇayāt dve eva yathā ukte pramāṇe na nyūnam adhikam ca iti ayam atra abhiprāyaḥ sva saṃvedanam prati nikhila jñānānām eka rūpa tayā sākṣāt karaṇa catura tvāt na asti eva bhedaḥ bahis artham punar apekṣya kaścid cakṣuḥ ādi sāmagrī bala labdha sattākaḥ sva avayava vyāpinam kāla antara saṃcariṣṇum sthagi ta kṣaṇa vivartam alakṣita paramāṇu pārimāṇḍalyam sannihitam viśada nirbhāsam sāmānyam ākāram sākṣāt kurvāṇaḥ prakāśaḥ prathate tatra pratyakṣa vyavahāraḥ pravartate 
NA_1.20^2	 yaḥ punar liṅga śabda ādi dvāreṇa niyatā niyata sāmānya ākāra avalokī parisphuṭa tā rahitaḥ khalu ātmanaḥ artha grahaṇa pariṇāmaḥ samullasati sa parokṣatām svīkaroti na ca aitau prakārau vihāya prakāra antareṇa jñāna pravṛttim paśyāmaḥ na ca apaśyantaḥ pramāṇa antara parikalpanam kṣamāmahe na ca dvayoḥ prathamānayoḥ ekam nihnuvānam apekṣāmahe viśeṣa abhāvāt tasmāt etat eva dvaividhyam urarīkartavyam iti sthitam 
NA_2.0	 sāmpratam yat asmābhiḥ prāk vivṛṇvadbhiḥ vyudapādi yat uta vipratipanna avyutpanna vyāmoha apoha saham iha idam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam iti tad sūtra mātra darśanāt eva vimala buddhayaḥ avagaccheyuḥ manda matayaḥ tu tāvatā na bhotsyante iti tad hita vidhitsayā vyaktam pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhidhāna phalam pratipipādayiṣuḥ api sa pūrva pakṣam nirākāṅkṣam lakṣayeyuḥ te iti tāvat pūrva pakṣam utthāpayan āha prasiddhāni pramāṇāni vyavahāraḥ ca tad kṛtaḥ pramāṇa lakṣaṇasya uktau jñāyate na prayojanam 
NA_2.1^1	 iha vacanam uccārayatā vimṛśya bhāṣiṇā pratyavamṛśyam kim idam māmakam vacanam śrotṛ saṃskāra ādhāyakam uta na iti itarathā paryālocita kāritā asya hīyate śrotṛ saṃskāra ādhāyakam ced uccārayati anyathā viparyayaḥ iti etat tu pramāṇa lakṣaṇa vākyam sakala janānādi prarūḍha artha pratyāyaka tvāt aśrotṛ saṃskāra ādhāyakam yatas āha prasiddhāni praruḍhāni na adhunā sādhyāni iti arthaḥ pramāṇāni pratyakṣa ādīni parokṣa gata bheda apekṣayā bahuvacanam vyakti bhede sāmānyam api kathañcid bhidyate iti darśana artham tathā hi tat avivakṣita vyaktikam eka rūpa tām bibharti pramāṇam iti vyakti avacchedena punar avacchidyamānam nānā tām ādatte pratyakṣa anumāna śābdāni pramāṇāni iti vyakti vyatirikta avyatirikta rūpa tvāt tasya tathā hi śabdāt cakṣuḥ ādeḥ vā dūrāt vṛkṣaḥ iti pratyaye dhava khadira palāśa ādi viśeṣa anapekṣayā sādhāraṇam vṛkṣa tvam eva cakāsti tasmāt tat tebhyaḥ bhinnam tad vyatirekiṇa ākāreṇa jñāne pratibhāsanāt ghaṭa ādi vat 
NA_2.1^2	 parisphuṭa dhava khadira palāśa ādi viśeṣa avalokana velāyām tu na tat atirekiṇā rūpeṇa prakāśate iti abhinnam tat avyatiriktasya saṃvedanāt tad svarūpa vat viśeṣa abhinnam eva rūpam tāttvikam sāmānyasya tasya aiva dāha pāka ādi artha kriyā kṣama tvāt bhinnam punar kalpanā buddhi viṭhapita tvāt avastu rūpam iti ced na dvayoḥ prakāśamānayoḥ ekasya nihnotum aśakya tvāt anyathā bhinnam eva rūpam svābhāvikam itarat tu kalpanā buddhi darśitam iti api vadatām na vadana bhaṅgaḥ syāt artha kriyā kāritā viśeṣaḥ tu bhinne api rūpe na durupapādaḥ tasya api jñāna sādhāraṇa vyavahāra karaṇa dakṣa tvāt na ca artha kriyā vastu lakṣaṇam iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ tasmāt sarvatra bhinna abhinnau sāmānya viśeṣau iti darśana arthaḥ bahuvacana nirdeśaḥ āsatām tāvat pramāṇāni 
NA_2.2^1	 vyavahāraḥ ca tad kṛtaḥ prasiddhaḥ iti sambandhaḥ caśabdaḥ api śabda arthaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ yad artham pramāṇa parīkṣaṇam asau api jala pāna śīta trāṇa ādiḥ vyavahāraḥ anādi prarūḍhaḥ tat nirarthakam pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhidhānam iti abhiprāyavān api paraḥ paruṣa tā parijihīrṣayā ātmanaḥ anyathā prāha pramāṇa lakṣaṇasya uktau para rūpa vyāvarta nakṣa māsa ādhāraṇa pramāṇa dharma kathana rūpāyām jñāyate nirṇīyate asmābhiḥ na prayojanam tad phalam ati sūkṣma tvāt tāvaka abhisandheḥ iti kā akvā praśnayati ulluṇṭhayati ca iti kim ca pramāṇa lakṣaṇam aniścitam vā abhidhīyate niścitam vā svarūpeṇa iti pakṣa dvayam na tāvat aniścitam aniścitasya lakṣaṇa tva ayogāt unmattaka viruta vat atha niścitam tat kim apramāṇāt pramāṇāt vā na tāvat apramāṇāt apramāṇasya niścāyaka tva ayogāt 
NA_2.2^2	 yadi punar apramāṇam api niścāyakam iti saṅgīryeta tadā pramāṇa paryeṣaṇam viśīryeta nairarthakyāpatteḥ apramāṇāt api niścāya abhyupagamāt atha pramāṇāt tat kim alakṣaṇam lakṣaṇa upetam vā alakṣaṇam ced niścāyakam pramāṇam tarhi sarva pramāṇānām lakṣaṇa abhidhānam anarthakam tad vyatirekeṇa api artha niścaya siddheḥ bhavat abhipreta lakṣaṇa niścāyaka pramāṇa vat atha lakṣaṇa upetam tatra api vikalpa yugalam anuvārita prasaram anudhāvati tad lakṣaṇam niścitam aniścitam vā na tāvat aniścitam lakṣaṇam lakṣyam lakṣayati niścayaḥ api pramāṇāt apramāṇāt vā apramāṇān niścaya asiddheḥ pramāṇāt iti vaktavyam tat api alakṣaṇam sa lakṣaṇam vā alakṣaṇa tve pūrvasya artha grahaṇe kim kṣūṇam sa lakṣaṇa tve tad lakṣaṇam nirṇītam anirṇītam vā iti tat eva āvartate tat na pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhidhāna upāyaḥ asti tasmāt prasiddhāni pramāṇāni iti aṅgīkartavyam iti 
NA_3.0–3.1^1	 adhunā ācāryaḥ gṛhītaḥ tāvakīnaḥ abhiprāyaḥ asmābhiḥ iti param pratyāyayan tat matam anudrāvya tat eva anumanyamānaḥ tathā api lakṣaṇa ukteḥ sāphalyam āvedayan āha prasiddhānām pramāṇānām lakṣaṇa uktau prayojanam tad vyāmoha nivṛttiḥ syāt vyāmūḍha manasām iha etat abhyadhāyi bhavatā yathā prasiddhāni pramāṇāni tatas teṣām lakṣaṇa uktau asādhāraṇa dharma kathana viṣaye prayojanam phalam kim iti śeṣaḥ tat etat ayuktam yatas yadi api pratiprāṇi prasiddhāni pramāṇāni anyathā tad kṛta nikhila vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt tat ucchede ca dṛṣṭa hāni ādi āpatteḥ tathā api kecid vitata moha avaṣṭabdha antaḥkaraṇāḥ tad svarūpam anubhavantaḥ api na lakṣayanti tatas tān avalokayatām asmākam tad viṣaya kṛpā parīta cetasām yathā avasthita pramāṇa lakṣaṇa āvirbhāvana dvāreṇa vyāmoham eteṣām apasārayāmaḥ iti pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhidhānam prati pravartate cetaḥ 
NA_3.1^2	 tat idam prayojanam tad vyāmoha nivṛttiḥ syāt iti tasmin pramāṇa lakṣaṇe vyāmohaḥ viparīta abhyupagamavatām viparyāsa lakṣaṇaḥ tīrthyānām pramāṇa apramāṇa viveka vikalānām anadhyavasāya ātmakaḥ tu mugdha buddhīnām laukikānām tasya nivṛttiḥ aviparīta lakṣaṇa avagamāt apagamaḥ iti arthaḥ sā syāt bhavet keṣām iti āha vyāmūḍham viparīta graha grastam vicitta tām gatam manaḥ antaḥkaraṇam yeṣām te tathā teṣām iha iti loke tat ayam tātparya arthaḥ 
NA_3.1^3	 yadi anādi prasiddham pramāṇa lakṣaṇam prati na kecid api vyāmuhyeyuḥ tadā yat bhavadbhiḥ prāk udagrāhi nirarthakam pramāṇa lakṣaṇa abhidhānam iti tat yuktam eva syāt na ca āitat evam tatra vyāmūḍhānām darśanāt etena yat adāyi dūṣaṇam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam aniścitam niścitam vā abhidhīyata ityādi tat api siddha sādhya tā madhya pratibaddha tvāt na bādhā vidhāyī asmākam iti mantavyam vyāmūḍha manasaḥ api prati pramāṇa lakṣaṇa prakāśane tat lagati iti ced na sva saṃvedana siddhasya vacanena prakāśanāt tasya vyāmoha apohaḥ eva vyāpārāt 
NA_3.1^4	 yathā vivikta bhū talāva lokane api adhyakṣāt yaḥ ghaṭa ādi vaiviktyam na pratipadyate kudarśana vyāmohāt tam pratyucyeta na asti atra ghaṭa upalambha kāraṇa samagra tāyām api anupalambhāt vaiviktyam hi tatra adhyakṣa siddham vacanāt vyāmohaḥ nivartyeta tathā iha api vidvadbhiḥ draṣṭavyam nirṇītam tad lakṣaṇam adhyakṣeṇa tasya vyavasāya rūpa tvāt vacanam punar viparīta āropa nirākaraṇe vyāpriyate iti sthitam tat evam pramāṇa lakṣaṇam sāmānyena pratipādya tad gatam kuca udyam paryahāri ācāryeṇa 
NA_4.0	 adhunā tad viṣayām eva saṃkhyā vipratipattim nirācikīrṣatā ye pratyakṣa parokṣa lakṣaṇe pramāṇa vyaktī prāk prakrānte tayoḥ api lakṣaṇam prati vipratipadyante apare atas tad lakṣaṇam api vaktavyam iti tāvat pratyakṣa lakṣaṇam abhidhātu kāmaḥ āha aparokṣatayā arthasya grāhakam jñānam īdṛśam pratyakṣam itarat jñeyam parokṣam grahaṇa īkṣayā 
NA_4.1	 tatra pratyakṣam iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ aparokṣatayā arthasya grāhakam jñānam iti lakṣaṇa nirdeśaḥ parokṣaḥ akṣa gocara atītaḥ tatas anyaḥ aparokṣaḥ tad bhāvaḥ tad tā tayā sākṣātkṛta tayā iti yāvat aryate iti arthaḥ avagamyate iti hṛdayam arthyate iti vā arthaḥ dāha pāka ādi artha kriyā arthibhiḥ abhilaṣyate iti yāvat tasya grāhakam vyavasāya ātmaka tayā sākṣāt paricchedakam yat jñānam tat īdṛśam iti īdṛś eva pratyakṣam iti saṇṭaṅkaḥ tatra jñāna grahaṇena yat sāṃkhyāḥ prāhuḥ śrotra ādi vṛttiḥ pratyakṣam iti tat tiraskaroti śrotra ādīnām prakṛti vikāra tayā tad vṛtteḥ vyāpāra lakṣaṇāyāḥ jaḍa tayā pratyakṣa tva ayogāt artha paricchitti hetu tayā pratyakṣa tve āloka ādi jaḍa kāraṇa kalāpa vyāpārasya api pratyakṣatāpadyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt iti 
NA_4.2	 arthasya grāhakam iti asya grahaṇa īkṣaya iti vakṣyamāṇa padasāpekṣa tvāt amunā bahis api ye artha kalā kalana vikalam sakalam api jñānam pralapanti tān nirasyati sva aṃśa grahaṇe hi antar saṃvedanam vyāpriyate yathā tathā bahis api ita ratha artha vat jñāna santāna antarāṇi api viśīryeran svapna dṛṣṭāntena tad anumānasya upaplava mātra tā āpatteḥ sva vijñānasya aiva tathā tathā vijṛmbhaṇāt tathā ca pramāṇa prameya pratipādya pratipādaka kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādayaḥ pralīyeran ātma vyatirekeṇa ātmīya pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ api jñānasya pravṛtti nirodha āpatteḥ advaya vijñāna tattva sādhanena anukūlam ācarasi iti ced syāt etat yadi bhavataḥ pramāṇa paridṛṣṭa sakala vyavahāra ucchedena kudarśana vāsanā hita adṛṣṭā dvaya tattva parikalpanāt pratikūlam na syāt tat na artha viraheṇa bahis pramāṇa bhūta jñāna ullāsaḥ asti nirhetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti 
NA_4.3^1	 grāhakam iti ca nirṇāyakam draṣṭavyam nirṇaya abhāve artha grahaṇa ayogāt tena yat tāthāgataiḥ pratyapādi pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham abhrāntam iti tat apāstam bhavati tasya yukti rikta tvāt tathā hi te nirvikalpaka tve adhyakṣasya ayuktīḥ kheṭayanti kila idam artha sāmarthyena udīyate sannihita artha kriyā samartha artha grāhaka tvāt na ca arthe dhvanayaḥ santi tad hetu vilakṣaṇa kāraṇa antara janya tvāt tatas ca asau upanipatya sva gocaram saṃvedanam utthāpayan su a ākāram anukārayati tat na tad grāhiṇi vijñāne śabda saṃśleṣaḥ yuktaḥ kim ca yadi utpādaka artha upayoge api tam tāvat na gṛhṇīyāt saṃvedanam api tu smaraṇa sampāditam tad abhidhāyaka dhvani saṃyojanam pratīkṣamāṇam tāvat āsīta tarhi dattaḥ jala añjaliḥ artha grahaṇasya 
NA_4.3^2	 tathā hi tam artham apaśyan tasmin gṛhīta saṅketam tad abhidhāyaka dhvanim na anusmarati upāya abhāvāt ananusmaran ca puras vartini arthe na yojayati smṛti upasthāpana vyatirekeṇa tad yojana aśakteḥ ayojayan ca bhavat abhiprāyeṇa na paśyati iti dhāndhyāt āndhyam āpadyeta yadi ca indriya jam api jñānam vikalpa kaluṣitam iṣyeta tadā tat api manaḥ rājya ādi vikalpa vat vikalpa antara āvirbhāve sati nivarteta na ca āitat asti sannihita gopiṇḍa gocarasya cakṣuḥ ja saṃvedanasya aśva ādi viṣaya vikalpa udaye api anivartanāt saṃhṛta sakala vikalpasya api ca parisphuṭa sannihita artha viṣaya darśana siddheḥ tat na akṣajam jñānam śabda samparkam anubhavati iti 
NA_4.4^1	 atra pratividhīyate yat tāvat uktam aśabdaka artha sāmarthya udbhava tvāt dhvani rahitam adhyakṣam iti tat ayuktam na hi śabda asampṛkta artha jam iti etāvatā aiva abhilāpa vinākṛtam iti vaktum śakyam anyathā jaḍa artha janitam iti jaḍam api tat syāt atha bodha rūpa manaskāra sāhityāt na jaḍam iti brūṣe tathā sati abhilāpa saṃsṛṣṭa manaskāra sanniyogāt sa abhilāpam api syāt kim ca viviktāḥ paramāṇavaḥ su a ākāra arpaṇa dvāreṇa sva gocaram jñānam utpādayantaḥ katham asantam ātmani sva avayava vyāpinam kāla antara saṃcariṣṇum ākāram tatra prathayanti vibhramāt iti ced na na idānīm arthe yat asti tat eva pratibhāti tatra asataḥ api sthūra ākārasya pratibhāsanāt tathā śabdaḥ api yadi avidyamānaḥ arthe tad grāhiṇi jñāne pratibhāseta kim kṣūyeta 
NA_4.4^2	 yat ca uktam smaraṇa janita śabda saṃyojanam pratīkṣamānam artha upayoge api yadi āsīta ityādi yāvat āndhyam āpadyeta tat tāvaka pakṣe api samānam tathā hi sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya indriya janiḥ vikalpaka jñāna sadbhāve api na tāvat idaṃtayā nidaṃtayā vā artha vyavasthitiḥ yāvat vidhi pratiṣedha dvāreṇa vikalpa yugalakam pāścātyam na udayate yatra aiva aṃśe vikalpam janayati tatra aiva asya pramāṇa tā iti vacanān nirvikalpakasya sataḥ api vyavahāram prati asat kalpa tvāt sa ca vikalpaḥ saṅketa kāla bhāvitam abhilāpa sāmānyam anusmarataḥ eva utpattum arhati abhilāpa sāmānya smaraṇa bījam ca kutas prabudhyeta tādṛśa darśanāt iti ced nanu tat api darśanam nirvikalpaka tvāt artham na atiśete tat katham sāmānya viṣaya vikalpa bījam prabodhayet 
NA_4.4^3	 arthaḥ punar sāmānya vyavasāya ātmikām buddhim na janayet iti bhavatām kadā grahaḥ tat arthavat tad viṣayam darśanam vyavasāya śūnya tvāt na abhilāpa sāmānya gocara smaraṇa bījam prabodhayati tat aprabuddham na smaraṇam janayati ajātam smaraṇam na śabdam yojayati ayojitaḥ śabdaḥ na artham niścāyayati aniścitaḥ arthaḥ na vyavahāram avatarati anavatīrṇaḥ na adṛṣṭāt viśiṣyate aviśiṣṭaḥ pramātuḥ āndhyam lakṣayati iti tasmāt yathā kathañcid nirṇaya abhāvāt svayam apratītam api nirvikalpaka darśanam vāsanā prabodha dvāreṇa vikalpam utthāpya ātma vyāpāram abhilāpayati katicid aṃśa viṣayam tathā arthaḥ api yadi cakṣuḥ ādi sāmagrī antaḥ pāti tvena apratītaḥ eva svayam tathā asvabhāva tvāt saṅketa kāla bhāvita abhilāpa sāmānya viṣaya ātma saṃskāra prabodha dvāreṇa ātma viṣayam abhilāpa saṃsṛṣṭam saṃvedanam ullāsayet na atyantam ayuktam paśyāmaḥ 
NA_4.4^4	 na ca ayam sa vikalpakaḥ bodhaḥ manaḥ rājya ādi vikalpa kalpaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi sāmagrī sampādya tvāt itarasya tu manaḥ mātra prabhava tvāt atas katham tad vikalpa antara āvirbhāve nivarteta mānasa vikalpasya aiva vikalpa antareṇa nivartanāt asya tu kāraṇa sāmarthyena balāt pravṛtteḥ etena saṃhṛta sakala vikalpa avasthāyām na āiṣa prāduḥṣyāt iti etat api pratikṣiptam asya pramātuḥ icchayā saṃhartum aśakya tvān mānasa vikalpa saṃharaṇaḥ eva tad sāmarthya upapatteḥ iti etat ca śabda sampṛkta pratyakṣa pakṣāt api ekānta nirvikalpaka pratyakṣa pakṣasya pāpīyaḥ tām darśayadbhiḥ asmābhiḥ udagrāhi 
NA_4.5^1	 paramārthataḥ punar pratyakṣe sākṣāt śabda ullekhaḥ na iṣyate viśada vyavasāyena artha sākṣāt karaṇa catura tvāt tasya kevalam tat api sannihitam parisphuṭam sva avayava vyāpinam kāla antara saṃcariṣṇum sthagi ta kṣaṇa vivartam alakṣita paramāṇu pārimāṇḍalyam padārtha antaraiḥ saha samāna asamāna ākāram sva paramāṇūnām sāmānya ākāram stambha adhikam padārtham gocarayati iti sa vikalpakam iti ucyate para parikalpita kṣaṇa kṣayi vivikta paramāṇu lakṣaṇa sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa pravaṇa nirvikalpaka pratyakṣa pratiṣedha artham kathañcid abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya gocara tā darśana artham vā evam ca pratyakṣa gocarīkṛte arthe saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandha grahaṇa ādayaḥ tad viṣayāḥ śābda vyavahārāḥ sarve eva nirupacaritā ghaṭantaḥ iti uktam bhavati 
NA_4.5^2	 yadi punar śabda saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsam adhyakṣam na syāt tatas kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced vikalpa anutthānena sakala vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi nirvyavasāyam darśanam atyanta pāṭava upetam api smṛti bīja ādhānam tad uttara kāla bhāvi vā tādṛśa artha darśanam tad prabodhanam abhyāsa vāsanā pāṭave api na vidhātum alam yatas sāmānya vikalpa utpattyā vyavahāraḥ pravarteta kṣaṇika tva ādiṣu sakala kālam nirvikalpaka adhyakṣa dṛṣṭa tayā abhyupagateṣu api tad adarśanāt tasmāt yatra kutracid artha aṃśe pāścātya vyavahāra pravṛttiḥ tatra prācīnam saṃvedanam nirṇāyakam abhyupagantavyam anyathā kṣaṇika tva ādi aṃśa vat sarva aṃśeṣu vyavahāraḥ pralīyeta tat na kadācana kalpanā apoḍha tvam pratyakṣasya pramātuḥ api pratīti gocara cāritām anubhavati apratītam ca asti iti śraddhātum duḥśakam atiprasaṅgāt iti alakṣaṇam 
NA_4.6	 abhrānta tvam api na jāghaṭī iti bhavat abhiprāyeṇa sthira sthūra artha grāhiṇaḥ saṃvedanasya viparyasta rūpa tvāt tad viparītasya tu svapna kāle api aprakāśa māna tvāt tat yadi yathā avasthita artha grāhi tvam abhrānta tvam tat na sambhavati eva vivikta kṣaṇa kṣayi paramāṇūnām kadācid api apratibhāsāt teṣām ca pāramārthika tvāt atha vyāvahārika abhiprāyeṇa yat idam ghaṭa ādikam sva lakṣaṇam artha kriyā kṣamam tatra yat na bhrāmyati tat abhra antam iti abhipretam tarhi kalpanā apoḍha padam utsāraṇīyam idānīm anena saha avasthāna abhāvāt vyavahāra avatāriṇaḥ ghaṭa ādi sva lakṣaṇasya nirṇayena aiva grahaṇāt anyathā vyavahāra apravṛtteḥ dṛṣṭasya api adṛṣṭa anati śayanāt tasmāt vyavasāya ātmakam adhyakṣam iti etat eva cāru iti sthitam 
NA_4.7	 aparokṣatayā iti anena tu parokṣa lakṣaṇa saṅkīrṇa tām adhyakṣasya pariharati tasya sākṣātkāri tayā artha grahaṇa rūpa tvāt iti īdṛśam iti amunā tu pūrva ukta nyāyāt sa avadhāraṇena viśeṣaṇa kadambaka saciva jñāna upapradarśanāt para parikalpita lakṣaṇa yuktasya pratyakṣatām pratikṣipati evam ca yat āhuḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa utpannam jñānam avyapadeśyam avyabhicāri vyavasāya ātmakam pratyakṣam tathā sat samprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇām buddhi janma tat pratyakṣam ityādi tat ayuktam iti uktam bhavati apūrva prādurbhāvasya pramāṇa bādhita tvāt atyanta asatām śaśa viṣāṇa ādīnām api utpatti prasaṅgāt tasmāt idam ātma rūpa tayā vidyamānam eva viśeṣa kṛt hetu kalāpa sannidhānāt sākṣāt artha grahaṇa pariṇāma rūpa tayā vivarteta tathā ca utpanna janma ādi viśeṣaṇam na sambhavet atha aivaṃvidha artha sūcakam eva āitat iti ācakṣīthāḥ tathā sati avigānam eva iti āstām tāvat 
NA_4.8	 adhunā parokṣa lakṣaṇam darśayati itarat ityādi aparokṣatayā arthasya grāhakam jñānam pratyakṣam iti uktam tasmāt itarat asākṣāt artha grāhakam jñānam parokṣam iti jñeyam avagantavyam etat api sva saṃvedana apekṣayā pratyakṣam eva bahis artha apekṣayā tu parokṣa vyapadeśam aśnutaḥ iti darśayan āha grahaṇa īkṣaya iti iha grahaṇam prakramāt bahis pravartanam ucyate anyathā viśeṣaṇa vaiyarthyāt tasya īkṣa apekṣā tayā bahis pravṛtti paryālocanayā iti yāvat tat ayam arthaḥ yadi api svayam pratyakṣam tathā api liṅga śabda ādi dvāreṇa bahis viṣaya grahaṇe asākṣāt kāritayā vyāpriyate iti parokṣam iti ucyate etat ca bubhutsita arthānyatha anupapanna artha antara pratīti vaśāt udaya dharmakam iti sāmānya lakṣaṇa sadbhāvāt eka ākāram api vipratipatti nirākaraṇa artham dvidhā bhidyate tat yathā anumānam śābdam ca iti yatas adya api śabdasya arthān yatha anupapanna tvam eva pare na pratipadyante na ca apṛthak kṛtasya tat viviktam vaktum śakyam atas bhedena upanyāsaḥ 
NA_5.0–5.1^1	 tatra tāvat anumāna lakṣaṇam abhidhitsuḥ āha sādhyāvinābhunaḥ liṅgāt sādhya niścāyakam smṛtam anumānam tat abhra antam pramāṇa tvāt samakṣa vat iha api anumānam iti lakṣya nirdeśaḥ tasya prasiddha tayā anūdya tvāt sādhyāvinābhunaḥ liṅgāt sādhya niścāyakam iti lakṣaṇa nirdeśaḥ tasya aprasiddha tayā vidheya tvāt iti atra api anumāna śabdasya kartṛ ādi kāraka vyutpatti krameṇa artha kathanam pramāṇa śabda vat draṣṭavyam tatas ca iha api liṅga grahaṇa sādhya avinābhāvi tva lakṣaṇa liṅga sambandha smaraṇa kālāt anu paścāt mīyate paricchidyate arthaḥ anumeyaḥ pāvaka ādiḥ yena jñānena tat anumānam iti tat kiṃbhūtam iti āha sādhya niścāyakam iti sādhanam arhati sādhayitum vā śakyaḥ iti sādhyaḥ anumeyaḥ iti arthaḥ tasya niścāyakam tad svarūpa nirṇāyakam iti yāvat 
NA_5.1^2–5.3	 tat kutas iti āha liṅgāt liṅgyate gamyate arthaḥ anena iti liṅgam hetuḥ tasmāt kiṃbhūtāt iti āha sādhyāvinābhunaḥ iti vinā bhavati iti vinā ābhu tatas anyat avinābhu sādhyena avinābhu sādhyāvinābhu sādhyam vimucya yat na bhavati iti arthaḥ tasmāt sādhya niścāyakam jñānam tat anumānam smṛtam abhipretam nīti vidbhiḥ iti sambandhaḥ tatra liṅgāt sādhya niścāyakam iti anena anumānasya pratyakṣa śābda lakṣaṇa saṅkīrṇa tām vārayati sādhyāvinābhunaḥ iti anena para praṇīta liṅga lakṣaṇa vyudāsam ācaṣṭe tatas ca yat pare procuḥ pakṣa dharma tva anvaya vyatireka lakṣaṇa rūpa traya upalakṣitāni trīṇi eva liṅgāni anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvaḥ kāryam ca iti tat uktam anumeye atha tad tulye sadbhāvaḥ na astitā asati niścita anupalambha ātma kārī a ākhyāḥ hetavaḥ trayaḥ iti 
NA_5.4^1	 tathā anye asya idam kāryam kāraṇam saṃyogi samavāyi virodhi ca iti laiṅgikam iti tathā pūrvavat śeṣavat sāmānyatodṛṣṭam ityādi tat bāla pralapita prāyam iti avagantavyam sarvatra sādhya avinābhāvi tvasya aiva gamaka tvāt tat rahitasya tu trailakṣaṇya lakṣitasya api agamaka tvāt itarathā tad putra tva ādīnām api gamaka tva prasaṅgān niyama vat trailakṣaṇyam lakṣaṇam na yat kiñcid tena ayam aprasaṅgaḥ iti ced na niyamena sādhya avinābhāvi tvasya aiva uddīpanāt tat ced asti kim trailakṣaṇya apekṣayā tasya aiva gamaka tvāt tathā hi jala candrāt nabhaḥ candram kṛttikā udayāt śakaṭa udayam puṣpita aika cūtāt puṣpita aśeṣa cūtān candra udayāt kumuda ākara prabodham vṛkṣāt chāyām ityādi pakṣa dharma tva virahe api anumimīmahe 
NA_5.4^2	 kāla ādikaḥ tatra dharmī samasti eva tatra pakṣa dharma tā liṅgasya gṛhyate iti ced na ati prasaṅgāt evam hi śabdasya anitya tve sādhye kāka kārṣṇi ādeḥ api gamaka tva prasakteḥ tatra api loka ādeḥ dharmiṇaḥ kalpayitum śakya tvāt tathā anvaya vikalaḥ api anityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt iti ayam samyak hetu tayā samarthayitum śakyaḥ iti na anvayaḥ api hetoḥ lakṣaṇam tathā hi tāvaka ākūtena aiva sakalam sattvam anitya tayā kroḍīkṛtam iti bhāva dharmaḥ śrāvaṇa tvam katham anitya tām vihāya vipakṣe vartitum utsaheta tad vikalasya niḥsvabhāvatā āpatteḥ anitya tā vinirmuktasya sattvasya asambhavāvat etena sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimattvān nirātmaka tve tad vaikalya prasaṅgāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti ayam api gamakaḥ vyākhyātaḥ sādhya arthāni atha anupapanna tvasya atra api sadbhāvāt pakṣa dharma tva anvayayoḥ tu alakṣaṇa tayā pratipādanāt 
NA_5.5^1	 tathā kārya svabhāva anupalabdhi rūpa liṅga traya niyamaḥ api kila tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa sambandha astitvam eteṣu eva iti yaḥ kriyate saḥ api ayuktaḥ prakṛta sambandha dvaya vikalasya api rūpa āde rasa ādi gamaka tva darśanāt mā bhūt tasya tādātmya tad utpattibhyām gamaka tvam samavāyāt bhaviṣyati tathā api na anyathā anupapanna tvam eva hetoḥ lakṣaṇam iti yadi vaiśeṣikaḥ manyeta saḥ anyathā nirloṭhanīyaḥ sa hi vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ samavāyibhyaḥ samavāyaḥ abhinnaḥ bhinnaḥ vā yadi abhinnaḥ samavāyinaḥ eva tarhi na samavāyaḥ tat avyatirikta tvāt tad svarūpa vat bhinnaḥ ced sa katham teṣu varteta sāmastyena āhosvit eka deśena 
NA_5.5^2–5.6	 tat yadi sāmastyena tat ayuktam samavāya bahutva prasaṅgāt pratisamavāyi tasya parisamāpta tā avāpteḥ atha aika deśena tat api acāru sa aṃśatā prasaṅgena niravayava tu a kṣateḥ sva aṃśa vartane api sāmastyāika deśa codyā avatārāt ca tatra api sāmastya pakṣe bahu tvam tad avastham eva eka deśa pakṣe tu aṃśa antara prasaṅgena anavasthā tat na samavāya balāt gamaka tām prati āśā vidheyāḥ tasya aiva tatra duḥsthita tvāt etena saṃyoginaḥ api gamakatā pratyuktāḥ samāna dūṣaṇa tvāt virodhinaḥ api viruddha abhāva gamaka tvam anyathā anupapanna tvam eva sūcayati tad abhāve gamaka tva ayogāt evam para parikalpitam anyat api liṅga lakṣaṇam yat gamakatā aṅgam tat anyathā anupapanna tvam na vyabhicarati sādhyam vinā api upapadyamānasya gamaka tā vaikalyāt iti atra aiva vyāpake liṅga lakṣaṇe antar bhāvanīyam viparītam tu nirasanīyam iti sthitam 
NA_5.7^1	 tat evam anumāna lakṣaṇam pratipādya adhunā yat śauddhodaniśiṣyakaiḥ nyagādi yat uta bhrāntam anumānam sāmānya pratibhāsi tvāt tasya ca bahis sva lakṣaṇe vyatireka avyatireka vikalpābhyām apākriyamāṇa tayā ayogāt tad rūpa tayā ca tena tasya adhyavasāyāt atasmin tad grahaṇasya ca bhrānti lakṣaṇa tvāt prāmāṇyam punar praṇālikayā bahis sva lakṣaṇa bala āyātatvāt anumānasya tathā hi na artham vinā tādātmya tad utpatti rūpa sambandha pratibaddha liṅga sadbhāvaḥ na tat vinā tad viṣayam jñānam na tat jñānam antareṇa prāk avadhārita sambandha smaraṇam tat asmaraṇe na anumānam iti artha avyabhicāri tvāt bhrāntam api pramāṇam iti saṅgīryate tat uktam atasmin tad grahaḥ bhrāntiḥ api sambandhataḥ pramā iti tat apākartum āha tat abhra antam ityādi tat anumānam bhrāmyati sva gocare viparyasyati iti bhrāntam tatas anyat abhra antam aviparīta artha grāhī iti yāvat iyam ca pratijñā pramīyate yathā avasthitaḥ arthaḥ paricchidyate anena iti pramāṇam tad bhāvaḥ tattvam tasmāt 
NA_5.7^2	 ayam tu hetuḥ saṅgatam akṣāṇām iti samakṣam tat iva samakṣavat iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ tat idam anumānasya bhrānta tā nirākārakam sampūrṇa avayavam upanaya nigamanayoḥ avayava traya pratipādanena aiva ākṣipta tvāt pramāṇam sūcitam prayogaḥ tu evam draṣṭavyaḥ abhrāntam anumānam pramāṇa tvāt iha yat yat pramāṇam tat tat abhra antam yathā samakṣam tathā ca pramāṇam bhavadbhiḥ abhyupagamyate anumānam tasmāt pramāṇa tvāt abhrāntam iti pratipadyantām iti tatra artha vādī tāvat samakṣa lakṣaṇe dṛṣṭānte sādhya vikalatām āvirbhāvayitum na pārayati svayam eva samakṣasya abhrānta tayā abhyupagamāt śūnya vādinaḥ punar samasta apala api tvāt pramāṇa prameya vyavahāram praty ayogyatāiva iti na tam adhikṛtya sva sādhana doṣāḥ parihartavyāḥ sva vacana bādhita pratijña tvena tad vāda utthāna abhāvāt tathā hi sarva abhāva pratipādakam vacaḥ asti na asti vā yadi asti tarhi pratijñā hāniḥ atha na asti sakala bhāva siddhiḥ pratiṣedhaka abhāvāt 
NA_6.0–6.1	 jñāna vādī punar vedya vedaka ākāra vikalam sakala vikalpa gocara atītam nirvikalpakam vivikta pāramārthika sva saṃvedana vedyam saṃvedanam āgūrya anādi kāla ālīna vāsanā bala prabhāvitam grāhya grāhaka ākāra kaluṣitam bahiṣprathamānam nikhilam api jñānam viparyasta tayā pratijānānaḥ samakṣa lakṣaṇasya prakṛta dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya śūnyatām abhidadhyāt atas tad mata vikuṭṭana artham āha na pratyakṣam api bhrāntam pramāṇa tva viniścayāt bhrāntam pramāṇam iti etat viruddham vacanam yatas yat bhavataḥ cetasi vivartate yat uta na kevalam anumānam bhrāntam kim tarhi yat bhavadbhiḥ dṛṣṭānta tayā upāttam pratyakṣam tat api bhrāntam eva sarvam ālambane bhrāntam iti vacanāt tat etat na kutas iti āha pramāṇa tva viniścayāt iti pramāṇa bhāva nirṇayāt iti arthaḥ 
NA_6.2	 nanu ca pramāṇa tām abhra anta tā anyathā anupapannām yadi paraḥ pratipadyate tatas tām abhyupagacchan katham bhrānta tā vipratipattim vidadhyāt iti pārśva sthita vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya bhrānta tā pramāṇa tayoḥ virodha sādhanena tatas pramāṇa tām vyāvartya ananya śaraṇa tayā pratijñāta abhra anta tā ākrāntām tām darśayan āha bhrāntam ityādi bhrāntam viparyastam atha ca pramāṇam grāhya pariccheda hetuḥ iti etat vacanam evaṃviddha artha pratyāyakaḥ dhvaniḥ viruddham pūrva apara vyāhata artha garbha tvāt 
NA_6.3^1	 nanu ca na aiva asya viruddha tā tathā hi avidita parama artha vyāva hārikā abhiprāyeṇa loka saṃvṛtim ghaṭayantaḥ vayam dṛḍhatara vāsanā prabodha sampādita sattākayoḥ pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ pramāṇa tām ācakṣmahe tad abhiprāyeṇa darśita artha prāpaka tvena tayoḥ avisaṃvādaka tvāt śithila vāsanāunmukhya nirmita janmakayoḥ punar apramāṇa tām tad ākūtena aiva darśite arthe vipralambhanāt iti bhrānta tām punar tattva cintaka abhiprāyeṇa sakalasya bahis upaplavamānasya grāhya grāhaka ākāra kāluṣya dūṣitasya pratibhāsasya pāramārthikā dvaya saṃvedana viparyasta rūpa tvāt abhidadhmahe bahis pratibhāsasya tad grāhya artha vicāra akṣa matayā upapluta rūpa tvāt tathā hi arthaḥ avayavi rūpaḥ avayava rūpaḥ vā syāt gati antara abhāvāt na tāvat avayavi rūpaḥ vicāram kṣamate avayava virahe avayavi tva ayogāt teṣu ca tad vṛtti vikalpa anupapatteḥ tathā hi teṣu asau eka deśena vartate sāmastyena vā na tāvat eka deśena tasya svayam niravayava tvāt avayava vṛtti nimittam aṃśa antara kalpane tad vṛttau api aṃśa antara kalpana prasaṅgaḥ tathā ca anavasthā 
NA_6.3^2	 na api sāmastyena pratyavayavam parisamāpta rūpa tayā avaya vibahutva prasaṅgāt bheda pakṣe doṣaḥ ayam abheda pakṣe na asti iti ced na tatra api avayava mātram avayavi mātram vā syāt itaretara avyatirikta tvāt itaretara svarūpa vat kim ca samasta avayava vyāpinaḥ avayavinaḥ abhyupagame paṭa ādeḥ eka deśa rāga kampa darśana ādiṣu sakala rāga kampa darśana ādīni durnivārāṇi syuḥ ekasya rāga ārāga ādi viruddha dharma adhyāsa ayogāt iti na api avayava rūpaḥ arthaḥ vicāra gocara cārī kara caraṇa śiraḥ grīvā ādīnām avayavānām sva avayava apekṣayā avaya vi rūpa tayā tad dūṣaṇena aiva apa asta tvāt paramāṇūnām niraṃśa tayā avayava tvam upapadyate iti ced na teṣām api diś ṣaṭka sambandhena ṣaṭaṃśa tā āpatteḥ anyathā avasthāna abhāvāt tatas ca artha virahāt tad unmukhaḥ grāhya ākāraḥ alīkaḥ tad alīka tāyām grāhaka ākāraḥ api na avasthānam ābadhnāti grāhya abhāve grāhaka ayogāt tad apekṣayā aiva tad svarūpa sthitiḥ grāhya grāhaka ākāra vilaye ca bodha ākāraḥ avaśiṣyate tasya sarvatra avyabhicarita rūpa tvāt tasmāt saḥ eva pāramārthikaḥ iti 
NA_6.4^1	 atra pratividhīyate yat avādi saṃvedanam advayam pāramārthikam grāhya grāhaka ākāra pravṛttam punar atāttvikam iti tat ayuktam pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi bahis antar ca aneka ākāra tayā harṣa viṣāda ādibhiḥ sthira sthūra tā ādi aneka dharma parikarita artha grahaṇa pariṇāmaiḥ ca vivartamānam saṃvedanam upalabhyate na punar vedya vedaka ākāra viviktam yādṛś bhavadbhiḥ upavarṇyate jñānam tādṛśam kasyacid kadācana pratīti gocara cāritām anubhavati advaya pratibhāsasya svapna daśāyām api ananubhūteḥ 
NA_6.4^2	 na ca tattva cintakāḥ api pramāṇam antareṇa sva ākūtam pratiṣṭhāpayantaḥ prekṣāvatām avadheya vacanāḥ bhavanti anyathāikam acetanam avyayam api brahma anekam cetanam kṣaṇa bhaṅgu ra ta ākrāntam avidyātaḥ prathate iti bruvāṇaḥ anirākāryaḥ syāt yat api bahis artha nirākaraṇa dhiyā avayavi avayava dvāreṇa dūṣaṇam adāyi tat api bahis antar prathamāna sakalā asumad pratīta pratibhāsa mudgara nirdalita śarīra tayā bhakta madhya niṣṭhyūta darśinaḥ puratas vipratāraṇa pravaṇa kuṭṭinī śapatha prāyam iti na vidvat jana manāṃsi rañjayati pratyakṣa pratibhāsā apahnave tad mūlaka tvāt kuyukti vikalpānām utthāna abhāvāt kim ca saṃvedanasya api sita asita ādi aneka ākāreṣu ekasya vartane bheda abheda sāmastyāika deśa ādi codyam samānam eva iti na dūṣaṇam 
NA_6.4^3	 aneka ākāra vivartasya alīka tvāt na tena saha saṃvedanasya pāramārthikasya bheda abheda ādi cintā iti ced nanu evam itaretara āśrayam duruttaram āḍhaukate tathā hi tad alīka tva siddhau advaya saṃvedana siddhiḥ tad siddhau ca tad alīka tvam iti nyāyāt anyat ca advayam api eka kṣaṇa varti saṃvedanam yathā pūrva uttara kṣaṇābhyām sambandham anubhavati tathā niraṃśāḥ api yadi paramāṇavaḥ diś aṃśaiḥ paramāṇu antaraiḥ vā saṃśleṣam āgaccheyuḥ kim ayuktam syāt na ca avayavi avayavayoḥ ekānta vyatireka avyatireka pakṣe yat dūṣaṇam tat asmad pakṣa bādha ākaram paraspara avinirluṭhita rūpayoḥ vivakṣayā sandarśanīya bhedayoḥ tayoḥ abhyupagamāt bahis antar ca tathā aiva prakāśamāna tayā tayoḥ nihnotum aśakya tvāt 
NA_6.4^4	 etena rāga arāga kampā kampa ādi virodha udbhāvanam api prativyūḍham pramāṇa prasiddhe arthe virodha abhāvāt pramāṇa bādhitasya aiva viruddha tvāt kuyukti vikalpānām ca pratyakṣa apahnave nirmūla tayā bādhaka tva ayogāt tad uddalita tvena utthāna abhāvāt bhinna pravṛtti nimitta tvāt ca sarva dharmānām tad viparyaya sampādyaḥ virodhaḥ dūrāpāstaḥ eva kim ca svayam eva saṃvedanam parama artha saṃvyavahāra apekṣayā pratyakṣa apratyakṣa sa vikalpakā vikalpaka bhrānta abhra anta ādi rūpam abhyupayataḥ bahis arthe viruddha dharma adhyāsa pratiṣedha buddhiḥ kevalam jāḍyam sūcayati tat na pramāṇam kathañcid bhrāntam samasti svarūpa pracyava prasaṅgāt iti sthitam 
NA_6.5	 nanu ca tad darśita artha alīka tayā jñānasya bhrānta tā na svarūpeṇa na ca tad udaya samaye kasyacid idam alīka artham idam tu analīka artham iti vivekena avadhāraṇam samasti bhrānta abhra anta abhimatayoḥ tad eka rūpa tayā prakāśanāt yadā ca viśada darśana patha cāriṇaḥ api śaśadhara yugala ādayaḥ alīka tām āviśantaḥ dṛśyante tadā sakala satya artha tā abhimata pratibhāseṣu api alīka artha tā śaṅkā nivṛtteḥ anāśvāsaḥ eva na ca tad artha prāpti ādikam āreka anirākaraṇa kāraṇam kalpanīyam svapna avasthāyām tad sadbhāve api alīkā artha tā siddheḥ bādhaka pratyaya upanipātāt tasya asatyārtha tā iti ced na tasya sva gocara paryavasita tvena bādhaka tva ayogāt anyathā nīlam ādadānā deva datta buddhiḥ prāc pravṛtta pīta buddheḥ bādhikā āpadyeta sarva pratibhāsasya bādhaka abhāva siddheḥ ca samāna tā tasmāt bhrānta abhra anta jñāna bhrāntiḥ iyam bhavatām viveka abhāvena sarvasya alīka artha tvāt iti 
NA_7.0–7.1	 atra āha sakala pratibhāsasya bhrānta tva asidhitaḥ sphuṭam pramāṇam sva anya niścāyi dvaya siddhau prasidhyati evam manyate yaḥ api samasta saṃvedanasya bhrānta tām pratijānīte tena api tad sādhakasya abhra anta tā abhyupagantavyā tad bhrānta tve tad pratipādita artha alīka tvena sakala jñāna abhra anta tā prasaṅgāt anyathā tad bhrānta tā yogāt evam ca tad jātīyam anyat api abhra antam syāt tatas ca sakala pratibhāsasya samasta saṃvedanasya bhrānta tva asidhitaḥ viparyasta tva aniṣpatteḥ yat sphuṭam sva anya niścāyi su niścita tayā sva para prakāśakam tat pramāṇam iti sambandhaḥ tat ca dvaya siddhau svarūpa artha lakṣaṇa yugma niṣpattau prasiddhi ati niṣpadyate anyathā prameya abhāve pramāṇa abhāvāt tasmāt pramāṇam urarī kurvāṇena arthaḥ api abhyupagantavyaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ iti 
NA_8.0–8.1^1^1	 tat evam sva artha anumāna lakṣaṇam pratipādya tadvatām bhrānta tā vipratipattim ca nirākṛtya adhunā pratipādita para artha anumāna lakṣaṇaḥ eva alpa vaktavya tvāt tāvat śābda lakṣaṇam āha dṛṣṭa iṣṭa avyāhatāt vākyāt parama artha abhidhāyinaḥ tattva grāhitayā utpannam mānam śābdam prakīrtitam atra api śābdam iti lakṣyam anūdya tvāt dṛṣṭa iṣṭa avyāhatāt ityādi lakṣaṇam vidheya tvāt dṛṣṭena pramāṇa avalokitena iṣṭaḥ pratipādayiṣitaḥ avyāhataḥ anirākṛtaḥ sāmarthyāt arthaḥ yasmin vākye tat tathā pramāṇa niścita artha ābādhitam iti yāvat tasmāt paramaḥ akṛtrimaḥ puruṣa upayogī śakya anuṣṭhānaḥ vā arthaḥ vācyaḥ tam abhidhātum śīlam yasya tat parama artha abhidhāyi viśiṣṭa artha darśakam iti arthaḥ 
NA_8.0–8.1^1^2	 tatas tattva grāhitayā utpannam prakṛta vākya pratipādya artha ādāna śīla tayā labdha ātma sattākam yat mānam tat śābdam iti prakīrtitam upavarṇitam pūrva ācāryaiḥ iti sambandhaḥ tatra dṛṣṭa iṣṭā vyāhatāt iti anena kutīrthika vacasām laukika vipratārakoktīnām ca śābda tām nirasyati pramāṇa bādhita tvāt vākyāt iti amunā tu vākyasya aiva niyata artha darśaka tvāt parama artha abhidhāyitā iti darśayan padāt śābda abhāvam āha parama artha abhidhāyinaḥ iti anena jvara hara takṣaka cūḍā ratna alaṅkāra upadeśa ādi vacana prabhava jñānasya niṣphala tayā prāmāṇyam nirācaṣṭe 
NA_8.1^2	 tattva grāhitayā utpannam iti amunā tu evaṃbhūtāt api vākyāt śrotṛ doṣāt viparīta ādi artha grahaṇa caturatayā prādurbhūtasya śābda tvam vārayati mānam iti anena antar bhāvita propasarga arthena śābde parasya aprāmāṇya buddhim tiraskurute tad aprāmāṇye para artha anumāna pralaya prasaṅgāt tasya vacana rūpa tvāt tri ava yava hetu sūcaka tvena upacārataḥ tasya prāmāṇyam na tattvataḥ iti ced na apramāṇasya sūcaka tva ayogāt nanu ca hetu pratipādane yadi tat pramāṇam tatas hetu samarthaka pramāṇa antara pratīkṣaṇam viśīryeta tena aiva nirṇīta svarūpa tvāt tasya pramāṇa prasiddhe punar pramāṇa antara vaiyarthyāt nāitat asti bhavat parikalpita adhyakṣasya api aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tad darśite arthe vikalpa pratīkṣaṇāt tasya aiva prāmāṇyam āsajyeta tat gṛhītam eva artham asau abhilāpayati iti ced śabda pratipāditam hetum pramāṇa antaram samarthayate iti samānaḥ nyāyaḥ 
NA_9.0	 śābdam ca dvidhā bhavati laukikam śāstra jam ca iti tatra idam dvayoḥ api sādhāraṇam lakṣaṇam pratipāditam samarthanam punar avipratāraka vacana prabhavasya iha ādi vākya prastāvaḥ eva laukikasya vihitam śāstra jasya tu vidhātavyam iti yādṛśaḥ śāstrāt tad jātam pramāṇa tām anubhavati tat darśayati āpta upajñam anullaṅghyam adṛṣṭa iṣṭa virodhakam tattva upadeśa kṛt sārvam śāstram kāpatha ghaṭṭanam 
NA_9.1	 śāsti śikṣayati jīvājīva ādi tattvam grāhayati śiṣyate anena iti vā śāstram tat kiṃbhūtam iti tad viśeṣaṇāni āha āptaḥ prakṣīṇa aśeṣa rāga ādi doṣa gaṇaḥ tena upajñam ādau upalabdham anena apauruṣeya apoham āha tasya pramāṇa bādhita tvāt puruṣa vyāpāra abhāve vacana anupalabdheḥ upalambhe api tad arthān avagamāt tad artha niścaya artham puruṣa āśrayaṇe gaja snāna nyāya prasaṅgāt tasya rāga ādi kaluṣita tvena vitatha artha kathana pravṛtteḥ tad anuṣṭhānāt api sva kārya siddhau praṇayana artham api puruṣaḥ kim na iṣyate viśeṣa abhāvāt tat na kṣīṇa doṣa vacanam vyatiricya anyatas prekṣāvatām para loka ādau adṛṣṭe arthe pravṛttiḥ yuktāḥ tat tat eva śāstram nirupacarita śabda artha upapatteḥ iti āstām tāvat 
NA_9.2	 atas eva ullaṅghyate prābalyena gamyate abhibhūyate anyaiḥ iti ullaṅghyam tatas anyat anullaṅghyam sarva vacana atiśāyī iti yāvat atas eva dṛṣṭena pramāṇa nirṇītena iṣṭasya tad vācyasya virodhaḥ yasmin tat tathā tat eva yadi vā dṛṣṭaḥ pramāṇena iṣṭaḥ vacana antareṇa tayoḥ virodhakam tad viruddha artha abhidhānāt tatas anyat adṛṣṭa iṣṭa virodhakam abādhā artha abhidhāyi iti arthaḥ 
NA_9.3–9.4	 tat iyatā śāstrasya sva artha sampad uktāḥ adhunā tattva upadeśa ādīnām parārtha tvāt para artha sampadam āha tattvam jīva ādayaḥ padārthāḥ pramāṇa pratiṣṭhita tvāt teṣām upadeśaḥ svarūpa prakāśanam tad rakṣaṇa ādi vidhānam vā tam karoti tattva upadeśa kṛt atas eva sārvam sarvasmai hitam prāṇirakṣaṇa upāya upadeśa parama pada dāyitayā viśva janīna tvāt etena para artha sampādaka tvam uktam adhunā pareṣām eva anartha vighāti tvam āha kutsitāḥ panthāḥ kāpathāḥ tīrtha antarāṇi teṣām ghaṭṭanam vicālakam nirākārakam sarva jana apakāri kumata vidhvaṃsakam iti arthaḥ īdṛśāt eva śāstrāt jātam śābdam pramāṇam na anyebhyaḥ vipralambhaka tvāt teṣām iti 
NA_10.0–10.1	 adhunā para artha anumāna lakṣaṇam vaktavyam tat ca pratyakṣe api paśyan eka yogakṣema tvāt sāmānyena āha sva niścaya vat anyeṣām niścaya utpādanam budhaiḥ para artham mānam ākhyātam vākyam tat upacārataḥ atra para artham mānam iti lakṣyam sva niścaya vat ityādi lakṣaṇam sve ātmā tasya niścayaḥ prameya adhigamaḥ tadvat anyeśām pratipādyānām niścaya utpādanam prameya paricchedaka jñāna prādurbhāvanam yathā ātmanaḥ artha nirṇayaḥ tathā pareṣām nirṇaya jananam iti arthaḥ budhaiḥ vidvadbhiḥ parasmai arthaḥ prayojanam yena tat para artham mīyate anena iti mānam ākhyātam kathitam 
NA_10.2	 nanu ca yadi niścaya utpādanam parārtha mānam tathā jñānam api para pratyāyanāya vyāpriyamānam para artham prāpnoti iti āha vākyam para artham na jñānam tasya aiva ānantaryeṇa vyāpārāt para prayojana mātra tvāt ca itarasya tu vyavahita tvāt sva para upakāri tvāt ca katham vacanam ajñāna rūpam pramāṇam iti āha tad upacārataḥ tasya jñānasya upacāraḥ atad rūpasya api tad aṅga tayā tad rūpa tvena grahaṇam tatas idam uktam bhavati pratipādya gatam utpatsyamānam yat jñānam tat avyavahita kāraṇa tvāt vacanam api upacāreṇa pramāṇam iti ucyate tatra anumānasya pārārthyam paraiḥ abhyupagatam eva pratyakṣasya na pratipadyante kila idam śabda praveśa śūnya sva lakṣaṇa grāhī iti nāitat gocaraḥ parebhyaḥ pratipādayitum pāryate na ca śabdāt parasya sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa dakṣam pratyakṣam unmaṅkṣyati śabdasya vikalpa utpādita tvena parasya api vikalpa utpādaka tvāt tat uktam vikalpa yonayaḥ śabdāḥ vikalpāḥ śabda yonayaḥ kārya kāraṇa tā teṣām na artham śabdāḥ spṛśanti api 
NA_11.0–11.1^1	 nirvikalpakam ca pratyakṣam atas na śabda janyam iti atas anumānam dṛṣṭāntīkṛtya pratyakṣasya api para artha tām sādhayitum āha pratyakṣeṇa anumānena prasiddha artha prakāśanāt parasya tad upāya tvāt parārtha tvam dvayoḥ api pratyakṣeṇa api anumānena iva prasiddha artha prakāśanāt sva pratīta prameya pratyāyaka tvāt parārtha tvam pratipādya prayojana tvam dvayoḥ api pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ tulya kāraṇa tvān na anumānasya aivāikasya iti abhiprāyaḥ iha ca aśrūyamāṇa tvāt tad artha gamanāt ca api iva śabdau lupta nirdiṣṭau draṣṭavyau pratyakṣa pratīta artha pratyāyanam ca pratijānānasya ayam abhiprāyaḥ yat paraḥ manyate nāi tat gocaram parebhyaḥ pratipādayitum pāryate iti tat ayuktam nirvikalpaka adhyakṣa apohena vyavasāya rūpasya pratyakṣasya prāk eva sādhita tvāt tad gocarasya kathañcid vikalpa gamya tvena śabda pratipādya tvāt tat yathā anumāna pratītaḥ arthaḥ parasmai pratipādyamānaḥ vacana rūpa āpannaḥ para artham anumānam tathā pratyakṣa pratītaḥ api para artham pratyakṣam para pratyāyanasya tulya tvāt vacana vyāpārasya aiva bhedāt 
NA_11.1^2	 tathā hi anumāna pratītam pratyāyayan evam vacanayati agniḥ atra dhūmāt yatra yatra dhūmaḥ tatra tatra agniḥ yathā mahānasa ādau vaidharmyeṇa vā agnyabhāve na kvacid dhūmaḥ yathā jalāśaya ādau tathā ca dhūmaḥ ayam tasmāt dhūmāt agniḥ atra iti avyutpanna vismṛta sambandhayoḥ tathā aiva pratipādayitum śakya tvāt smaryamāṇe sambandhe punar evam agniḥ atra dhūma upapatteḥ vaidharmyeṇa agniḥ atra anyathā dhūma anupapatteḥ pratyakṣa pratītam punar darśayan etāvat vakti paśya rāja gacchati tatas ca vacanāt dvividhāt api samagra sāmagrīkasya pratipādyasya anumeya pratyakṣa artha viṣayā yatas pratītiḥ ullasati atas dvayoḥ api parārtha ta iti āha parasya tad upāya tvāt pratipādyasya pratītim prati pratipādaka stha pratyakṣa anumāna nirṇīta artha prakāśana kāraṇa tvāt iti arthaḥ etena pūrva kārikā ukta upacāra kāraṇam ca lakṣayati 
NA_11.2	 yat ca uktam na śabdāt parasya pratyakṣa utpattiḥ tasya vikalpa janaka tvāt pratyakṣasya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvena nirvikalpaka tvāt  tat ayuktam sāmānya viśeṣa ātmaka artha viṣayasya nirṇaya rūpasya tasya kathañcid eka viṣaya tayā śabda utpādya tva avirodhāt evaṃvidhasya ca prāk eva samarthanāt cakṣuḥ ādi sāmagrītaḥ tat utpadyate na śabdāt iti ced anumānam api pratyakṣa ādi niścitāt dhetoḥ avismṛta sambandhasya pramātuḥ ullasati na śabdāt atas tasya api parārtha tā viśīryeta samartha hetu kathanāt tatra vacanasya parārtha ta iti ced atra api darśana yogya artha pratipādanāt iti brūmaḥ tat na pratyakṣa parokṣayoḥ pārārthyam prati viśeṣa upalabdhiḥ iti mucyatām pakṣapātaḥ 
NA_12.0–12.1	 tat evam dvayoḥ api para artha tām pratipādya tad svarūpam āha pratyakṣa pratipanna artha pratipādi ca yat vacaḥ pratyakṣam pratibhāsasya nimitta tvāt tat ucyate yat vacaḥ pratyakṣa pratipanna artha pratipādi sākṣātkāri jñāna gocara kathana caturam tat pratyakṣam ucyate iti sambandhaḥ tat ca pratyakṣa rūpam eva ucyamānam pratyakṣam vipratipannam prati punar anumāna dvāreṇa ucyamānam anumānam eva iti caśabdena aneka artha tvāt darśayati vacanam kutas pratyakṣam iti āha pratibhāsasya nimitta tvāt pratipādya pratyakṣa prakāśa hetu tvāt upacāreṇa ucyate iti arthaḥ 
NA_13.0–13.1	 anumānam āha sādhyāvinābhuvaḥ hetoḥ vacaḥ yat pratipādakam para artham anumānam tat pakṣa ādi vacana ātmakam hinoti gamayati artham iti hetuḥ tasya sādhyāvinābhuvaḥ prāk nirūpitasya yat vacaḥ pratipādakam sandarśakam tat anumāna prakāśa hetu tvāt para artham anumānam tat kīdṛśam iti āha pakṣaḥ vakṣyamāṇa lakṣaṇaḥ saḥ ādiḥ yeṣām hetu dṛṣṭānta upanaya nigamana ādīnām tāni tathā teṣām vacanāni pratipādakāḥ dhvanayaḥ tāni eva ātmā svarūpam yasya tat pakṣa ādi vacana ātmakam 
NA_13.2^1	 nanu ca hetu pratipādakam vacaḥ para artham anumānam iti abhidhāya tat pakṣa ādi vacana ātmakam iti vadataḥ pūrva apara vyāhatā vācaḥ yuktiḥ nāitat asti evam manyate nāikaḥ prakāraḥ para artha anumānasya kim tarhi yathā parasya sukhena prameya pratītiḥ bhavati tathā yatnatas pratyāyanīyaḥ tatra daśa avayavam sādhanam pratipādana upāyaḥ tat yathā pakṣa ādayaḥ pañca tad śuddhayaḥ ca tatra yadā pratipādyaḥ prakramāt eva nirṇīta pakṣaḥ avismṛta dṛṣṭānta smārya pratibandha grāhaka pramāṇaḥ vyutpannam ati tvāt śeṣa avayava abhyūhana samarthaḥ ca bhavati yat vā atyanta abhyāsena parikarmitam ati tvāt tāvatā iva prastuta prameyam avabudhyate tadā hetu pratipādanam eva kriyate śeṣa abhidhānasya śrotṛ saṃskāra ākāri tayā nairarthakyāt ityādau hetu pratipādanam sūtra kṛtā para artham anumānam uktam 
NA_13.2^2	 yadā tu pratipādyasya na adya api pakṣa nirṇayaḥ tadākāṇḍaḥ eva hetu upanyāsaḥ adṛṣṭa mudgara pātāyamānaḥ syāt iti pakṣaḥ api nirdiśyate tathā asmaryamāṇe pratibandha grāhiṇi pramāṇe dṛṣṭāntaḥ api varṇī eta anyathā hetoḥ sāmarthya anavagateḥ smṛte api pramāṇe dārṣṭa antike yojayitum ajānānasya upanayaḥ darśyate tathā api sa ākāṅkṣasya nigamanam ucyate anyathā nirākula prastuta artha asiddheḥ tathā yatra pakṣa ādau sva rūpa vipratipattiḥ tatra tad śuddhiḥ pramāṇena kartavyā itarathā teṣām sva sādhya asādhanāt sarveṣām ca amīṣām sādhana avayava tvam pratipādya prati iti upāya tvāt 
NA_13.3	 nanu ca sva niścaya vat para niścaya utpādanam para artham anumānam uktam na ca sva artha anumāna kāle kramaḥ ayam anubhūyate sambandha vedinaḥ hetu darśana mātrāt sādhya pratīti siddheḥ na hi pratipattā pakṣam kṛtvā tatas hetum nibhālayati na api dṛṣṭānta ādikam viracayati tathā pratīteḥ abhāvāt kim ca anvaya vyatirekābhyām hetoḥ eva sāmarthyam unnīyate na pakṣa ādīnām tad vyatirekeṇa api sādhya siddheḥ tathā api teṣām sādhana aṃśa tva kalpane anavasthā prasaṅgāt yadi ca tad sāmarthyam syāt tadā pakṣa upanyāsa mātrāt eva sādhya avagateḥ hetuḥ ānarthakyam aśnuvīta uttara avayavāḥ ca evam hi tad sāmarthyam siddhyet na anyathā tasmāt yaḥ eva para nirapekṣam sādhyam bodhayati saḥ eva hetuḥ sādhanam na pakṣa ādayaḥ iti
