NA_13.4^1	 atra ucyate sva niścaya vat para niścaya utpādanam para artham anumānam uktam ityādi yat uktam tat yuktam uktam kevalam tad artham na jānīṣe niścaya apekṣayā aiva vatinā tulya tā abhidhānān na punar sarva sāmānyam abhipretam anyathā dhvanim anuccārayan sva artha anumāne sādhyam avabudhyate iti tad anuccāraṇena para niścaya utpādanam prasajyeta na ca āitat asti śabdān uccāraṇe para pratipādana asambhavāt tad artham śabda aṅgīkaraṇe yena yena vinā para pratipādana āsambhavaḥ tat tat urarīkartavyam samāna nyāyāt na ca pakṣa ādi virahe pratipādya viśeṣaḥ pratipādayitum śakyaḥ hetu gocara ādi tad sādhya artha pratīti vikala tayā tasya sa ākāṅkṣa tvāt tathā ca bubhutsita artha bodha abhāvāt apratyāyitaḥ eva tiṣṭhet atas tad bodhana artham pakṣa ādayaḥ darśanīyāḥ iti te api sādhana aṃśāḥ syuḥ yat ca uktam anvaya vyatireka anukaraṇa abhāvāt na sādhanam hetu mātrāt api sādhya siddheḥ tat ayuktam avipratāraka tā niścita puruṣa vacana mātrāt api agniḥ atra ityādi rūpāt kvacid prameyaḥ arthaḥ sidhyati iti hetoḥ api asādhana tā prasaṅgāt 
NA_13.4^2	 tad viraheṇa api sādhya siddheḥ yuktam ca āitat avipratāraka vacanasya prāk eva prāmāṇya prasādhanāt yat ca uktam yadi amīṣām sāmarthyam syāt tadā pakṣa mātrāt eva sādhya pratīteḥ hetoḥ vaiyarthyam syāt iti tat ayuktataram bhavat pakṣe api samāna tvāt tatra api samartha hetu upanyāsāt eva sādhya avagateḥ anyathā samartha tā yogāt paścāt tasya aiva pramāṇena samarthanam sarvatra gṛhīta vyāptikasya ca punar pakṣa dharmiṇī upasaṃharaṇam anarthaka tām prāpnuvat kena nivāryeta tad abhāve hetoḥ sāmarthyam na avagamyate tena sārthakam iti ced pakṣa ādīn api virahayya pratipādya viśeṣaḥ pratipādayitum na pāryate iti teṣām api sārthaka tā na durupapāda iti mucyatām āgrahaḥ tasmāt dhetu vat pakṣa ādayaḥ api sādhanam hetoḥ api kvacid pratipādye tad apekṣa tayā nirapekṣatā siddheḥ iti tat idam sakalam ākalayya uktam tat pakṣa ādi vacana ātmakam iti 
NA_14.0–14.1^1	 tat evam arthataḥ pakṣa ādīn prastutya tāvat pakṣa lakṣaṇam āha sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣaḥ pratyakṣa ādi a nirākṛtaḥ tad prayogaḥ atra kartavyaḥ hetoḥ gocara dīpakaḥ pacyate iti pakṣaḥ vyaktīkriyate itibhāvaḥ kiṃbhūtaḥ iti āha sādhyasya anumeyasya abhyupagamaḥ aṅgīkaraṇam prāśnika ādīnām puratas pratijñāsvīkāraḥ iti arthaḥ kim abhyupagama mātram na iti āha pratyakṣa ādi a nirākṛtaḥ iti pratyakṣam sākṣātkāri saṃvedanam ādi śabdāt anumāna sva vacana lokāḥ gṛhyante taiḥ anirākṛtaḥ abādhitaḥ pakṣaḥ iti sambandhaḥ tat yathā sarvam anekānta ātmakam asti sarvajña ityādi vā 
NA_14.0–14.1^2	 ayam ca kevalam eṣṭavyaḥ na punar para artha anumāna kāle vacanena abhidhātavyaḥ iti yaḥ manyeta tam pratyāha tasya pakṣasya prayogaḥ abhidhānam atra para artha anumāna prastāve kartavyaḥ vidheyaḥ kutas iti āha hetoḥ prāc nirūpitasya gocara dīpakaḥ iti nimitta kāraṇa hetuṣu sarvāsām prāyas darśanam iti vacanāt bhāva pradhāna tvāt ca nirdeśasya viṣaya sandarśaka tvāt iti arthaḥ ayam atra abhiprāyaḥ na hi sarvatra prativādinaḥ prakramāt eva nirṇīta pakṣasya kūrca śobhā puraḥsaram hetuḥ upanyasyate api tu kvacid kathañcid 
NA_15.0–15.1	 tatas yadā adya api pratipādyaḥ pakṣa artham na jānīte tadākāṇḍaḥ eva hetau ucyamāne viṣaya vyāmohāt bhrānti lakṣaṇaḥ doṣaḥ syāt iti āha anyathā vādi abhipreta hetu gocara mohinaḥ pratyāyyasya bhavet dhetuḥ viruddha arekitaḥ yathā anyathā iti ukta viparīta āśrayaṇe pakṣa prayoga akaraṇaḥ iti arthaḥ vādinaḥ hetu upanyāsa kartuḥ abhipretaḥ abhimataḥ sa ca asau hetu gocaraḥ ca vādi abhipreta hetu gocaraḥ tatra muhyati dolāyate tat śīlaḥ ca yaḥ tasya pratyāyyasya prativādinaḥ hetuḥ viruddha arekitaḥ bhavet virodha śaṅkā kalaṅkitaḥ syāt iti arthaḥ tatas ca samyak hetau api vipakṣaḥ eva ayam vartata iti vyāmohāt viruddha dūṣaṇam abhidadhīta pakṣa upanyāsāt tu nirṇīta hetu gocarasya nāiṣa doṣaḥ syāt iti abhiprāyaḥ amum eva artham spaṣṭa dṛṣṭāntena āha yathā iti tad upanyāsa arthaḥ dhānuṣka guṇa samprekṣi janasya parividhyataḥ dhānuṣkasya vinā lakṣya nirdeśena guṇa itarau 
NA_16.1	 yathā lakṣya nirdeśam vinā dhānuṣkasya iṣum prakṣipataḥ yau guṇa doṣau tau tad darśi janasya viparyastau api pratibhātaḥ guṇaḥ api doṣa tayā doṣaḥ api vā guṇa tayā tathā pakṣa nirdeśam vinā hetum upanyasyataḥ vādinaḥ yau sva abhipreta sādhya sādhana samartha tva asamartha tva lakṣaṇau guṇa doṣau tau prāśnika prativādya ādīnām viparītau api pratibhātaḥ iti bhāva arthaḥ akṣara arthaḥ tu dhanuṣā carati dhānuṣkaḥ tasya guṇaḥ lakṣya vedha prāvīṇya lakṣaṇaḥ tatra prekṣakāṇām kutūhalam iti tasya aiva upādānam anyathā doṣaḥ api draṣṭavyaḥ tad samprekṣi janasya tad samprekṣaṇa śīla lokasya parividhyataḥ yathā kathañcid bāṇam muñcate iti arthaḥ dhanuṣkasya vinā lakṣya nirdeśena cāpa dharasya vedhya niṣṭaṅkanam ṛte yau guṇa itarau guṇa doṣau tau yathā viruddha arekitau bhavataḥ tathā vādinaḥ api iti arthaḥ tasmāt avijñāta tad arthe prativādini vādidhā anuṣkeṇa pakṣa lakṣyam nirdiśya aiva hetu śaraḥ proktavyaḥ iti sthitam 
NA_17.0	 sāmpratam hetoḥ lakṣaṇa avasaraḥ tat ca sva artha anumāna vat nirviśeṣam draṣṭavyam prayogaḥ tu tatra na darśitaḥ sva artha anumānasya bodha rūpa tvāt iha tu darśanīyaḥ para artha anumānasya vacana rūpa tvāt atas tam darśayati hetoḥ tathā upapattyā vā syāt prayogaḥ anyathā api vā dvividhaḥ anyatareṇa api sādhya siddhiḥ bhavet iti 
NA_17.1^1	 sva artha anumāna prastāve hi para praṇīta lakṣaṇa antara vyapohena sādhya vyatirekāt sāmastyena hetoḥ vyāvṛttiḥ evāikam lakṣaṇam iti nirṇītam para artha anumāne api tat eva prakāśanīyam vacana racanā tu kvacid kathañcid pravartate iti abhiprāyavān tat dvaividhyam āha hetoḥ dvividhaḥ prayogaḥ syāt iti sambandhaḥ katham iti āha tathā aiva sādhya sadbhāvaḥ eva upapattiḥ vidyamāna tā tayā tathā upapattyā yathā agniḥ atra dhūmasya tathā aiva upapatteḥ iti anyathā api vā iti anena avayave samudāya upacārāt anyathā anupapattim lakṣayati 
NA_17.1^2	 anyathā sādhya vyatireke anupapattiḥ avidyam āna tauiva tayā vā anyathā anupapattyā hetoḥ prayogaḥ syāt yathā agniḥ atra dhūmasya anyathā anupapatteḥ iti ete ca dve api ekasmin sādhye prayoktavye iti yaḥ manyeta tad śiṣyaṇa artham āha anyatareṇa api tathā upapatti prayogeṇa anyathā anupapatti prayogeṇa vā sādhyasya pratipipādayiṣita arthasya siddhiḥ niṣpattiḥ pratipādya pratītau ārohaṇam bhavet iti yasmāt tasmāt na dve api prayoktavye prayoga dvaye api yasmāt vacana racanā bhidyate na arthaḥ prayogasya ca sādhya sādhanam phalam tat ced ekena aiva sidhyati dvitīya prayogaḥ kevalam vaktuḥ akauśalam ācakṣīta nairarthakyāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
NA_18.0–18.1^1	 adhunā dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇa avasaraḥ sa ca dvedhā sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca tatra sādharmya dṛṣṭāntam adhikṛtya āha sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāptiḥ yatra niścīyata itarām sādharmyeṇa sa dṛṣṭāntaḥ sambandha smaraṇāt mataḥ dṛṣṭayoḥ avalokitayoḥ sāmarthyāt sādhya sādhanayoḥ antar pariniṣṭhitiḥ anvayāt vyatirekāt vā sādhya sādhana bhāva vyavasthiti nibandhanā asmin iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ samānaḥ dharmaḥ asya iti sadharmā tad bhāvaḥ sādharmyam tena sādharmyeṇa sa kiṃvidhaḥ bhavati iti āha sādhyam jijñāsita artha ātmakam sādhanam tad gamakaḥ hetuḥ tayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ vyāptiḥ idam anena vinā na bhavati iti evaṃrūpā yatra kvacid niścīyata itarām atiśayena nirṇīyate sa sādharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā agniḥ atra dhūmasya tathā aiva upapatteḥ mahānasa ādi vat iti 
NA_18.1^2	 ayam ca avismṛta pratibandhe prativādini na prayoktavyaḥ iti āha sambandha smaraṇāt iti lya blope pañcamī prāk gṛhīta vismṛta sambandha smaraṇam adhikṛtya mataḥ abhipretaḥ ayam nīti vidām na anyadā yadā hi pratipādyaḥ adya api sambandham sādhya avinābhau= i tva lakṣaṇam na avabudhyate tadā pramāṇena sambandham grāhaṇīyaḥ na dṛṣṭānta mātreṇa na hi saha darśanāt eva kvacid sarvatra idam amunā vinā na bhavati iti sidhyati atiprasaṅgāt gṛhīte ca pratibandhe smaryamāṇe kevalam hetuḥ darśanīyaḥ tāvatā iva bubhutsita artha siddheḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ na vācyaḥ vaiyarthyāt yadā tu gṛhītaḥ api vismṛtaḥ kathañcid sambandhaḥ tadā tad smaraṇa artham dṛṣṭāntaḥ kathyate 
NA_18.2^1	 nanu ca katham tri kāla samasta deśa vyāpi sambandha avagatiḥ na tāvat nirṇaya ātmakam api pratyakṣam deśa kāla antara saṃcariṣṇunoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ sambandham nirīkṣitum kṣamate sannihite arthe viśada adhyavasāyena pravṛtteḥ na api śabdāt tat nirṇayaḥ tasya para upadeśa rūpa tayā sva artha anumāna abhāva prasaṅgāt tatra para upadeśa abhāvāt tad abhāve sambandha asiddeḥ tat asiddhau anumāna anutthānāt iti anumānāt sambandha grahaṇe niravadhiḥ anavasthā anuṣa jyeta sambandha grāhiṇaḥ api anumānasya punar sambandha antara grahaṇa savyapekṣa tvāt iti 
NA_18.2^2	 atra ucyate pratyakṣa anumāne dve eva pramāṇe iti yeṣām mithyā abhiniveśaḥ teṣām eṣa doṣaḥ na asmākam anvaya vyatireka grāhi pratyakṣa anupalambha uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ avyabhicarita tri kāla vyāpi gocarasya mati nibandhanasya ūha saṃjñitasya pramāṇa antarasya sambandha grāhitayā iṣṭa tvāt tad aniṣṭau dṛṣṭa vyavahāra vilopa prasaṅgāt tad vilope ca vicāra anarthakya prāpteḥ iti atra prakaraṇe punar anumānāt pārthakyena ūhaḥ na darśitaḥ saṅkṣipta ruci sattva anugraha pravṛtta tvāt asya śābdam tu pṛthak samarthitam tasya atra aiva para artha anumāna upayogi tvāt iti āstām tāvat 
NA_19.0–19.1	 idānīm vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntam upadarśayan āha sādhye nivartamāne tu sādhanasya api asambhavaḥ khyāpyate yatra dṛṣṭānte vaidharmyeṇa iti sa smṛtaḥ visadṛśaḥ dharmaḥ asya iti vidharmā tad bhāvaḥ vaidharmyam tena vaidharmyeṇa dṛṣṭāntaḥ kīdṛśaḥ iti āha sādhye gamye nivartamāne asambhavati tuśabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ bhinnakramaḥ sa ca sādhanasya api gamakasya api asambhavaḥ eva iti atra draṣṭavyaḥ khyāpyate pratipādyate yatra kvacid dṛṣṭānte sa vaidharmyeṇa bhavati iti śabdena sambandha smaraṇāt iti 
NA_20.0–20.1^1	 idam atra api sambadhnāti asya api smaryamāṇe sambandhe prayoga ayogāt iti kim artham vismṛta sambandhaḥ eva prativādini dṛṣṭāntaḥ prayujyate na anyat ā iti para vacana avakāśam āśaṅkya āha antar vyāptyā aiva sādhyasya siddheḥ bahis udāhṛtiḥ vyarthā syāt tad asadbhāve api evam nyāya vidaḥ viduḥ anyadāhi smaryamāṇe vā sambandhe prayujyeta agṛhīte vā yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ saḥ ayuktaḥ yadā sarvatra sādhya avinābhāvinam hetum smarati pratipādyaḥ tadā pakṣe api tam avabudhya katham sādhyam na pratipadyeta tatas ca antar pakṣa madhye vyāptiḥ sādhanasya sa adhya ākrānta tvam antar vyāptiḥ tayā aiva sādhyasya gamyasya siddheḥ pratīteḥ bahis vivakṣita dharmiṇaḥ a nyatra dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī udāhṛtiḥ vyāpti darśana rūpā vyarthāḥ niṣprayojanā tad pratyāyya artha abhāvāt iti dvitīya pakṣasya api nirdoṣa tām nirasyan āha tad asadbhāve api evam sambandha agrahaṇāt antar vyāpti abhāve api evam iti vyartha aiva bahis udāhṛtiḥ na hi saha darśanāt kvacid sarvatra tad rūpa tā sidhyati vyabhicāra darśanāt 
NA_20.1^2	 tasmāt agṛhīta sambandhe pratipādye pramāṇena pratibandhaḥ sādhyaḥ tad siddhau tatas eva sādhya siddheḥ akiñcitkarī dṛṣṭānta udāhṛtiḥ iti nyāya vidaḥ nyāya vidvāṃsaḥ viduḥ avabudhyante iti iha ca prakaraṇe śeṣa avayavānām upanaya nigamana śuddhi pañcaka lakṣaṇānām saṅkṣipta ruci sattva anugraha para tvāt asya yadi api sākṣāt lakṣaṇam na uktam tathā api atas eva pratipādita avayava trayāt buddhimadbhiḥ unneyam yatas avayava apekṣayā jaghanya madhyama utkṛṣṭāḥ tisraḥ kathāḥ bhavanti tatra hetu pratipādana mātram jaghanyā dvi ādi a vayava nivedanam madhyamā sampūrṇa daśa avayava kathanam utkṛṣṭāḥ tatra iha madhyamāyāḥ sākṣāt kathanena jaghanya utkṛṣṭe arthataḥ sūcayati tad sadbhāvasya pramāṇa siddha tvāt iti 
NA_21.0–21.1	 evam pakṣa ādi lakṣaṇam pratipādya idānīm heya jñāne sati upādeyam viviktataram vedyate iti tad vyudaḥ tāḥ pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ vaktavyāḥ tatra tāvat pakṣa lakṣaṇa vyudaḥ tān pakṣa ābhāsān āha pratipādyasya yaḥ siddhaḥ pakṣa ābhāsaḥ akṣa liṅgataḥ loka sva vacanābhyām ca bādhitaḥ anekadhā mataḥ pakṣa sthāna upanyasta tvāt tad kārya akaraṇa tvāt ca pakṣa vat ābhāsate iti pakṣa ābhāsaḥ asau anekadhā aneka prakāraḥ mataḥ iti sambandhaḥ katham iti āha pratipādyasya prativādinaḥ yaḥ kaścid siddhaḥ pratītau ārūḍhaḥ eva sa pakṣa ābhāsaḥ sādhyasya aiva pakṣa tvāt siddhasya sādhana anarha tvāt ati prasakteḥ tathā akṣaliṅgataḥ adhyakṣa hetubhyām loka sva vacanābhyām ca bādhitaḥ tiraskṛtaḥ yaḥ sa pakṣa ābhāsaḥ tatra pratipādya siddhaḥ yathā paudgalikaḥ ghaṭaḥ saugatam vā prati sarvam kṣaṇikam ityādi pratyakṣa bādhitaḥ yathā niraṃśāni sva lakṣaṇāni paraspara viviktau vā sāmānya viśeṣau iti anumāna bādhitaḥ yathā na asti sarvajñaḥ iti loka bādhitaḥ yathā gamyāḥ mātā iti sva vacana bādhitaḥ yathā na santi sarve bhāvāḥ iti 
NA_22.0–22.1	 sāmpratam hetu lakṣaṇam smārayan tad apāstān hetvābhāsān āha anyathā anupapanna tvam hetoḥ lakṣaṇam īritam tad apratīti sandeha viparyāsaiḥ tad ābhatā hetoḥ lakṣaṇam asādhāraṇa dharma rūpam yat īritam gamitam aneka artha tvāt vā pratipāditam sva artha anumāna prastāve yat uta anyathā anupapanna tvam iti tasya apratītiḥ anadhyavasāyaḥ sandehaḥ dolāyamāna tā viparyāsaḥ vaiparīti anirṇayaḥ apratītiḥ ca sandehaḥ ca viparyāsaḥ ca iti dvandvaḥ paścāt tadā saha tatpuruṣaḥ taiḥ tad apratīti sandeha viparyāsaiḥ tad ābhatāa ābhānam ābhā tasya iva samyak hetoḥ iva ābhāsya iti tad ābhaḥ tad bhāvaḥ tat tāḥ hetvābhāsa tā bhavati iti arthaḥ 
NA_23.0–23.1	 adhunā yena lakṣaṇena yat nāmā hetvābhāsaḥ bhavati tat darśayati asiddhaḥ tu apratītaḥ yaḥ yaḥ anyathā aiva upapadyate viruddhaḥ yaḥ anyathā api atra yuktaḥ anaikāntikaḥ sa tu yaḥ kaścid apratītaḥ pratītyai agocarīkṛtaḥ aniścitaḥ saḥ asiddha nāmā hetvābhāsaḥ tuśabdaḥ trayasya api bheda uddyotakaḥ yaḥ tu anyathā aiva sādhyam vinā aiva vipakṣaḥ eva iti yāvat upapadyate sambhavati sa viruddha abhidhānaḥ yaḥ punar anyathā api sādhya viparyayeṇa api yuktaḥ ghaṭamānakaḥ api śabdāt sādhyena api saḥ atra vyatikare anaikāntika saṃjñaḥ jñātavyaḥ iti tatra pratiprāṇi prasiddha pramāṇa pratiṣṭhita anekānta viruddha buddhibhiḥ kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda buddha ādi śiṣyakaiḥ upanyasyamānāḥ sarve eva hetavaḥ tat yathāikāntena anityaḥ śabdaḥ nityaḥ vā sattvāt utpattimat tvāt kṛtaka tvāt pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt ityādayaḥ vivakṣayā asiddha viruddha anaikāntika tām svīkurvanti iti avagantavyam 
NA_23.2^1	 tathā hi anityāikā ante tāvat asiddhāḥ sarve eva hetavaḥ cākṣuṣa tva vat teṣām dhvanau avidyamāna tvāt asat ādi vyavacchedena alīka saṃvṛti vikalpita tvāt pāramārthika tve tu ekasya aneka rūpa āpattyā anekāntavāda āpatteḥ kalpanā racita sattākānām ca sarva śakti viraha rūpa tayā niḥsvabhāva tvāt tathā api teṣām sādhana tve sādhyam api niḥsvabhāvam iti khara viṣāṇam śaśa viṣāṇasya sādhanam āpadyate iti śobhanaḥ sādhya sa dhana vyavahāraḥ sarve eva ayam anumāna anumeya vyavahāraḥ buddhi ārūḍhena dharma dharmi nyāyena na bahis sat asat tvam apekṣate tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced evam tarhi cākṣuṣa tvam api śabde buddhyā adhyāropya hetutayā ucyamānam na asiddhatayā udbhāvanīyam viśeṣa abhāvāt 
NA_23.2^2	 acākṣuṣa tva vyavacchedena cākṣuṣa tvam buddhyā adhyāropayituṃpāryate na yathā kathañcin na ca asau śabde asti acakṣuḥ grāhya tvāt tasya tena ayam adoṣaḥ iti ced kaḥ ayam acākṣuṣa tva vyavacchedaḥ nāma vyavaccheda mātram nīrūpam vyavacchinnam vā sva lakṣaṇam vyavacchedikā vā buddhiḥ sva aṃśam agnā api bahis vastu grahaṇa rūpa tayā plavamānāḥ na aparaḥ vastu dharmaḥ yatra bheda abheda vikalpa dvāreṇā dūṣaṇam ditsuḥ bhavān iti ced tarhi sa śabde na asti iti kāiṣā bhāṣā evam hi nabhaḥ puṇḍarīkam tatra na asti iti sattva ādikam api kalpayitum na śakyam iti prasajyeta kim ca te sādhana dharmāḥ dharmiṇi bhavantaḥ api na bhavat darśane pratītim ārohanti pratyakṣasya vikalpa vikala tayā dharma nirṇaya śūnya tvāt tad uttara kāla bhāvinyā vāsanā prabodha janyāyāḥ vikalpa buddheḥ sva aṃśa grahaṇa paryavasita śarīra tvena bahis sva lakṣaṇe praveśa abhāvāt tatas ca apratīta tvāt sarvasya asiddha tvam 
NA_23.3–23.5	 nityāikā ante api dharmiṇaḥ atyanta vyatiriktānām apāramārthikānām vā sva sādhana dharmāṇām pramāṇena apratīta tvāt asiddha tā draṣṭavyā dharmiṇaḥ avinirluṭhita rūpāṇām pāramārthikānām sakala dharmāṇām pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa prasiddha tvena nihnotum aśakya tvāt iti tathā viruddha tā api pakṣa dvaye api sarva sādhana dharmāṇām unneyān ekānta pratibaddha svabhāva tvena tad sādhana pravaṇa tvāt etat ca uttaratra vakṣyāmaḥ evam pakṣa dvaye api nirdiśyamānāḥ sarve eva hetavaḥ anaikāntika tām ātmasāt kurvanti paraspara viruddha avyabhicāri tvāt samāna yukti upanyāsena vipakṣe api darśayitum śakya tvāt 
NA_23.6^1	 tathā hi anitya vādī nitya vādinam prati pramāṇayati sarvam kṣaṇikam sattvāt akṣaṇike krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhāt artha kriyā kāritvasya ca bhāva lakṣaṇa tvāt tatas artha kriyā vyāvartamānā sva kroḍīkṛtām sattām vyāvartayet iti kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ na hi nityaḥ arthaḥ artha kriyāyām krameṇa pravartitum utsahate pūrva artha kriyā karaṇa svabhāva upamarda dvāreṇa uttara kriyāyām pravṛtteḥ anyathā pūrva artha kriyā karaṇa avirāma prasaṅgāt tad svabhāva pracyave ca nitya tāpayāti atādavasthyasya anitya lakṣaṇa tvāt 
NA_23.6^2	 nityaḥ api krama vartinam sahakāri kāraṇam artham udīkṣamāṇaḥ tāvat asīt paścāt tam āsādya krameṇa kāryam kuryāt iti ced na sahakāri kāraṇasya nitye akiñcitkara tvāt akiñcitkarasya api pratīkṣaṇe anavasthā prasaṅgāt na api yaugapadyena nityaḥ arthaḥ artha kriyām kurute adhyakṣa virodhāt na hi eka kālam sakalāḥ kriyāḥ prārabhamāṇaḥ kaścid upalabhate karotu vā tathā api ādi akṣaṇaḥ eva sakala kriyā parisamāpteḥ dvitīya ādi kṣaṇeṣu akurvāṇasya anitya tā balāt āḍhaukate karaṇa akaraṇayoḥ ekasmin viruddha tvāt iti 
NA_23.7	 nitya vādī punar evam pramāṇayati sarvam nityam sattvāt kṣaṇike sat asat kālayoḥ artha kriyā virodhāt tad lakṣaṇam sattvam na avasthām badhnāti iti tatas nivartamānam ananya śaraṇa tayā nitya tvam sādhayati tathā hi kṣaṇikaḥ arthaḥ sat vā kāryam kuryāt asat vā gati antara abhāvāt na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sama samaya vartini vyāpāra ayogāt sakala bhāvānām parasparam kārya kāraṇa bhāva prāptyā atiprasaṅgāt ca na api dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ kṣodam kṣamate asataḥ kārya karaṇa śakti vikala tvāt anyathā śaśaviṣāṇa ādayaḥ api kārya karaṇāya utsaheran viśeṣa abhāvāt iti 
NA_23.8	 tat evam ekānta dvaye api ye ye hetavaḥ te te yukteḥ samāna tayā viruddham na vyabhicaranti avicārita ramaṇīya tayā mugdha jana dhyāndhyam ca utpādayanti iti virudha avi abhicāriṇaḥ anaikāntikāḥ sarva vastu dharmāṇām vastutas anekānta pratibaddha tvāt iti tasmāt amī sarve eva hetavaḥ santaḥ aneka antam antareṇa na upapadyante iti tam eva pratipādayitum īśate vimūḍha buddhibhiḥ punar vipakṣa sādhana artham upanyasyamānā vivakṣaya asiddha viruddha anaikāntika tām ābibhrati iti sthitam 
NA_24.0–24.1	 tat evam hetvābhāsān pratipādya dṛṣtānta lakṣaṇa vyudaḥ tān dṛṣṭānta ābhāsān āha sādharmyeṇa atra dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ nyāya vidīritāḥ apalakṣaṇa hetu utthāḥ sādhya ādi vikala ādayaḥ sādhanam sādhya ākrāntam upadarśayitum abhipretam yasmin tat sādharmyam tena atra vyatikare dūṣyante iti doṣāḥ dṛṣṭāntāḥ eva doṣāḥ dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ iti arthaḥ nyāya vidīritāḥ vidvadbhiḥ gaditāḥ sādhyam gamyam ādi śabdāt sādhana ubhaya parigrahaḥ tad vikalāḥ tat śūnyāḥ ādi śabdāt sandigdha sādhya sādhana ubhaya dharmāḥ gṛhyante kiṃbhūtā ete iti āha apagatam lakṣaṇam yebhyaḥ te tathā te ca te hetavaḥ tebhyaḥ utthāḥ utthānam yeṣām te apalakṣaṇa hetu utthāḥ idam ca prāyikam viśeṣaṇam samyak hetau api vaktṛ doṣa vaśāt dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa ta upapatteḥ yathā nitya anityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt ghaṭa vat ityādi 
NA_24.2^1	 tatra sādhya vikalaḥ yathā bhrāntam anumānam pramāṇa tvāt pratyakṣa vat pratyakṣasya bhrānta tā vikala tvāt tad bhrānta tve sakala vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt tat ucchede ca pramāṇa prameya abhāvāt na kiñcid kenacid sādhyate iti bhrānta vādinaḥ mūka tāpa nipadyeta sādhana vikalaḥ yathā jāgrat saṃvedanam bhrāntam pramāṇa tvāt svapna saṃvedana vat svapna saṃvedanasya pramāṇa tā vaikalyāt tad pratyanīka jāgrat pratyaya upanipāta bādhita tvāt iti ubhaya vikalaḥ yathā na asti sarvajñaḥ pratyakṣa ādi anupalabdha tvāt ghaṭa vat ghaṭasya sattvāt pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ upalabdha tvāt ca 
NA_24.2^2	 sandigdha sādhya dharmaḥ yathā vīta rāgaḥ ayam maraṇa dharma tvāt rathyā puruṣa vat rathyā puruṣe vīta rāga tvasya sandigdha tvāt viśiṣṭa cetaḥ dharmāṇām viśiṣṭa vyāhāra ādi liṅga gamya tvāt rathyā puruṣe tat nirṇayasya api abhāvāt iti sandigdha sādhana dharmaḥ yathā maraṇa dharma ayam puruṣaḥ rāga ādimattvāt rathyā puruṣa vat rathyā puruṣe rāga ādimattu asyasandigdha tvāt vīta rāgasya api tathā sambhavāt iti sandigdha ubhaya dharmaḥ yathā sarva jñaḥ ayam rāga ādimattvāt rathyā puruṣa vat rathyā puruṣe pradarśita nyāyena ubhayasya api sandigdha tvāt iti 
NA_24.3	 nanu ca paraiḥ anyat api dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa trayam uktam tat yathā ananvayaḥ apradarśita anvayaḥ viparītā anvayaḥ ca iti tatra ananvayaḥ yathā rāga ādimān vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ vaktṛ tvāt iṣṭa puruṣa vat iti yadi api kila iṣṭa puruṣe rāga ādimattvam vaktṛ tvam ca sādhya sādhana dharmau dṛṣṭau tathā api yaḥ yaḥ vaktā sa sa rāga ādimān iti vyāptyasiddheḥ ananvayaḥ ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā pradarśita anvayaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti atra yadi api vāstavaḥ anvayaḥ asti tathā api vādinā vacanena na prakāśitaḥ iti apradarśita anvayaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ viparitā anvayaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti hetum abhidhāya yat anityam tat kṛtakam ghaṭa vat iti viparīta vyāpti darśanāt viparīta anvayaḥ sādharmya prayoge hi sādhanam sādhya ākrāntam upadarśanīyam iha tu viparyāsa darśanāt viparīta tā tat etat bhavadbhiḥ kasmāt na uktam iti 
NA_24.4^1	 atra ucyate pareṣām na su paryālocitam etat dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa traya abhidhānam iti jñāpana artham tathā hi na tāvat ananvayaḥ dṛṣṭānta ābhāsaḥ bhavitum arhati yadi hi dṛṣṭānta balena vyāptiḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ pratipādyeta tatas syāt anavayaḥ dṛṣṭānta ābhāsaḥ sva kārya akaraṇāt yadā tu pūrva pravṛtta sambandha grāhi pramāṇa gocara smaraṇa sampādana artham dṛṣṭānta udāhṛtiḥ iti sthitam tadā ananvayatva lakṣaṇaḥ na dṛṣṭāntasya doṣaḥ kim tarhi hetoḥ eva pratibandhasya adya api pramāṇena apratiṣṭhita tvāt pratibandha abhāve ca anvaya asiddheḥ na ca hetu doṣaḥ api dṛṣṭānte vācyaḥ ati prasaṅgāt iti 
NA_24.4^2	 tathā pradarśita anvaya viparīta anvayau api na dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa tām svīkurutaḥ anvayā pradarśanasya viparyasta anvaya pradarśanasya ca vaktṛ doṣa tvāt tad doṣa dvareṇa api dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa pratipādane tat iyattā viśīryeta vaktṛ doṣāṇām ānantyāt vaktṛ doṣa tve api para artha anumāne tat kauśalam apekṣate iti evam ca upanyāse na bubhutsita artha sādhakau atas dṛṣṭānta ābhāsau etau iti ced evam tarhi karaṇa apāṭava ādayaḥ api dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ vācyāḥ tathā hi karaṇa pāṭava vyatirekeṇa api na para pratyāyanam samasti vispaṣṭa varṇa agrahaṇe vyakta tayā tad artha avagama abhāvāt iti āstām tāvat 
NA_25.0–25.1	 tat evam sādharmyeṇa dṛṣṭānta ābhāsān pratipādya vaidharmyeṇa āha vaidharmyeṇa atra dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ nyāya vidīritāḥ sādhya sādhana yugmānām anivṛtteḥ ca saṃśayāt sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāva vyāptau darśayitum abhipretaḥ yasmin tat vaidharmyam tena atra dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ nyāya vidīritāḥ iti datta artham sādhya sādhana yugmānām gamya gamaka ubhayānām anivṛtteḥ anivartanāt caśabdasya vyavahita prayoga tvāt saṃśayāt ca nivṛtti sandehāt ca iti arthaḥ tat anena ṣaṭ dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ sūcitāḥ tat yathā sādhya avyatirekī sādhana avyatirekī sādhya sādhana avyatirekī tathā sandigdha sādhya vyatirekaḥ sandigdha sādhana vyatirekaḥ sandigdha sādhya sādhana vyatirekaḥ ca iti 
NA_25.2^1	 tatra sādhyāvyatirekī yathā bhrāntam anumānam pramāṇa tvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yat punar bhrāntam na bhavati na tat pramāṇam tat yathā svapna jñānam iti svapna jñānāt bhrānta tā nivṛtteḥ sādhya avyatireki tvam iti sādhana avyatirekī yathā nirvikalpakam pratyakṣam pramāṇa tvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yat punar sa vikalpakam na tat pramāṇam tat yathā anumānam anumānāt pramāṇa tā nivṛtteḥ sādhana avyatireki tvam iti ubhayā vi atirekī yathā nitya anityaḥ śabdaḥ sattvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yaḥ punar na nitya anityaḥ sa na san tat yathā ghaṭaḥ ghaṭāt ubhayasya api avyāvṛtteḥ ubhaya avyatireki tvam iti 
NA_25.2^2	 tathā sandigdha sādhya vyatirekaḥ yathā sarva jñāḥ anāptā vā kapila ādayaḥ ārya satya catuṣṭaya apratipādaka tvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yaḥ punar sarvajña āptaḥ vā asau ārya satya catuṣṭayam pratyapīpadat tat yathā śauddhodaniḥ iti ayam ca sādhyāvyatirekī vāri asatya catuṣṭayasya duḥkha samudaya mārga nirodha lakṣaṇasya pramāṇa bādhita tvena tad bhāṣakasya asarvajña tānāpta tā upapatteḥ kevalam tad nirākāraka pramāṇa sāmarthya paryālocana vikalānām sandigdha sādhya vyatireka tayā pratibhāti iti tathā upanyastaḥ 
NA_25.2^3	 tathā hi yadi api ārya satya catuṣṭayam śauddhodaniḥ pratipāditavān tathā api sarvajña tā āptate tasya na siddhi atas tābhyām sahārya satya catuṣṭaya pratipādanasya anyathā anupapatti asiddheḥ asarva jñāna āptena api para pratāraṇa abhiprāya pravṛtta nipuṇa buddhi śaṭha puruṣeṇa tathāvidha pratipādanasya kartum śakya tvāt tasmāt śauddhodaneḥ sakāśāt asarvajña tān āpta tā lakṣaṇasya sādhyasya vyāvṛttiḥ sandigdhā iti sandigdha sādhya vyatireki tvam iti sandigdha sādhana vyatirekaḥ yathā anādeya vākyaḥ kaścid vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ rāga ādimattvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yaḥ punar ādeya vākyaḥ na sa rāga ādimān tat yathā sugataḥ iti 
NA_25.2^4	 yadi api tad darśana anurakta antaḥkaraṇāṇām sugatasya ādeya vacana tā siddhi saudham adhya ārūḍhāḥ tathā api rāga ādi mattva abhāvaḥ tad pratipādaka pramāṇa vaidhuryāt sandeha gocara cāritām anubhavati atas sugatāt rāga ādi mattā vyāvṛtti saṃśayāt sandigdha sādhana vyatireki tvam iti sandigdha sādhya sādhana vyatirekaḥ yathā na vīta rāgāḥ kapila ādayaḥ karuṇā āspadeṣu api akaruṇā parīta citta tayā ādatta nijaka māṃsa śakala tvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ ye punar vīta rāgāḥ te karuṇā āspadeṣu karuṇā parīta citta tayā datta nija māṃsa śakalāḥ tat yathā bodhisattvāḥ iti atra sādhya sādhana dharmayoḥ bodhisattvebhyaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ sandigdhā tad pratipādaka pramāṇa vaikalyāt na jñāyate kim te rāga ādimante uta vīta rāgāḥ tathā anukampyeṣu kim sva piśita khaṇḍāni dattavantaḥ na iti vā atas sandigdha sādhya sādhana vyatireki tvam iti 
NA_25.3^1	 paraiḥ apare api dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ trayaḥ avimṛśya bhāṣitayā darśitāḥ tat yathā avyatirekaḥ apradarśita vyatirekaḥ viparīta vyatirekaḥ ca iti te asmābhiḥ ayukta tvāt na darśayitavyāḥ tathā hi avyatirekaḥ taiḥ darśitaḥ yathā vīta rāgaḥ kaścid vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ vaktṛ tvāt iti atra vaidharmya ḍṛṣṭa antaḥ yaḥ punar vīta rāgaḥ na sa vaktā yathā upalakhaṇḍaḥ iti yadi api kila upala khaṇḍāt ubhayam vyāvṛttam tathā api vyāptyā vyatireka asiddheḥ avyatireki tvam iti ayuktaḥ ca ayam vaktum avyatirekitāyāḥ hetu doṣa tvāt yadi hi dṛṣṭānta balena aiva vyatirekaḥ pratipādyeta tadā tathāvidha sāmarthya vikalasya tad ābhāsa tā yujyeta na ca āitat asti prāc pravṛtta sambandha grahaṇa pravaṇa pramāṇa gocara smaraṇa sampādana artham dṛṣṭānta upādānāt 
NA_25.3^2	 na hi ekatra yaḥ yad abhāve na dṛṣṭaḥ sa tad abhāve na bhavati iti pratibandha grāhi pramāṇa vyatirekeṇa sidhyati atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt asiddha pratibandhasya hetoḥ eva ayam doṣaḥ na dṛṣṭāntasya iti tathā apradarśita vyatireka viparīta vyatirekau api vaktum ayuktau tayoḥ vaktṛ doṣa tvāt tathā hi apradarśita vyatirekaḥ taiḥ uktaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ākāśa vat iti atra vidyamānaḥ api vyatirekaḥ vādinā vacanena na udbhāvitaḥ iti duṣṭa tā viparīta vyatirekaḥ punar abhihitaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti atra vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ yat akṛtakam tat nityam bhavati yathā ākāśam iti atra viparyasta vyatireka pradarśanāt viparīta vyatireki tvam vaidharmya prayoge hi sādhya abhāvaḥ sādhana abhāva ākrāntaḥ darśanīyaḥ na ca aievam atra sādhana abhāvasya sādhya abhāva vyāpta tayā abhidhānāt iti 
NA_25.4^1	 vyatireka apradarśanam viparīta vyatireka pradarśanam ca na vastunaḥ doṣaḥ kim tarhi vacana kuśa latā vikalasya abhidhāyakasya kim ca yeṣām bhavatām adaḥ darśanam yat uta sva artha anumāna kāle svayam hetu darśana mātrāt sādhya pratīteḥ para artha anumāna avasare api hetu pratipādanam eva kartavyam viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ iti vacanāt teṣām kṛtaka tvāt itīyatā hetu upanyāsena aiva sisādhayiṣita sādhya siddheḥ samasta dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa varṇanam api pūrva apara vyāhata vacana racanā cāturyam āvirbhāvayati āsātām tāvat etau dṛṣṭāntasya sādhana avayava tvena anabhyupagamāt 
NA_25.4^2	 atha ittham ācakṣīthāḥ anvaya vyatireka aparijñāne pratipādyasya na dṛṣṭāntam antareṇa aitau darśayitum śakyau atas anvaya vyatireka darśana artham dṛṣṭāntaḥ abhidhātavyaḥ tatas ca tad kārya akāriṇām tadā abhāsatā iti ced gale gṛhītasya ayam ullāpaḥ tathā api apradarśita vyatireka viparīta vyatirekau dṛṣṭānta ābhāsau na vāstavau kim tarhi vaktṛ doṣa samutthau atas na abhidhātum yuktau tathāvidhasya vidyamāna vastu prakāśana sāmarthya rahitasya nibiḍa jaḍima avaṣṭabdhasya puṃsaḥ vāda an adhikāri tvān mātṛkā pāṭha śālā yogya tayā viduṣām vādayitum ayukta tvāt iti 
NA_26.0	 tat evam para artha anumānam vyācakṣāṇena yat uktam yat uta tat pakṣa ādi vacana ātmakam iti tat pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭāntānām sa ābhāsānām pratipādanāt prāyas paryantitam kevalam tat para ukta dūṣaṇa uddhārāt eva samīcīnatām ābibharti iti amunā prastāvena dūṣaṇam sa ābhāsam abhidhātu kāmaḥ āha vādī ukte sādhane prokta doṣāṇām udbhāvanam dūṣaṇam niravadye tu dūṣaṇa ābhāsa nāmakam 
NA_26.1	 vadana śīlaḥ vādī pratyāyakaḥ tena uktaḥ upanyaste kasmin sādhane sādhyate pratipādya pratītau āropyate anumeyam yena tat sādhanam tat ca aneka rūpam prāk pratyapādi tat yathā kvacid dhetuḥ eva aikaḥ kvacid pakṣa hetū kvacid pakṣa hetu dṛṣṭāntāḥ kvacid te eva sa upanayāḥ kvacid sa nigamanāḥ kvacid ekāika ta= śuddhi vṛddhyā iti pratipādyasya kvacid kathañcid pratyāyayitum śakya tvāt tad pratyāyana upāyasya ca sādhana tvāt iti tatra iha samyak sādhanasya dūṣayitum aśakya tvāt sādhana ābhāsaḥ eva tad sāmarthya upapatteḥ sādhana ābhāsam eva dūṣana upanipātāt prāk avasthāyām anirjñātam sāmānyena sādhana dhvaninā uktam tatra prokta doṣāṇām pratyakṣa ādi nirākṛta pakṣa asiddha ādi hetu sādhya ādi vikala dṛṣṭānta ādi upanyāsa lakṣaṇānām udbhāvanam prāśnikānām puratas prakāśanam yat tat dūṣyate sva abhipreta sādhya pratyāyana vaikalya lakṣaṇām vikṛtim nīyate sādhanam anena iti dūṣaṇam iti jñeyam 
NA_26.2	 adhunā tad ābhāsam āha nirgatam samyak prayukta tvāt avadyam pāpam pakṣa ādi doṣa lakṣaṇam dauṣṭyam asmāt iti niravadyam tasmin sādhane vādinā uktaḥ iti vartate tathā api mad saritayā pramṛdya udaram yat avidyamānānām doṣāṇām udbhāvanam tat dūṣaṇa sthāna upanyasta tvāt tad kārya akaraṇāt samyak sādhane doṣa udbhāvanasya pralāpāyamāna tvāt dūṣaṇa vat ābhāsate iti dūṣaṇa ābhāsam iti tat eva nāma saṃjñā yasya tat tathā samartha sādhana upanyāsa tvāt sādhite sādhye satām api apaśabda alaṅkāra ādi doṣāṇām yat udbhāvanam tat api dūṣaṇa ābhāsa nāmakam iti tuśabdena viśeṣaṇa arthena darśayati vastu siddhi artham vāda pravṛtteḥ tasya siddha tvāt apaśabda ādīnām aprastuta tayā tad dvareṇa doṣa prakāśa nasya asambaddha pralāpa rūpa tvāt itarathā tāvat mātreṇa aiva para apāka raṇa siddheḥ samartha sādhana anveṣaṇa prayatnaḥ viśīryeta prayojana abhāvāt iti 
NA_27.0	 tat evam vyāvahārika pramāṇasya pratyakṣa parokṣa sva artha parārha ādi bheda bhinnasya lakṣaṇam pratipādya adhunā yaiḥ pāramārthikam samasta āvaraṇa viccheda labhyam aśeṣa artha gocaram kevala jñānam na abhyupagamyate tad mata uddalana artham tad lakṣaṇam abhidhitsuḥ āha sakala āvaraṇa muktā ātma kevalam yat prakāśate pratyakṣam sakala artha ātma satata pratibhāsanam 
NA_27.1^1	 sakalam samastam āvṛṇoti āvriyate vānena iti āvaraṇam tad svarūpa pracchādanam karma iti arthaḥ sakalam ca tat avāraṇam ca sakala āvaraṇam tena muktaḥ rahitaḥ ātmā svarūpam yasya tat tathā atas eva kevalam asahāyam āvaraṇa kṣaya upaśama vicitra tayā aiva bodhasya nānā ākāra tayā pravṛtteḥ sāmastyena punar āvaraṇa nirdalane vibandhaka kāraṇa vaikalyāt eka ākāra tayā aiva tasya vivartanāt atas jñāna antara nirapekṣam yat prakāśate prathate nirupādhikam dyotate iti arthaḥ tat paramārthataḥ pratyakṣam 
NA_27.1^2	 tat idam sakala āvaraṇa muktā ātmā iti hetu dvāreṇa tathā kevalam yat prakāśate iti svarūpataḥ nirūpya adhunā kārya dvāreṇa nirūpayan āha sakala artha ātmanām samasta vastu svarūpāṇām satata pratibhāsanam anavarata prakāśanam sakala artha ātma satata pratibhāsanam iti pratibhāsyate anena iti pratibhāsanam ātmanaḥ dharma rūpa tayā bheda vat vivakṣitam jñānam iti yāvat asya ca pāramārthika tvam nirupacarita śabda artha upapatteḥ tathā hi akṣa śabdaḥ jīva paryāyaḥ tatas ca akṣam prati vartate iti pratyakṣam yatra ātmanaḥ sākṣāt vyāpāraḥ vyāvahārikam punar indriya vyavahita ātma vyāpāra sampādya tvāt paramārthataḥ parokṣam eva dhūmāt agni jñāna vat tirodhāna aviśeṣāt 
NA_27.2	 nanu ca prasiddham lakṣyam anūdya aprasiddham lakṣaṇam vidhīyate sarvatra ayam nyāyaḥ aprasiddhe punar lakṣye lakṣaṇam abhidhīyamānam ambara aravindinī kusuma lakṣaṇa vat nirgocaratām yāyāt tat idam svarūpataḥ aprasādhya lakṣaṇam abhidadhānasya kaḥ abhiprāyaḥ iti atra ucyate ye ye mithyā avalepa ādhmāta antaḥkaraṇāḥ pramāṇa prasiddham api adaḥ prati vipratipadyante teṣām dhyāndhīkṛta buddhi tvāt avadhāraṇīyatām anena darśayati kim asya pratipādakam pramāṇam iti ced ete brūmaḥ 
NA_27.3^1	 samasti samasta vastu vistāra gocaram viśada darśanam tad gocara anumāna pravṛtteḥ iha yat yat gocaram anumānam pravartate tasya tasya grāhakam kiñcid pratyakṣam udaya padavīm samāsādayati yathā citrabhānoḥ pravartate ca sakala artha viṣayam anumānam atas tad avalokinā viśada darśanena api bhāvyam iti sarva artha viṣayam kim anumānam pravartate iti ced idam api brūma iha yat yat asti tat tat sarvam sthiti udayā apavarga saṃsargam anubhavati vastu tvāt yat yat vastu tat tat sthema janma pralayaiḥ kroḍīkṛtam tat yathā aṅguliḥ aṅguli tva vakra tvaṛjutvā apekṣayā iti vastu ca yat asti atas prastuta traya ākrāntam tat avagantavyam 
NA_27.3^2	 idam eva nikhila artha gocaram anekānta anumānam jñāna kriyā bhyāsa atiśayān nikhila āvaraṇa vicchede vibandhaka kāraṇa abhāvāt viśada darśanībhavati na ca anumāna pravṛttau api anarthi tva ādinā pramātuḥ apravṛttau anumeya gocara pratyakṣā sambhavena vyabhicāraḥ codanīyaḥ sambhavasya sādhya tayā abhipreta tvāt na ca sambhava mātre asti vyabhicāraḥ sarva anumeyānām sambhavat pratyakṣa tayā vyāpta tvāt iti 
NA_27.4^1	 athavā anyathā anumānayāmaḥ sambhavat samasta śuddhikaḥ ātmā vidyamāna śuddhi upāya tvāt iha yaḥ yaḥ vidyamāna śuddhi upāyaḥ sa sa sambhavat samasta śuddhikaḥ yathā vidyamāna kṣāra mṛd puṭa pāka ādi śuddhi upāyaḥ ratna viśeṣaḥ tathā ca vidyamāna jñāna ādi abhyāsa śuddhi upāyaḥ ātmātaḥ sambhavat samasta śuddhikaḥ iti sāmastya śuddhaḥ ca ātmā jñāna jñāninoḥ kathañcid abhedāt kevalam abhidhīyate iti jñāna ādi abhyāsaḥ katham viśuddhi kāraṇam iti ced āvaraṇa mala pratipakṣa rūpa tvāt iti brūmaḥ pratipakṣa rūpa tā katham avadhāritā iiti ced tava aiva darśanāt tathā hi dṛśyate jñāna ādi abhyāsataḥ pratikṣaṇam āvaraṇa vilayaḥ viśiṣṭa viśiṣṭatara tad kārya bodha ādi anubhavāt tat atiśaye punar sāmastya ucchedaḥ syāt iti abhidadhmahe etena yat pare procuḥ yathā pratyakṣa ādi pramāṇa pañcaka gocara atikrānta tvāt sarva artha saṃvedanam abhāva ākhya ṣaṣṭha pramāṇa gocara tām pratipadyate tat ayuktam tad sambhavasya anumānena pratipādanāt pramāṇa pañcaka pravartana abhāva asiddheḥ 
NA_27.4^2	 kim ca pramāṇa pañcakam tat gocaram na pravartate iti katham bhavataḥ nirṇayaḥ kim niyata deśa kāla vyāptyā yat vā samasta deśa kāla askandanena iti yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tatas yathā ghaṭa ādeḥ kvacid pramāṇa pañcakam tat gocaram nirvartamānam abhāvam sādhayati evam samasta vastu saṃvedana gocaram api tat nivartamānam niyata deśa daśā avacchinnam abhāvam sādhayet na sarvatra tatas ca ghaṭa ādi vat tat durnivāram syāt atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ asau asambhavi eva samasta deśa kāla varti puruṣa pariṣad saṃvedana sākṣāt kāriṇaḥ hi evam vaktum yuktam yat uta na kvacid samasta artha saṃvedanam asti iti na bhavataḥ tathāvidha puruṣa sambhava anabhyupagamāt itarathāḥ yaḥ eva kaścid niścitya aivam abhidadhyāt saḥ eva samasta vastu vistāra vyāpi jñāna ālokaḥ iti samasta artha gocara saṃvedana siddhiḥ iti āstām tāvat 
NA_28.0–28.1^1	 tat evam pramāṇa viṣaye lakṣaṇa saṃkhyā vipratipattī nirākṛtya adhunā krama prāptām gocara vipratipattim bahu vaktavya tvāt anirākṛtya tāvat phala vipratipattim nirācikīrṣuḥ āha pramāṇasya phalam sākṣāt ajñāna vinivartanam kevalasya sukha upekṣe śeṣasya ādāna hāna dhīḥ dvividham hi pramāṇasya phalam sākṣāt asākṣāt ca anantaram vyavahitam ca iti arthaḥ tatra sākṣāt ajñānam anadhyavasāyaḥ prameya aparicchittiḥ tasya vinivartanam viśeṣeṇa pralaya āpādanam pramāṇasya phalam ajñāna uddalana dvāreṇa tasya pravṛtteḥ tasya ca sarva anartha mūla tayā pramātṛ apakāri tvāt tad nivartanasya prayojana tā yukta aiva 
NA_28.0–28.1^2	 etat ca anantara prayojanam sarva jñānānām eka rūpa tvāt sāmānyena uktam vyavahita prayojanam punar vibhāgena āha kevalasya sarvajña jñānasya sukham vaiṣayika sukha atīta parama āhlāda anubhava upekṣā sākṣāt samasta artha anubhave api hāna upādāna icchā bhāvāt madhyastha vṛtti tā te sukha upekṣe phalam iti arthaḥ śeṣasya tad vyatirikta prākṛta loka pramāṇasya ādānam grahaṇam hānam parityāgaḥ tayoḥ ādāna hānayoḥ dhīḥ buddhiḥ ādāna hāna dhīḥ sā phalam iti yāvat tatas ca ādeyānām samyak darśana ādi sraj candana ādīnām yāditsā tathā heyānām mithyā darśana ādi viṣa kaṇṭaka ādīnām yā jihāsā sā pramāṇa sādhya apramāṇāt tad asiddheḥ prekṣā pūrva kāriṇām tatas pravṛtti ayogāt iti uktam bhavati 
NA_29.0–29.1^1	 adhunā gocara vipratipattim nirācaṣṭe anekānta ātmakam vastu gocaraḥ sarva saṃvidām eka deśa viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ nayasya viṣayaḥ mataḥ aneke bahavaḥ antāḥ aṃśāḥ dharmāḥ vā ātmānaḥ svarūpāṇi yasya tat anekānta ātmakam kim tat vastu bahis antar ca gocaraḥ viṣayaḥ sarva saṃvidām samasta saṃvittīnām anena anekāntam antareṇa saṃvedana prasara vyavacchedam darśayati bhrānta saṃvedanānām api anekānta uddyotana paṭiṣṭha tayā pravṛtteḥ kevalam keṣucid aṃśeṣu visaṃvādaka tvāt apramāṇāni tāni saṅgīryante 
NA_29.1^2	 tat ayam abhiprāyaḥ yadā saṃvedana sāmānyam api anekānta viraheṇa na pravartitum utsahate tadā tad viśeṣa bhūtam pramāṇam ekānte pravartiṣyate iti dūra apāḥ tāvaka aśāi va āiṣāḥ vārtā tathā api anādi mithyā abhiniveśa vāsita antaḥkaraṇāḥ kudarśana vipralabdha buddhayaḥ bahavaḥ atra vipratipadyante iti sarva pramāṇānām anekānta gocara tva sādhakam pramāṇam abhidhīyate iha yat pramāṇam tat paraspara avinirluṭhita aneka dharma parikarita vastunaḥ grāhakam tasya aiva tatra pratibhāsamāna tvāt iha yat yatra pratibhāti tat eva tad gocara tayā abhyupagantavyam tat yathā nirādīn avanayana prabhava darśane pratibhāsamānam pāṭala tayā japā kusumam tathā aiva tad gocara tayā abhyupagamyate paraspara avibhakta aneka svabhāva ākrānta mūrtikam ca bahis antar ca vastu sarva pramāṇeṣu prathate iti atas tat eva teṣām gocaraḥ 
NA_29.2^1	 na ca itaretara viśakalita dharmi dharma bhāva vādibhiḥ kaṇa bhakṣa akṣa pāda śiṣyakaiḥ tāvat asya hetoḥ asiddha tā ādi doṣaḥ pratipādayitum śakyaḥ tad abhyupagamam antareṇa sva abhipreta vastunaḥ avasthāna abhāvāt tathā hi ekasmin dharmiṇi bahavaḥ dharmāḥ tatas bhinna tanavaḥ katham varteran bheda aviśeṣeṇa sarvatra tad vṛtti prasaṅgāt tatra aiva teṣām samavāyāt na anyatra vartante iti ced nanu saḥ api samavāyaḥ yadi upakārya upakāraka bhāva vyatirekeṇa api bhavati tatas sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa prasajyeta tad abhāva aviśeṣāt asti eva upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ iti ced hanta hataḥ asi aneka upakārakasya aneka svabhāvatā prāpteḥ tad virahe aneka upakāraka tva abhāvāt 
NA_29.2^2	 na hi yena svabhāvenāikasya upakaroti tena aiva dvitīyasya tasya tatra aiva upayukta tvāt dvitīya upakāraka svabhāvasya tad upamardana dvāreṇa utpatteḥ itarathāikam eva upakurvan tiṣṭhet tad eka svabhāvāt bhinnābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ upakaroti na bhinnaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ tena na anekāntaḥ iti ced tāḥ tarhi tatra katham vartante iti vācyam samavāyāt iti uttare asau api upakārya upakāraka bhāvam antareṇa katham na sarvatra iti prācīnam ca udyam paścāt lagnam anudhāvati upakārya upakāraka bhāva abhyupagame punar api aneka svabhāvatā pradarśita yukteḥ punar śakti upakāraka bhinna śakti parikalpane tat eva āvartate tat na bhinna dharma parikalpane api anekāntān mokṣaḥ iti varam ādau eva mad saritām vihāya aneka dharma adhyāsitam vastu abhyupagatam kim bheda kalpa nayā sthānaḥ eva ātmanā parikleśitena iti 
NA_29.2^3	 kim ca anekānta abhyupagame sati eṣa guṇaḥ paraspara vibhakteṣu saṃyogi saṃyoga samavāyi samavāya guṇa guṇī avayava avayavi vyakti sāmānya ādiṣu saṃyoga samavāya guṇya vaya vi sāmānya ādīnām saṃyogi sama vāyi guṇa avayava viśeṣa ādiṣu vartana cintāyām yat dūṣaṇa jālam upanipatati tat api parihṛtam bhavati ekānta bhedaḥ eva tad upapatteḥ anekānte tad utthāna abhāvāt tathā hi bhinnāḥ khalu saṃyoga ādayaḥ saṃyogi ādibhyaḥ vikalpayitum pāryante yat uta katham ete eteṣu vartante iti kim eka deśena yat vā sāmastyena yadi eka deśena tat ayuktam teṣām niravayava tva abhyupagamāt sāvayava tve api tebhyaḥ avayavebhyaḥ yadi abhinnāḥ tatas anekānta āpattiḥ ekasya aneka avayava tva prāpteḥ atha bhinnāḥ teṣu api te katham vartante iti vācyam eka deśena sāmastyena vā 
NA_29.2^4	 eka deśa pakṣe tat eva āvartate iti anavasthā atha sāmastyena tat api asādhīyaḥ pratyekam parisamāpta tayā saṃyoga ādi bahutva prasaṅgāt tat abhinnāḥ punar saṃyoga ādayaḥ na vikalpa bhājaḥ bhavanti abheda pakṣe api saṃyoga ādi mātram saṃyogi ādi mātram vā syāt iti ced na tasya api ekāntena anabhyupagamāt kim tarhi anyonya aviśliṣṭa svarūpāḥ vivakṣayā sandarśanīya bhedāḥ sarve eva āite abhyupagamyante tathāvidhānām kuyukti vikalpa utthāpita dūṣaṇa samūha nirākaraṇa kṣama tvāt abādhita pratibhāseṣu sarvatra teṣām tathā aiva pratibhāsanāt anyathā pratibhāsamānānām anyathā parikalpane dṛṣṭa hānyadṛṣṭa parikalpanā t vāreṇa asamañjasa prāpteḥ tathā ca brahmādvaita śūnyavāda ādayaḥ siddhim aśnu vīran viśeṣa abhāvāt iti 
NA_29.3^1	 etena asya hetoḥ kāpilāḥ api asiddha tā ādi doṣam abhidhitsavaḥ maukyam ānītāḥ tathā hi antar ekam saṃvedanam apara apara harṣa viṣāda ādi ananta dharma vivartā ākrānta rūpam bahis ca ghaṭa ādikam artham navapurāṇa ādi vartula pārthiva tva ādi aneka svabhāva avaṣṭabdha śarīram sākṣāt lakṣayantaḥ katham tad viparīta kathane pravarteran prakṛti puruṣa ātmakam dravyam evāikam tāttvikam paryāya bhrānti janakaḥ punar vivartaḥ apāramārthikaḥ iti ced na dvayoḥ api sarva pramāṇeṣu prakāśamānayoḥ abādhitayoḥ sarva vyavahāra nibandhanayoḥ pakṣapātam antareṇa aikasya nihnotum aśakya tvāt tathā sati vivarte eva tāttvikaḥ dravyam punar alīkam iti paryāya pakṣa pātī prasañjayan durniṣedhaḥ syāt iti atha ittham abhidadhīthāḥ dravyam sarvatra avyabhicarita rūpa tvāt satyam paryāyāḥ punar vyabhicāriṇaḥ iti asatyāḥ tat ayuktam 
NA_29.3^2	 yadi nāma dravyam abheda rūpa tvāt sarvatra anuvartate paryāyāḥ tu bheda rūpa tvāt vyavacchidyante tathā api tat satyam itare alīkāḥ iti vaktum na pāryate na hi nīlam pīta rūpa tām na bibharti iti etāvatā tat asatyam atiprasaṅgāt sarvasya para rūpa parihāra avasthāyitayā alīka tva prāpteḥ atha dravyam eva paryāyāḥ tat avyatirikta tvāt tad svarūpa van na santi vā dravya vyatirekiṇaḥ paryāyāḥ niḥsvabhāva tvāt kha puṣpa vat iti pramāṇayasi tathā sati paryāyāḥ eva dravyam tat avyatirikta tvāt tad svarūpa van na asti vā paryāya vyatiriktam dravyam niṣparyāya tvāt ākāśa kusuma vat iti itaraḥ api pramāṇayan kena vāryete tat na pakṣa dvaye api kācid viśeṣa upalabdhiḥ iti yathā aiva ananta sahakrama varti paryāya adhyāsitam vastu sarva pramāṇeṣu prakāśate tathā aiva abhyupagantavyam tathā ca anyasya abhāvāt tat eva tad gocaraḥ iti sthitam 
NA_29.4^1	 tathā sugata mata anusāriṇām api madhye sautra antikaḥ tāvat asya hetoḥ asiddha tām āvirbhāvayitum na utsahate tad abhyupagati vyatirekeṇa nija darśana vyavasthā anupapatteḥ tathā hi bahis tāvat ekam kāraṇam apara apara sāmagrī antar pāti taya aneka kārya kāryā vedyate yathā rūpam sva uttarakṣaṇam sva avagāhi jñāna ādikam ca yugapad janayati yadi cāika kṣaṇa vartinaḥ sāmagrī bhedena bhedam anubhavataḥ eva bhinna deśa nānā kārya kāritā tathā sati nitya pakṣa uditam dūṣaṇam sva mastaka upanipāti syāt tasya api tathā iva bhinna kāla kārya nirvartane api bheda abhāva prasaṅgāt 
NA_29.4^2	 tathā pratibhāsa bhedena kṣaṇa kṣayi rūpā ādi sva lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇa tva abhyupagamaḥ ca aivam nirnibandhanaḥ syāt kauṭasthyam ābibhrataḥ api dravyasya apara apara kāraṇa kalāpa antargata tayā navapurāṇa ādi paryāya rūpa rasa gandha sparśa avabhāsa lakṣaṇa kārya sampādana avirodha prasakteḥ kim ca ayam ekam sva avayava vyāpinam kāla antara saṃcariṣṇum ākāram sākṣāt lakṣayan kṣaṇa kṣayi para māṇu lakṣaṇāni sva lakṣaṇāni ācakṣīta na anyathā yathākūtam tad avabhāsasya svapna antare api anupalakṣaṇāt lakṣitasya ca alakṣita vyatireka nirākaraṇataḥ tādātmyam kathayan sva girā anekānta avabhāsam samarthayate 
NA_29.4^3	 tathā hi alakṣita paramāṇu pārimāṇḍalya pratikṣaṇa vivartam api sva lakṣaṇam sthira sthūra ādi ātmanā darśayati sva rūpam anyathā suṣuptam jagat āsajyeta tad aprakāśane pramāṇa antarasya api atyanta vilakṣaṇa sva lakṣaṇa āvedakasya apravṛtti prasaṅgāt tathā antar saṃvedanam artha svarūpa apekṣayā bahirmukha antarmukha sa vikalpa avikalpa bhrānta abhra anta ādi pratibhāsam ekam abhyupayataḥ katham anekānta avabhāsaḥ asiddhaḥ syāt 
NA_29.4^4	 tathā nānā deśa sthita artha sārtha samarpita ākāra uparaktam ekam ākāra bhede api anyathā yugapad prakāśa māna sita asita ādi artha vyavasthiti anupapatteḥ saṃvedanam anumanyamānaḥ katham bhinna samaya bhāvi harṣa viṣāda ādi aneka vivarta vaśāt tad bhedam ātyantikam abhidadhīta abhinna yogakṣema tvāt yugapad bhāvinām saṃvid antar niviṣṭa ākārāṇām eka tvam na harṣa ādīnām tad viparyayāt iti ced na tad sāmarthya vyavasthāpya artha abheda prasaṅgāt tad eka tayā sita pīta ādiṣu jñānasya bodha rūpeṇa aiva aviśiṣṭa tvāt tat evam bahis antar cāika aneka rūpa tve pramāṇataḥ sthiteḥ sva lakṣaṇasya anyathā sva abhyupeta darśana vyavasthā yogāt na artha vādi anekānta prakāśam pratikṣeptum arhati 
NA_29.5	 tathā urarīkṛta yoga ācāra matam api balāt anekānta prakāśa rajjuḥ āveṣṭayati ekasya api jñānasya aneka vedya vedaka ākāratayā prathana upagateḥ eka yogakṣema tvāt tat aikyam iti ced na yugapad udaya pralayavatām saha vedinām sakala santānānām ekatva prasaṅgāt saṃvṛti darśita tvāt aneka tvasya na tena sva saṃvedana sākṣāt kṛta pārama arthi kāika tva kṣatiḥ iti ced na brahma vādi matā pratiṣedha prasakteḥ yatas anādya vidyā balāt ekam akramam sa cetanam sva saṃvedana sākṣātkṛtam api brahma anekam krama vat cetana acetanam parokṣa aparokṣam lakṣyate bhavat parikalpita grāhya grāhaka ākāra vivikta saṃvedana vat iti tena api na durupapādam astu vā ayam anekānta avabhāsaḥ bhrāntaḥ tathā api saṃvedanasya advayatā na lakṣyate tad lakṣaṇe sakala asumatām adhunā aiva mukta tā avāpteḥ lakṣyate ca tat kathañcid itarathā suṣupta daśā vat sarva vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt iti ekasya api saṃvedanasya lakṣita alakṣita tvena anekānta pratibhāso duḥśakaḥ apahnotum iti jñāna vādī api asya hetoḥ asiddha tā āvirbhāvanam prati tūṣṇīm āsīta 
NA_29.6^1	 śūnya vādinaḥ samasta abhāvāt asiddhaḥ anekānta prakāśaḥ iti ced na tasya api pramāṇa prameya abhāve na sarva abhāva āvedanam samasti anyathā pramāṇakam sarvam sarvatra vidyate iti parasya api vadataḥ na vadana bhaṅgaḥ syāt tad abhyupagame abhyupagama kṣatiḥ tayoḥ ca darśita vat anekānta prakāśaḥ iti na asiddhaḥ hetuḥ maru marīcikā nicaya cumbini saṃvedane jala ullekhe api tad gocara tva abhyupagama abhāvāt anaikāntikaḥ ayam iti mā śaṅkiṣṭhāḥ tasya bhrānta tvāt abhrānta prakāśaḥ hi tad abhyupagati hetuḥ atha ayam api itaretara vi nirluṭhita paramāṇu kṣaṇa kṣayi bodhena bādhyamāna tvāt bhrāntaḥ iti ācakṣīthāḥ tat ayuktam yatas tad bodhaḥ kim upalabdhi mātram yat vā nirṇayaḥ yadi ādyaḥ kalpaḥ tadā anumānam viśīryeta nirgocara tvāt prāthama kalpikena aiva nirvikalpa ka vi vikta darśanena virodha bhīru tayā sarvathā vastu grahaṇa abhyupagamāt pramāṇa kalite ca māna antara vaiyarthyāt anavasthā prāpteḥ 
NA_29.6^2	 atha dvitīyaḥ tathā sati sarvam nirvikalpakam apramāṇa tām aśnuvīta na ca nirṇayaḥ anekānta prakāśam bādhate api tu samarthayate bahis antar ca tathā aiva tad vijṛmbhaṇāt atha sarvathā vastu grahaṇe api nirvikalpakam yatra aṃśe pāścātyam vyavahāra kāri vyavasāyam upajanayati tatra aiva pramāṇa tām āskandati na anyatra iti manyethāḥ tathā sati yad anantaram artha kriyā samartha artha prārthanayā puruṣaḥ pravartate saḥ eva nirṇayaḥ prāmāṇyam svīkuryāt na nirvikalpakam tad janaka tve api sannikarṣa ādi vat iti āsajyeta nirvikalpakam anadhigata artha adhigantṛ tvāt pramāṇam na vyavasitiḥ tad vikalpa tvāt iti ced na anumiteḥ api tadvat aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt na ca viparīta ākāra nirākaraṇa caturatayā anumitiḥ viśeṣavatī nirṇīteḥ api tad apanoda dakṣa tvāt asamāropa viṣaye apravṛtteḥ 
NA_29.6^3	 trirūpa liṅga jatayā viśeṣaḥ anumiteḥ mānatā sādhakaḥ iti ced sākṣāt anubhavāt utpādaḥ tarhi nirṇīteḥ mahā aparādhaḥ iti bhavataḥ bāla tām īkṣāmahe kim ca yathā nirvikalpakam alakṣitam sakala vyāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa pravaṇam api katicid aṃśa viṣayam vikalpam utthāpayati tathā arthaḥ eva indriya āloka ādi sannikṛṣṭa tayā katicid nija aṃśa viṣayam sākṣāt viśadavikalpam janayet iti kim ajāgala stana kalpa nirvikalpaka kalpanayā tāvantaḥ aṃśāḥ bahis arthe virudhyante iti ced pāṭava apāṭava ādayaḥ darśane api ekasmin na virudhyante iti kim rājñām ājñā tasmāt na kṣaṇa kṣayi para māṇu lakṣaṇa sva lakṣaṇa lakṣakam kvacid kadācid darśanam lakṣayanti bhavantaḥ api kevalam sva darśana anurakta antaḥkaraṇa tayā na tad asat tām pratipadyante 
NA_29.6^4	 sva aṃśa vyāpinam kāla antara anuyāyinam ekam bahis antar ca artham bodham ca prakāśayan prathamānaḥ nirṇayaḥ na punar nirmūlakaiḥ kuyukti vikalpaiḥ bādhyate iti na bhrāntaḥ kim ca asya bhrānta tām kathayan sarva pramāṇa prameya vyavasthām unmūlyati tathā hi yat sattva bodha rūpa tva sukha tva ādiṣu pramāṇam tat eva kṣaṇa kṣayi tva svarga prāpaṇa śakti yukta tva ādiṣu apramāṇam tathā yat vastu nīla caturasra ūrdhva tā ādi rūpa tayā prameyam tat eva madhya bhāga kṣaṇa vivartā ādinā aprameyam tathā yat bahis artha apekṣayā sa vikalpakam svapna ādi darśanam vā bhrāntam tat eva svarūpa apekṣayā bhrāntam tathā yat niśīthinī nātha dvaya ādikam dvi tve alīkam tat api dhava latā niyata deśa cārita ādau analīkam iti nirṇayaḥ yadi tu virodhāt bibhyadbhiḥ bhavadbhiḥ ayam apahnūyate kim aparam aikāntikam pramāṇam prameyam corarīkṛtya sva ākūtam pratiṣṭhāpayeyuḥ iti sa kautukam naḥ cetaḥ 
NA_29.7^1	 atha jñāna vādī advaita prakāśam alakṣitam abhyupetya tena bāhu vidhyam dadhānaḥ bodhaḥ bādhyamāna tvāt bhrāntaḥ iti abhidadhyāt tat ayuktam dṛṣṭa hānyadṛṣṭa parikalpanā prasaṅgāt alakṣita nirvikalpa darśanasya ca prāk eva pratikṣipta tvāt atha yuktiḥ bodhasya vaividhyam bādheta tathā hi bhrānta abhra anta saṃvedana vivekasya kartum aśakya tvāt saṃvid mātrasya tu sarvatra avyabhicāri tvāt advayam saṃvedanam vivikta yuktyā prakāśamānam anādi kāla ālīna vāsanā samupajanita saṃvṛti darśita sattākam sita asita ādi vividha pratibhāsam nirākurute atra pratividadhmahe kim ayam aneka ākāraḥ bodhaḥ advaya saṃvedanāt vyatyaraikṣīt vā na vā 
NA_29.7^2	 kim ca atas yadi vyabhaitsīt katham adṛṣṭa tad kārya tve vyatiriktaḥ ayam tat advayam saṃvedanam anumāpayet avyatireka pakṣe punar anekaḥ san eka saṃvedana tādātmyena prathamānaḥ katham advaitam na uddalayet atha saṃvṛti darśita tvāt alīkatayā asya sita asita ādi a ākāra bahirmukha kāluṣyasya bodhena tāttvikena saha bheda abheda vikalpa anupapattiḥ iti brūṣe tathā sati paraḥ bodhasya apāram ārthika tvam avidyā darśita tvāt artha sattāyāḥ punar tattva rūpa tā sarvatra avyabhicārāt iti bruvāṇaḥ durnivāraḥ syāt jaḍasya prakāśa ayogāt saṃvittiḥ satyāḥ na arthaḥ iti ced ekasya aneka tā ava bhāsa abhāvāt anekāntaḥ satyaḥ na advaitam iti pratijānīmahe 
NA_29.7^3	 saṃvṛtya advayasya api nānā pratibhāsaḥ aviruddhaḥ iti ced anādi a vidyā balāt jaḍasya api cetana tayā prakāśaḥ na viruddhaḥ iti parasya api śaṭha uttaram na ati durlabham bhavet kim ca nānā ākāra kaluṣita caitanya sāmānyasya anyathā anupapatti sāmarthyataḥ tasya siddha tvāt advayam saṃvedanam asiddham sādhayet ayam anyathā nirnibandhana tayā sādhanasya apravṛtteḥ tathā ca sthira sthūra ādi upalakṣita artha aṃśa vaśāt viśakalita paramāṇu kṣaṇa kṣayi paryāya tādātmyam sādhayan tam anekānta vādinam na pratikṣeptum arhati yukteḥ ubhayatra api tulya tvāt 
NA_29.7^4	 kim ca yaḥ ayam sita pīta ādi aneka ākāra nirṇayaḥ asau api sva saṃvedana apekṣayā dvaya rūpaḥ iti bhavat abhiprāyaḥ yathā ca anavasthā abhīru tayā sarvam jñānam sva prakāśam abhyupetam tathā sarvaḥ niścayaḥ sva niścāyakaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ anyathā tatra api anavasthā doṣaḥ anuṣajyeta niścayāḥ ca sarvathā svarūpam niścinuyuḥ nāika deśena yatas niścayaiḥ yat na niścīyate rūpam tat teṣām viṣayaḥ katham iti svayam eva sva vadhāya pralapitam tathā ca advayasya kṣaṇa kṣayiṇaḥ svarūpasya taiḥ grahaṇe viparīta āropābhāvāt āditas eva anutthānam saṃsārasya iti yukti riktaḥ eva amukta tā abhimānaḥ syāt na ca aivam bhava bhāvasya pratiprāṇi prasiddha tvāt tat na ayam itaretarā vinirluṭhita dravya paryāya prakāśaḥ bhrāntaḥ tad viparīta artha upasthāpaka pramāṇa antara abhāvāt iti sthitam 
NA_29.8^1	 yadā tu śūnya vādī nirālambanāḥ sarve pratyayāḥ pratyaya tvāt svapna pratyaya vat iti para abhiprāya pravṛtta anumāna balāt bhrānta tām asya kathayet tadā tam prati sa ālambanāḥ sarve pratyayāḥ pratyaya tvāt jāgrat daśa apratyaya vat iti viparīta anumānam upaḍhaukanīyam sa yadi dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya vikala tām udbhāvayet tadā tad dṛṣṭānte api sā darśanīyāḥ yadi punar asau svapna pratyayasya nirālambana tvam bhavadbhiḥ abhipretam iti vilapan āsitum na dadyāt tadā sa vikalpataḥ paryanuyojyaḥ asmad abhyupagamaḥ pramāṇam bhavataḥ apramāṇam vā 
NA_29.8^2	 pramāṇam ced yathā tad balāt dṛṣṭānta samarthanam tathā jāgrat pratyaya gocara artha samarthanam api kim na kuruṣe kaḥ ayam ardha jaratīya nyāyaḥ atha apramāṇam evam sati svapna pratyaya nirālamba natā sādhakam pramāṇa antaram mṛgaṇīyam kim anena kuśa kāśa avalambanena tatra api pramāṇa antare vikalpa yugalam amalam avatarati tat kim nirālambanam sa ālambanam vā nirālambanam ced na anya pratyayasya nirālambanatām gaditum paṭiṣṭham nirgocara tvāt atha sa ālambanam hanta hataḥ asi nirālambanāḥ sarve pratyayāḥ iti pratijñāta kṣateḥ anena aiva vyabhicārāt iti śaṭhaḥ pratiśaṭha ācaraṇena nirloṭhanīyaḥ tat na asya anaikāntika tvam 
NA_29.9	 viruddha tā śaṅkā punar dūra apāsta prasara aiva pramāṇa prakāśite arthe sarva vādinām tathā abhyupagama avigānāt iti anena saṃśaya virodha anavasthā vaiyadhi karaṇyā sambhava ādi dūṣaṇāni nirmūlaka mithyā vikalpa utthāpitāni pratibhāsa mudgara nipāta nirdalita mastaka tvāt na jīvitum utsahante iti tasmāt asiddha tā ādi doṣa vinākṛtaḥ ayam tathā apratibhāsa lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ anekānta gocara tām pramāṇasya parān abhyupagamayati iti alam vistareṇa tasmāt tasya aiva tatra pratibhāsanāt sarva saṃvidām anekānta ātmakam vastu gocaraḥ iti sthitam 
NA_29.10	 ayam ca yathā avasthita pramāṇa vyāpāra paryālocaka pramātṛ abhiprāyeṇa pramāṇa gocaraḥ darśitaḥ nayaḥ tarhi kiṃbhūtam tam manyate iti vacana avakāśe sati āha eka ityādi ananta dharma adhyāsitam vastu sva abhipretāika dharma viśiṣṭam nayati prāpayati saṃvedanam ārohayati iti nayaḥ pramāṇa pravṛtteḥ uttara kāla bhāvī parāmarśaḥ iti arthaḥ tasya viṣayaḥ gocaraḥ mataḥ abhipretaḥ eka deśena anitya tva ādi dharma lakṣaṇena viśiṣṭaḥ para rūpebhyaḥ vibhinnaḥ arthaḥ prameya rūpam pramāṇam evaṃvidham eva artham gṛhṇāti iti svākutena tena vyavasthāpanāt iti 
NA_29.11	 athavā pramāṇa viṣayām lakṣaṇa saṃkhyā gocara phala rūpām caturvidhām vipratipattim nirākṛtya atra aiva naya gocaram nirūpayan āha eka ityādi nanu ca ādi vākyena pramāṇa vyutpādana mātram pratijñānam tat kim ayam aprastutaḥ atra naya gocaraḥ pratipādyate iti satyam evam manyate na nayaḥ pramāṇāt atyantam dūra yāyī kim tarhi tad aṃśa bhūtaḥ eva naya samudāya sampādya tvāt pramāṇasya atas tad vyutpādana pratijñāne asau api tad madhya patitaḥ tad grahaṇena gṛhyate iti nyāyāt gṛhītaḥ eva tat na ayam aprastutaḥ iti 
NA_29.12^1	 atra api padārthaḥ saḥ eva kevalam vākya artha bhedaḥ tathā hi iha aivam ghaṭanā nayasya viṣayaḥ eka deśa viśiṣṭaḥ arthaḥ mataḥ nīti vidām iti nanu ca yadi nayasya pramāṇa antar pāti tve api pṛthak gocaraḥ pratipādyate tatas pramāṇa vat etat viṣayā lakṣaṇa ādi vipratipattiḥ api nirākartavyā satyam kim tu na pareṣām naya vyavahāraḥ prasiddhaḥ atas dharmiṇaḥ abhāvāt tad gocarā vipratipattiḥ na asti eva na ca te tena tattvam pratipādanīyāḥ tattva pratipādane pramāṇasya aiva vyāpārān nayasya punar eka deśa niṣṭhatvena tad pratipādana sāmarthya vikala tvāt atas eva ācāryasya na tad lakṣaṇa ādi svarūpa kathane api mahān ādaraḥ 
NA_29.12^2	 gocaram punar heya pakṣe kā akvā prakṣipan sākṣāt pratipādayati mā bhūt sva darśana antaḥpātinām manda buddhīnām pramāṇa pratipanne api anekānta ātmake vastuni eka deśa samartha nābhi niveśa lakṣaṇaḥ kadā grahaḥ iti athavā sva darśana antaḥpātinaḥ prati anena aiva gocara kathanena upalakṣaṇa tvāt lakṣaṇa ādīni api lakṣayati tatra pramāṇa pratipanna arthāika deśa parāmarśaḥ nayaḥ iti lakṣaṇam sarva naya viśeṣa anuyāyi tvāt para rūpa vyāvartana kṣama tvāt ca asya saṃkhyayā punar anantāḥ iti ananta dharma tvāt vastunaḥ tad eka dharma paryavasita abhiprāyāṇām ca naya tvāt tathā api cirantana ācāryaiḥ sarva saṅgrāhi sapta abhiprāya parikalpanā t vāreṇa sapta nayāḥ pratipāditāḥ tat yathā naigama saṅgraha vyavahāra ṛju sūtra śabda samabhirūḍha aivambhūtā nayāḥ iti atas asmābhiḥ api te eva varṇyante 
NA_29.13^1	 katham ete sarva abhiprāya saṅgrāhakāḥ iti ced ucyate abhiprāyaḥ tāvat artha dvāreṇa śabda dvāreṇa vā pravarteta gati antara abhāvāt arthaḥ ca sāmānya rūpaḥ viśeṣa rūpaḥ vā śabdaḥ api rūḍhitaḥ vyutpattitaḥ ca vyutpattiḥ api sāmānya nimitta prayuktā tad kāla bhāvi nimitta prayuktā vā syāt tatra ye kecana artha nirūpaṇa pravaṇāḥ pramātṛ abhiprāyāḥ te sarve api ādye naya catuṣṭaye antarbhavanti tatra api ye paraspara viśakalitau sāmānya viśeṣau icchanti tad samudāya rūpaḥ naigamaḥ ye punar kevalam sāmānyam vāñchanti tad samūha sampādyaḥ saṅgrahaḥ 
NA_29.13^2	 ye punar anapekṣita śāstrīya sāmānya viśeṣam loka vyavahāram avatarantam ghaṭa ādikam padārtham abhiprayanti tad nicaya janyaḥ vyavahāraḥ ye tu kṣaṇa kṣayiṇaḥ paramāṇu lakṣaṇāḥ viśeṣāḥ satyāḥ iti manyante tad saṅghāta ghaṭitaḥ ṛju sūtraḥ iti tathā ye rūḍhitaḥ śabdānām pravṛttim vāñchanti tad nivaha sādhyaḥ śabdaḥ iti ye tu vyutpattitaḥ dhvanīnām pravṛttim vāñchanti na anyathā tad vāra janyaḥ samabhirūḍhaḥ iti ye tu vartamāna kāla bhāvi vyutpatti nimittam adhikṛtya śabdāḥ pravartante na anyathā iti manyante tad saṅgha ghaṭitaḥ khalu evambhūtaḥ iti tat evam na kaścid vikalpaḥ asti vastu gocaraḥ yaḥ atra naya saptake na antaryāti iti sarva abhiprāya saṅgrāhakāḥ ete iti sthitam 
NA_29.14^1	 sāmpratam eṣām eva pratyekam matam upavarṇayāmaḥ tatra gamanam gamaḥ paricchedaḥ iti arthaḥ niścitaḥ gamaḥ nigamaḥ vivikta vastu grahaṇam saḥ eva prajñā ādeḥ ākṛti gaṇa tayā svārthikāṇ pratyaya vidhānāt naigamaḥ yadi vā nigamyante niyatam paricchidyante iti nigamāḥ arthāḥ teṣu bhavaḥ yaḥ abhiprāyaḥ niyata pariccheda rūpaḥ sa naigamaḥ iti ayam hi sattā lakṣaṇam mahā sāmānyam avāntara sāmānyāni ca dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva ādīni tathā antyān viśeṣān sa kalāsā dhāraṇa rūpa lakṣaṇān avāntara viśeṣān ca apekṣayā para rūpa vyāvartana kṣamān sāmānyāt atyanta vinirluṭhita svarūpān abhipraiti 
NA_29.14^2	 tathā hi kila saṃvid niṣṭhāḥ padārtha vyavasthitayaḥ na ca sāmānya grāhiṇi vijñāne viśeṣa avabhāsaḥ asti anuvartamānāikā ākāra parāmarśena tad grahaṇāt anyathā sāmānya grāhaka tva ayogāt na api viśeṣa grahaṇa dakṣe saṃvedane sāmānyam cakāsti viśiṣṭa deśa daśā avacchinna padārtha grāhitayā tad pravṛtteḥ anyathā viśeṣa saṃvedana tva ayogāt na ca aitau paraspara vibhinnau api pratibhā samānau sāmānya viśeṣau kathañcid miśrayitum yuktau atiprasaṅgāt vibhinna pratibhāsinām api nikhila artha ātmanām aikya prāpteḥ 
NA_29.14^3	 evam ca pramāṇayati paraspara viśliṣṭau sāmānya viśeṣau pārthakyena upalabdheḥ iha yat yat pārthakyena upalabhyate tat tat paraspara viśliṣṭam dravyam tat yathā devadatta yajñadattau iti pārthakyena ca upalabhyete sāmānya viśeṣau atas paraspara vibhinnau iti na sāmānyāt pṛthak viśeṣa upalambhaḥ iti ced katham tarhi tasya upalambhaḥ iti vācyam sāmānya vyāptasya iti ced na tarhi sa viśeṣa upalambhaḥ sāmānyasya api tena grahaṇāt tatas ca tena bodhena vivikta viśeṣa grahaṇa abhāvāt tad vācakam dhvanim tat sādhyam ca vyavahāram na pravartayet pramātā na ca āitat asti viśeṣa abhidhāna vyavahārayoḥ pravṛtti darśanāt 
NA_29.14^4	 tasmāt viśeṣam abhilaṣatā tatra ca vyavahāram pravartayatā tad grāhakaḥ bodhaḥ viviktaḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ tathā sāmānyam api vivikta ākāra tayā sva grāhiṇi jñāne yadi na prakāśeta tadā tad gocara abhimata saṃvedanena viśeṣasya api ākalanāt sāmānya abhidhāna vyavahārayoḥ pravṛtteḥ ucchedaḥ tathā iva vaktavyaḥ vivikta sāmānya grāhi bodha mūlaka tvāt tayoḥ tad aniṣṭau tayoḥ api abhāva āpatteḥ na ca sāmānyam viśeṣam vā tiraskṛtya kevalasya viśeṣasya sāmānyasya vā abhyupagamaḥ kartum yuktaḥ dvayoḥ api sva grāhi jñāne pratibhāsamāna tayā viśeṣa abhāvāt tasmāt etau dvau api itaretara viśakalitau aṅgīkaraṇa arhau iti naigamaḥ 
NA_29.15^1	 adhunā saṅgraha abhiprāyaḥ varṇyate tatra saṅgṛhṇāti aśeṣa viśeṣa tirodhāna dvāreṇa sāmānya rūpa tayā jagat ādatte iti saṅgrahaḥ ayam hi manyate bhāva lakṣaṇa sāmānyāt vyatiricyamāna mūrtayaḥ vā viśeṣāḥ parikalpyeran avyatiricyamāna mūrtayaḥ vā gati antara abhāvāt tatra yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā niḥsvabhāva tām te svīkuryuḥ bhāva vyatireki tvāt gagana kusuma ādi vat atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ tarhi bhāva mātram āpadyante tathā hi bhāva mātram viśeṣāḥ tat avyatirikta tvāt iha yat yatas avyatiriktam tat tat eva bhavati tat yathā bhāvasya aiva svarūpam avyatirekiṇaḥ ca viśeṣāḥ atas tad rūpāḥ eva nanu ca yadi bhāva mātram eva tattvam tadā tasya sarvatra aviśeṣāt ye ete pratiprāṇi prasiddhāḥ stambha ibha kumbha ambhorūha ādi viśiṣṭa vastu sādhyāḥ vyavahārāḥ te sarve api pralayam āpadyeran atas viśeṣāḥ api vivikta vyavahāra hetavaḥ abhyupagantavyāḥ 
NA_29.15^2	 nāitat asti vyavahārasya anādya vidyā bala pravartita tvāt tena pārāmarthika pramāṇa pratiṣṭhita tattva pratibandha abhāvāt kim ca viśeṣa agrahaḥ viśeṣeṇa tyājyaḥ viśeṣa vyavasthāpaka pramāṇa abhāvāt tathā hi bheda rūpāḥ viśeṣāḥ na ca kiñcid pramāṇam bhedam avagāhate pratyakṣam hi tāvat bhāva sampādita sattākam tam eva sākṣatkartum yuktam na abhāvam tasya sakala śakti viraha rūpa tayā tad utpādane vyāpāra abhāvāt anutpādakasya ca sākṣātkaraṇe sarva sākṣāt karaṇa prasaṅgāt tathā ca viśeṣa abhāvāt sarvaḥ draṣṭā sarva darśī syāt aniṣṭam ca aitat bhavatām tasmāt bhāva grāhakam eva tat eṣṭavyam sa ca bhāvaḥ sarvatra aviśiṣṭaḥ iti tathā iva tena grāhyaḥ tad uttara kāla bhāvī punar vikalpaḥ ghaṭaḥ ayam paṭa ādiḥ na bhavati iti evam ākāraḥ vyavahāram racayan avidyā mūla tvāt na pramāṇam tat na pratyakṣāt viśeṣa avagatiḥ na api anumāna ādeḥ pratyakṣa mūlaka tvāt śeṣa pramāṇa vargasya tasmāt sāmānyam eva parama arthaḥ na viśeṣāḥ iti saṅgrahaḥ 
NA_29.16^1	 sāmpratam vyavahāra matam ucyate tatra vyavaharaṇam vyavahriyate vā anena laukikaiḥ abhiprāyeṇa iti vyavahāraḥ ayam tu manyate yathā loka grāham eva vastu astu kim anayā dṛṣṭa avyavahriyamāna vastu parikalpana kaṣṭa piṣṭikayā yat eva ca loka vyavahāra patham avatarati tasya anugrāhakam pramāṇam upalabhyate na itarasya na hi sāmānyam anādinidhanam ekam saṅgrāha abhimatam pramāṇa bhūmiḥ tathā anubhava abhāvāt sarvasya sarva darśi tva prasaṅgāt ca na api viśeṣāḥ paramāṇu lakṣaṇāḥ kṣaṇa kṣayiṇaḥ pramāṇa gocaraḥ tathā pravṛtteḥ abhāvāt 
NA_29.16^2	 tasmāt idam eva nikhila loka ābādhitam pramāṇa prasiddham kiyat kāla bhāvi sthūra tām ābibhrāṇam udaka āharaṇa ādi artha kriyā nirvartana kṣamam ghaṭa ādikam vastu rūpam pāramārthikam astu pūrva uttara kāla bhāvi tatparyāya paryālocanā punar ajyāyasī tatra pramāṇa prasara abhāvāt pramāṇam antareṇa ca vicārasya kartum aśakya tvāt avastu tvāt ca teṣām kim tad gocara paryālocanena tathā hi pūrva uttara kāla bhāvinaḥ dravya vivartāḥ kṣaṇa kṣayi paramāṇu lakṣaṇāḥ vā viśeṣāḥ na kañcana loka vyavahāram uparacayanti tat na te vastu rūpāḥ loka vyavahāra upayoginām eva vastu tvāt iti vyavahāraḥ 
NA_29.17^1	 sāmpratam ṛju sūtra abhiprāyaḥ kathyate tatra rju praguṇam akuṭilam atītāna gata vakra parityāgāt vartamāna kṣaṇa vivarti vastunaḥ rūpam sūtrayati niṣṭaṅkitam darśayati iti ṛju sūtraḥ tathā hi asya abhiprāyaḥ atītasya vinaṣṭa tvāt anāgatasya alabdha ātma lābha tvāt khara viṣāṇa ādibhyaḥ a viśiṣyamāṇa tayā sakala śakti viraha rūpa tvāt na artha kriyā nirvartana kṣama tvam artha kriyā kṣamam ca vastu tad abhāvāt na tayoḥ vastu tvam iti vartamāna kṣaṇa āliṅgitam ca punar vastu rūpam samasta artha kriyāsu vyāpriyate iti tat eva pāramārthikam tat api ca niraṃśam abhyupagantavyam aṃśa vyāpteḥ yukti rikta tvāt ekasya aneka svabhāva tām antareṇa aneka sva avayava vyāpanā yogāt aneka svabhāvatāiva astu iti ced na virodha vyāghra āghrāta tvāt tathā hi yadi ekaḥ svabhāvaḥ katham anekaḥ anekaḥ ced katham ekaḥ 
NA_29.17^2	 eka anekayoḥ paraspara parihāreṇa avasthānāt tasmāt svarūpa nimagnāḥ paramāṇavaḥ eva paraspara upasarpaṇa dvāreṇa kathañcin nicaya rūpa tām āpannā nikhila kāryeṣu vyāpāra bhājaḥ iti te eva sva lakṣaṇam na sthūra tām dhārayat pāramārthikam iti kim ca pramāṇataḥ artha vyavasthā na ca pramāṇam deśa kāla vyāpti grahaṇe kiñcana pravartate sarva pramāṇānām vartamāna prakāśa rūpa tvāt tathā hi pratyakṣam tāvat rūpa āloka manaskāra cakṣuḥ lakṣaṇa kāraṇa catuṣṭayāt labdha sattākam vartamāna kṣaṇaḥ eva prakāśate atīta vartsyat kṣaṇayoḥ asannihita tvāt tatas ca tat tad kāla sambaddham eva vastunaḥ rūpam sākṣātkartum kṣamate na pūrvam aparam vāsannidhānāt eva yadi punar vinaṣṭam api pūrvakṣaṇa varti rūpam ākalayet tadā vinaṣṭa tva aviśeṣāt niravadhiḥ kṣaṇa paramparā tatra pratīyeta tathā ca sati saṅkalikayā ana ādi janma paramparā grāhi pratyakṣam anuṣajyeta evam anāga takṣaṇa grahaṇe api yojyam aniṣṭam ca aitat tasmāt tat vārtamāni kakṣaṇa grahaṇa dakṣam eva iti abhyupagantavyam 
NA_29.17^3	 nanu ca yadi kṣaṇa bhaṅgura tām artha ātmanām adhyakṣam avalokayati tadā nīlatā iva pratibhā asamānā sā vipratipatti gocaram na yāyāt iti tad viṣayaḥ laukikānām vyavahāraḥ pravarteta na ca āitat asti sthira tā dvāreṇa vyavahāra pravṛtteḥ iti atra pratividhīyate sākṣāt kurvāṇāḥ api kṣaṇa vinaśvara tām sadṛśa apara apara utpatti vipralabdha buddhayaḥ mandāḥ na adhyavasyanti anādi kāla prarūḍha vāsanā prabodha samupajanita mithyā vikalpa sāmarthyāt ca viparyasta sthira tā vyavahāram pravartayanti tat na ayam adhyakṣasya aparādhaḥ api tu pramātḥṇām eva tathā ghana ākāraḥ api pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhā vimithyā vikalpa sandarśitaḥ eva vivikta darśane tad pratibhāsā yogāt kara caraṇa śiraḥ grīvā ādayaḥ hi avayavāḥ paraspara vibhaktāḥ eva tatra pratibhānti na vyāpya ākāraḥ na ca te api sva aṃśa vyāpinaḥ pratibhānti tad avayavānām api itaretara viśakalita rūpāṇām pratibhāsāt tāvat yāvat paramāṇavaḥ eva prathante vyāpi rūpasya vicāra akṣamatvāt iti ukta prāyam 
NA_29.17^4	 na api anumānāt sthira sthūra vastu siddhiḥ pratyakṣa parigṛhītam hi sambandham āsādya anumānam pravarteta yadā ca tat kṣaṇa bhaṅgura vivikta aṃśa grahaṇa cāturyam ābibhrat darśitam tadā anumānam api tad pratibandha mūlakam tat gocaram eva pāramparyeṇa pratiṣṭhāpayati sva pratibhāsinaḥ rūpasya alīka tayā tad pratiṣṭhāpana dvāreṇa aiva tasya prāmāṇyāt nanu ca smaraṇa pratyabhijñāna ādīni sthira sthūra vastu vyatirekeṇa na upapadyante pūrvam adṛṣṭe tad abhāvāt puruṣa ādi avayavinām smaraṇāt pratyabhijñānāt ca nāitat asti teṣām alīka vāsanā prabodha utthāpita tvena prāmāṇya ayogāt kim ca tāni api svayam vartam āna kṣaṇaḥ eva prakāśante viplava vaśāt tu svarūpam eva vāsanā sampādita atīta artha rūpa tayā vyavasyanti ghana ākāram ca tasya asantam adhyāropayanti tat na tebhyaḥ api vyāpi vastu siddhiḥ tasmāt vyāpini rūpe pramāṇān avatārāt paraspara viśliṣṭāḥ paramāṇavaḥ eva paramārthataḥ iti rju sūtraḥ 
NA_29.18^1	 tat idam artha svarūpa nirūpaṇa nipuṇānām nayānām matam upavarṇitam adhunā śabda vicāra caturāṇām upavarṇyate tatra trayāṇām api śabda ādīnām idam sādhāraṇam ākūtam yat uta śabdaḥ eva parama arthaḥ na arthaḥ tasya tat avyatirikta tvāt pārthakyena vastu tva siddheḥ katham avyatirekaḥ iti ced pramāṇāt iti brūmaḥ tathā hi na vyatiriktaḥ arthaḥ śabdāt tad pratītau tasya pratīyamāna tvāt iha yat pratītau yat pratīyate tat tatas avyatiriktam bhavati tat yathā śabde pratīyamāne tasya aiva svarūpam pratīyate ca śabde pratīyamāne arthaḥ atas asau tatas avyatiriktaḥ iti agṛhīta saṅketasya ghaṭa śabda śravaṇe api ghaṭa pratīteḥ abhāvāt vyatiriktaḥ iti ced evam tarhi viṣasya māraṇa ātmaka tvam tat ajñasya na pratibhāti iti tat tatas vyatiriktam āpadyeta na ca āitat asti tad vyatireka aviśeṣeṇa guḍa khaṇḍa vat viṣasya api amāraka tva āpatteḥ sambandhasya ca vyatiriktena saha prāk eva apāsta tvāt tat na abuddha pramātṛ doṣeṇa vastunaḥ anyathātvam anyathā andhaḥ rūpam na īkṣate iti tad abhāvaḥ api pratipattavyaḥ iti 
NA_29.18^2	 ye nirabhidhānāḥ vartante arthāḥ teṣām śabdāt pārthakyena vastu tva siddhiḥ iti ced na nirabhidhāna artha abhāvāt kevalam kecid viśeṣa śabdaiḥ saṅkīrtyante kecid sāmānya dhvanibhiḥ iti etāvān viśeṣaḥ syāt yadi vā sakala artha vācakāḥ viśeṣa dhavanayaḥ na santi iti na asti atra pramāṇam tatas ca sarve arthāḥ vidyamāna sva vācakāḥ artha tvāt ghaṭa arthavat iti pramāṇāt sarveṣām sva vācaka tvena pūrva ukta yukteḥ śabdāt apārthakī a siddhiḥ tasmāt na paramārthataḥ arthaḥ śabda atiriktaḥ asti upacārataḥ punar laukikaiḥ aparyālocita parama arthaiḥ vyavahriyate asau api aupacārikaḥ śabda ātmakaḥ vā arthaḥ pratikṣaṇa bhaṅguraḥ svīkartavyaḥ varṇānām kṣaṇa dhvaṃsitā pratīteḥ ṛju sūtra pratipādita yukti kalāpāt ca 
NA_29.19	 sāmpratam eteṣām eva pratyekam abhiprāyaḥ kathyate tatra śabdaḥ rūḍhitaḥ yāvantaḥ dhvanayaḥ kasmiṃścid arthe pravartante yathā indra śakra purandara ādayaḥ teṣām sarveṣām api ekam artham abhipraiti kila pratīti vaśāt yathā śabda avyatirekaḥ arthasya pratipādyate tathā aiva tasya aika tvam vā aneka tvam vā pratipādanīyam na ca indra śakra purandara ādayaḥ paryāya śabdāḥ vibhinna artha vāci tayā kadācana pratīyante tebhyaḥ sarva dāivāika ākāra parāmarśa utpatteḥ askhalat vṛtti tayā tathā aiva vyavahāra darśanāt tasmāt ekaḥ eva paryāya śabdānām arthaḥ iti śabdaḥ śabdyate āhūyate anena abhiprāyeṇa arthaḥ iti niruktāt eka artha pratipādana abhiprāyeṇa aiva paryāyadhvanīnām prayogāt iti 
NA_29.20^1	 sāmpratam samabhirūḍha matam upavarṇyate tatra sam ekībhāvena abhirohati vyutpatti nimittam āskandati śabda pravṛttau yaḥ abhiprāyaḥ sa samabhirūḍhaḥ ayam hi paryāya śabdānām prativibhaktam eva artham abhimanyate tat yathā indanāt indraḥ parama aiśvaryam indra śabda vācyam paramārthataḥ tadvati arthe punar upacārataḥ pravartate na vā kaścid tadvān sarva śabdānām paraspara vibhakta artha pratipādaka tayā āśraya āśrayi bhāvena pravṛtti asiddheḥ evam śakanāt śakraḥ pūrdāraṇāt purandaraḥ ityādi bhinna artha tvam sarva śabdānām darśayati pramāṇayati ca paryāya śabdāḥ vibhinna arthāḥ prativibhakta vyutpatti nimittaka tvāt iha ye ye prativibhakta vyutpatti nimittakāḥ te te bhinna arthāḥ yathā indra ghaṭa puruṣa śabdāḥ vibhinna arthāḥ vibhinna vyutpatti nimittakāḥ ca paryāya śabdāḥ api atas abhinna arthāḥ iti 
NA_29.20^2	 yat punar avicārita pratīti balāt eka artha abhidhāyaka tvam pratipādyate tat ayuktam atiprasaṅgāt tathā hi yadi yukti riktā pratītiḥ eva śaraṇīkriyate tadā manda manda prakāśe davīyasi deśe sanniviṣṭa śarīrāḥ vibhinnā api nimba kadamba aśvattha kapittha ādayaḥ ekatarva ākāra tām ābibhrāṇāḥ pratīyante iti ekatayā aiva abhyupagantavyāḥ na ca āitat asti vivikta tad svarūpa grāhi pratyanīka pratyaya upanipāta bādhita tvena pūrva pratīteḥ viviktānām eva teṣām abhyupagamāt tat nāika artha vācinaḥ dhvanayaḥ santi rūḍhiḥ punar avicārita tad arthānām iti samabhirūḍhaḥ 
NA_29.21^1	 sāmpratam evambhūta abhiprāyaḥ pratipādyate tatra aivaṃśabdaḥ prakāra vacanaḥ tatas ca aivam yathā vyutpāditaḥ tam prakāram bhūtaḥ prāptaḥ yaḥ śabdaḥ saḥ evambhūtaḥ tad samarthana pradhānaḥ abhiprāyaḥ api evambhūtaḥ tad viṣaya tvāt viṣaya śabdena ca viṣayiṇaḥ abhidhānāt ayam hi yasmin arthe śabdaḥ vyutpādyate sa vyutpatti nimittam arthaḥ yadā aiva vivartate tadā aiva tam śabdam pravartamānam abhipraiti na sāmānyena yathā udaka ādi āharaṇa velāyām yoṣit ādi mastaka ārūḍhaḥ viśiṣṭa ceṣṭāvān eva ghaṭaḥ abhidhīyate na śeṣaḥ ghaṭa śabda vyutpatti nimitta śūnya tvāt paṭa ādi vat iti 
NA_29.21^2	 atītām bhāvinīm vā ceṣṭām adhikṛtya sāmānyena aiva ucyate iti ced na tayoḥ vinaṣṭa anutpanna tayā śaśa viṣāṇa kalpa tvāt tathā api tad dvāreṇa śabda pravartane sarvatra pravartayitavyaḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt kim ca yadi atīta vartsyat ceṣṭā apekṣayā ghaṭa śabdaḥ aceṣṭāvatī api prayujyeta kapāla mṛd piṇḍa ādau api tat pravartanam durnivāram syāt viśeṣa abhāvāt tasmāt yatra kṣaṇe vyutpatti nimittam avikalam asti tasmin eva saḥ arthaḥ tad śabdena vācyaḥ iti evambhūtaḥ 
NA_29.22^1	 tat evam aneka dharma parīta artha grāhikā buddhiḥ pramāṇam tad dvāra āyātaḥ punar eka dharma niṣṭhā artha samarthana pravaṇaḥ parāmarśaḥ śeṣa dharma svīkāra tiraskāra parihāra dvāreṇa vartamānaḥ nayaḥ sa ca dharmāṇām ānantyāt ananta bhedaḥ tathā api sarva saṅgrāhaka abhiprāya parikalpana mukhena aivam sapta bhedaḥ darśitaḥ ayam eva ca sva abhipreta dharma avadhāraṇa ātmaka tayā aśeṣa dharma tiraskāra dvāreṇa pravartamāṇaḥ parāmarśaḥ durnaya saṃjñām aśnute tad bala prabhāvita sattākāḥ hi khalu ete para pravādāḥ tathā hi naigama naya darśana anusāriṇau naiyāyika vaiśeṣikau saṅgraha abhiprāya pravṛttāḥ sarve api advaita vādāḥ sāṃkhya darśanam ca vyavahāra nayā anupāti prāyas cārvāka darśanam 
NA_29.22^2	 ṛju sūtra ākūta pravṛtta buddhayaḥ tāthāgatāḥ śabda ādi naya mata avalambinaḥ vaiyākaraṇa ādayaḥ iti atha ittham abhidadhīthāḥ yathā katham ete avadhāraṇa dvāreṇa svakam artham samarthayantaḥ tad viparītam nirākurvāṇāḥ durnayatām pratipadyante iti atra ucyate evam pravṛttau nirgocara tvān nirgocarasya naya tva ayogāt tathā hi nayati kenacid aṃśena viśiṣṭam artham prāpayati yaḥ abhiprāyaḥ sa nayaḥ sva abhipreta dharmāt śeṣa dharma pratikṣepa dvāreṇa tu pravṛttaḥ na kiñcid nayati eka dharma āliṅgitasya vastunaḥ asambhavāt bahis antar ca aneka dharma parikarita svabhāvasya tasya pratibhāsāt tad apahnava kāriṇām kadabhiprāyāṇām pratibhāsa bādhita tvena alīka tvāt 
NA_29.23^1	 tathā hi yaḥ tāvat naigama nayaḥ paraspara viśliṣṭau sāmānya viśeṣau pratyapīpadat tat ayuktam tayoḥ tathā kadācana pratibhāsā bhāvāt yat ca uktam anuvartamānāikā ākāra parāmarśa grāhyam sāmānyam yatra na tatra viśeṣa pratibhāsaḥ yatra ca viśiṣṭa deśa daśā avacchinna bodha nirgrāhyaḥ viśeṣaḥ na tatra sāmānya avagatiḥ tad vacana mātram eva dhava khadira palāśa ādi samasta viśeṣa apasāraṇe vṛkṣa tva ādi sāmānya pratibhāsā bhāvāt dūrāt viśeṣa agrahaṇe api kevalam tat cakāsti iti ced na tatra api abhyantarībhūta viśeṣa pratibhāsāt tad virahe śaśa viṣāṇa rūpa tvāt evam viśeṣāḥ api na sāmānyāt atyanta vyatirekiṇaḥ pratibhānti tad nimagnānām eva teṣām grahaṇāt itarathā sattātaḥ atiricyamānāḥ bhāvāḥ niḥsvabhāva tām ātmasāt kurvanti tathā vṛkṣa tva ādi sāmānyebhyaḥ api bhedinaḥ vṛkṣa ādayaḥ na syuḥ tad abheda nibandhana tvāt tad svarūpa sthiteḥ 
NA_29.23^2	 tasmāt tat eva saṃvedanam upasarjanīkṛta vaiṣamyam pradhānīkṛtāika ākāram sāmānyam gṛhṇāti iti ucyate nyakkṛta sama tvam utkalita nānā tvam punar viśeṣa grahī iti sama tva nānā tvayoḥ kathañcid bheda abhedinoḥ parasparam sarva artheṣu bhāvāt tad abhāve tathāvidha pratibhāsā anupapatteḥ etena yat avādi na ca aitau vibhinnau api pratibhā samānau sāmānya viśeṣau kathañcid miśrayitum yuktau ityādi tat apāstam avagantavyam vibhinnayoḥ pratibhāsā bhāvāt vyavahāraḥ api sarvaḥ pradhāna upasarjana dvāreṇa kathañcid itaretarā vinirluṭhita sāmānya viśeṣa sādhyaḥ eva na hi sāmānyam doha vāha ādi kriyāyām upayujyate viśeṣāṇām eva tatra upayogān na api viśeṣāḥ eva tad kāriṇaḥ go tva śūnyānām teṣām vṛkṣa ādya viśiṣṭa tayā tad karaṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt 
NA_29.23^3	 kim ca atyanta vyatireke sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ vṛkṣam chindhi iti coditaḥ kim iti tad viśeṣe palāśa ādauchedam vidhatte tatra tasya samavāyāt iti ced na samavāya grāhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt bhāve api viśliṣṭayoḥ abheda buddhi utpādana akṣama tvāt tasya api vyatirikta tayā padārtha antara aviśeṣāt nitya tvāika tva sarva gata tva ādibhiḥ ca sarvatra tad karaṇa prasaṅgāt ca yat punar avādīḥ yat uta yadi sāmānyam viśeṣa niṣṭham viśeṣaḥ vā sāmānya vyāptaḥ samupalabhyeta tatas viviktayoḥ tayoḥ kvacid anupalambhāt yaḥ ayam vivikteṣu sāmānyeṣu viśeṣeṣu ca abhidhāna artha kriyā lakṣaṇaḥ vyavahāraḥ sa samastaḥ pralayam yāyāt lolībhāvena tad vivekasya kartum aśakya tvāt tat api asamīcīnam yatas yadi api paraspara aviviktayoḥ sāmānya viśeṣayoḥ sarvatra upalambhaḥ tathā api yatra aiva pramātuḥ arthi tvam tat eva sāmānyam viśeṣān vā pradhānīkṛtya tad gocaram dhvanim artha kriyām vā pravartayati itarasya api upasarjana bhāvena tatra vyāpārāt tad vikalasya itarasya api śaśa viśāṇāyamāna tayā kvacid anupayogāt 
NA_29.23^4	 kim ca atyanta vyatirekiṇi viśeṣebhyaḥ sāmānye vṛtti vikalpa upalambha nūtana viśeṣa sambandha ādi dvāreṇa dūṣaṇa mudgara kadambakam mūrdhani patat durviṣaham syāt tathā hi tat teṣu katham varteta sāmastyenāika deśena vā sāmastya pakṣe prativiśeṣam parisamāpta tayā sāmānya bahutva prasaṅgaḥ aniṣṭam ca āitat eka tva abhupagama kṣateḥ eka deśena vartane punar yāvantaḥ viśeṣāḥ tāvantaḥ tad aṃśāḥ prasajanti na ca āitat asti sāmānyasya niravayava tvāt sāvayava tve api punar te abhinnāḥ bhinnā vā 
NA_29.23^5	 yadi abhinnāḥ viśeṣāḥ tarhi abhedinaḥ kim na iṣyante viśeṣa abhāvāt bheda pakṣe punar teṣu api tat katham varteta sāmastyenāika deśena vā iti tat eva codyam alabdha pariniṣṭham avatarati tat na atyanta bhedinaḥ vṛttiḥ sambhavati kim ca yadi ekam sāmānyam bheda vat samasta viśeṣeṣu varteta tadāika viśeṣa upalambha kāle tat upalambhyate na vā yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tasya aika tayā sarvatra upalambhāt vyāpya grahaṇa abhāve vyāpaka grahaṇā siddheḥ nikhila tad vyāpya viśeṣa grahaṇam āsajyeta na ca āitat asti puras varti viśeṣasya aiva sākṣātkaraṇāt cheṣa viśeṣāṇām asannidhānāt sannihita viśeṣa niṣṭham eva tat upalabhyate 
NA_29.23^6	 tasya aiva tad vyañjaka tvāt itareṣām tad abhāvāt iti ced nāika svabhāvasya khaṇḍaśas vyañjana ayogāt sannihita viśeṣa vyañjitam eva tat sarvatra svabhāva antara abhāvāt sarva viśeṣa gatam ca tad rūpam atas tad darśanam kena vāryete atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ tathā sati yathāika viśeṣa upalambha samaye na upalabhyate tathā śeṣa viśeṣa upalambha kāle api na upalabhyeta viśeṣa abhāvāt atas tad abhāvaḥ eva uktaḥ syāt kevalasya upalambha abhāvāt upalambhe api sva svabhāva sthiteḥ viśeṣa rūpa tā āpattiḥ tathā cirantana viśeṣa vyavasthita sattākam tat nūtana viśeṣa utpāde sati katham tena saha sambandham anubhavet na tāvat viśeṣa antarebhyaḥ tat utpitsu viśeṣa deśam gantum arhati niṣkriya tvāt na api tatra aiva abhavat viśeṣa utpādāt prāk tad deśe tad upalambha abhāvāt na api viśeṣeṇa aiva saha utpadyate nitya tvāt nityasya ca utpatti virodhāt 
NA_29.23^7	 atha aitad doṣa parijihīrṣayā tat sa kriyākam abhidhīyeta tathā api pūrva vyakti tyāgena vā nūtana viśeṣa deśam ākrāmet tad abhāvena vā na tāvat adyaḥ pakṣaḥ cirantana vyaktīnām sāmānya vikala tayā tad sambandha sādhya buddhi dhvani viraha prasaṅgāt na ca āitat asti apara apara viśeṣa utpāde api prācīnavyaktiṣu tad darśanāt atha dvitīyaḥ kalpaḥ tat api asambaddham niravayavasya pūrva vyakti tyāga vaikalye sati utpitsu vyaktim pratigamana abhāvāt sa avayava pakṣasya punar prāk eva apāsta tvān nāitat abhyupagama dvāreṇa parihāraḥ śreyān anyat ca vyatirikta sāmānya sambandhāt yadi bhāvāḥ samānāḥ na svarūpeṇa tadā sattva sambandhāt prāk bhāvāḥ santaḥ asantaḥ vā santaḥ ced apārthakaḥ sattā sambandhaḥ anyathā anavasthā prasajyeta punar satta antara sambandha anivāraṇāt 
NA_29.23^8	 asantaḥ ced atyanta asatām api gagana aravinda ādīnām sattā sambandhāt bhāva rūpa tā āpadyeta evam dravya tva guṇa tva karma tva gotva ādi sāmānyeṣu api samastam etat vācyam eka yogakṣema tvāt tat na parasparam atyanta vyatirekiṇau sāmānya viśeṣau kathañcana ghaṭām āṭīkete atas eva tad samarthana pravaṇaḥ tad tādātmya pratikṣepakaḥ abhiprāyaḥ nirālambana tvāt naigama durnaya vyapadeśam āskandati tādātmya upekṣayā aiva sāmānya viśeṣa vyatireka samarthakasya naigamanaya tvāt vyatirekiṇoḥ api tayoḥ vastuni kathañcid bhāvāt itarathāḥ vivakṣayā api tathā darśayitum aśakya tvāt pradhāna upasarjana bhāvasya dvaya niṣṭha tvāt atyanta tādātmye tad kāriṇyāḥ vivakṣāyāḥ api nirgoca rata aprasaṅgāt tasmāt kathañcid bheda abhedinau eva aitau tad anyatara samarthakaḥ punar nirālambana tvāt durnayatām svīkaroti iti sthitam
